
说明：
- 词根下面，单词是每行一个单词，然后提供拆解，例句。
- 有些单词的中文解释后面可以用括号（=...）加上简单英文解释或者替换的简单词
- 包括高考范围的单词。

- [ ] 补充初中常见词根。剔除高考外的生僻词汇。
## 词根单词

列举词根下的单词

### 动作词根

> 表示各种动作、行为及其状态变化。

#### 手部操作


★**man/manu=hand 手**: 

- **manu**al /ˈmænjuəl/ = manu (手) + al (形容词后缀，…的) → 手册（=handbook）：Please read the manual before using the machine. (使用机器前请阅读手册。)
- **manu**facture /ˌmænjəˈfækʧər/ = manu (手) + fact (做) + ure (名词后缀) → 用手做 → 制造（=produce）：This company manufactures high-quality furniture. (这家公司制造高品质家具。)
- **manu**facturer /ˌmænjəˈfækʧərər/ = manu (手) + fact (做) + ur(e) + er (人) → 制造的人 → 制造商
- **man**ipulate /məˈnɪpjəˌleɪt/ = mani (手) + pul (拉/推) + ate (动词后缀) → 用手操作 → 操作/操纵（=control）
- **man**ner /ˈmænər/ = man (手) + ner (名词后缀) → 手的动作方式 → 方式/举止
- **man**age /ˈmænɪʤ/ = man (手) + age (动词后缀) → 用手处理 → 管理（=run/control）
- **man**ager /ˈmænɪʤər/ = man (手) + ag(e) + er (人) → 管理的人 → 经理
- **man**agement /ˈmænɪʤmənt/ = man (手) + age (动词后缀) + ment (名词后缀) → 管理的行为 → 管理
- **man**icure /ˈmænɪkjər/ = mani (手) + cure (照顾/护理) → 手部护理 → 修指甲（=nail care）


★**tract=draw/pull 拉**（→ treat 为法语音变形式）: 

- at**tract** /əˈtrækt/ = at (向) + tract (拉) → 拉过来 → 吸引：The colorful lights attract many tourists at night. (彩灯在夜晚吸引了许多游客。)
- at**tract**ion /əˈtrækʃən/ = at (向) + tract (拉) + ion (名词后缀) → 吸引力/景点：The Eiffel Tower is a famous tourist attraction. (埃菲尔铁塔是著名的旅游景点。)
- at**tract**ive /əˈtræktɪv/ = at (向) + tract (拉) + ive (形容词后缀) → 有吸引力的：She has an attractive smile. (她有着迷人的微笑。)
- con**tract** /ˈkɑnˌtrækt/ = con (一起) + tract (拉) → 拉到一起 → 合同（=agreement）/收缩（=shrink）：They signed a contract with the supplier. (他们与供应商签订了合同。)
- **tract**or /ˈtræktər/ = tract (拉) + or (名词后缀，物) → 拉东西的机器 → 拖拉机：The farmer drives a tractor in the field. (农民在田里开着拖拉机。)
- ex**tract** /ˈɛkˌstrækt/ = ex (出) + tract (拉) → 拉出来 → 提取（=pull out）/摘录（=excerpt）：Scientists extract oil from plants. (科学家从植物中提取油。)
- sub**tract** /səbˈtrækt/ = sub (下) + tract (拉) → 向下拉 → 减去：Children learn to add and subtract in school. (孩子们在学校学习加减法。)
- abs**tract** /ˈæbˌstrækt/ = abs (离开) + tract (拉) → 抽离 → 抽象的（=conceptual）/摘要（=summary）：The concept is too abstract for beginners. (这个概念对初学者来说太抽象了。)
- dis**tract** /dɪˈstrækt/ = dis (分开) + tract (拉) → 拉开注意力 → 分心（=divert attention）：Don't let the noise distract you from studying. (不要让噪音分散你学习的注意力。)
- re**treat** /riˈtrit/ = re (回) + treat (拉)（treat ← tract 音变） → 拉回 → 撤退/退避（=withdraw）：The army was forced to retreat. (军队被迫撤退了。)


★**press=press 压**: 

- ex**press** /ɪkˈsprɛs/ = ex (出) + press (压) → 压出来 → 表达：She finds it hard to express her feelings. (她觉得很难表达自己的感受。)
- ex**press**ion /ɪkˈsprɛʃən/ = ex (出) + press (压) + ion (名词后缀) → 表达/表情：His expression showed surprise. (他的表情流露出惊讶。)
- im**press** /ˌɪmˈprɛs/ = im (进) + press (压) → 压进去 → 给……留下印象：Her performance impressed the audience deeply. (她的表演给观众留下了深刻印象。)
- im**press**ion /ˌɪmˈprɛʃən/ = im (进) + press (压) + ion (名词后缀) → 印象：My first impression of the city was very good. (我对这座城市的第一印象非常好。)
- im**press**ive /ˌɪmˈprɛsɪv/ = im (进) + press (压) + ive (形容词后缀) → 令人印象深刻的：The view from the mountain is impressive. (山上的景色令人印象深刻。)
- de**press** /dɪˈprɛs/ = de (向下) + press (压) → 向下压 → 使沮丧（=sadden）/使萧条：Rainy weather always depresses me. (雨天总是让我沮丧。)
- de**press**ion /dɪˈprɛʃən/ = de (向下) + press (压) + ion (名词后缀) → 抑郁（=sadness）/萧条（=slump）：He suffered from depression for many years. (他患有抑郁症很多年。)
- com**press** /ˈkɑmprɛs/ = com (一起) + press (压) → 压到一起 → 压缩（=squeeze）：You need to compress the files before sending. (发送之前你需要压缩文件。)
- **press**ure /ˈprɛʃər/ = press (压) + ure (名词后缀) → 压力：He works well under pressure. (他在压力下工作得很好。)
- op**press** /əˈprɛs/ = op (对着) + press (压) → 对着压 → 压迫（=treat cruelly）：The regime oppressed its citizens. (那个政权压迫其公民。)


★**pos/pon=put/place 放置**: 

- **pos**ition /pəˈzɪʃən/ = pos (放置) + ition (名词后缀) → 放置的地方 → 位置（=place），职位（=job）：She accepted a position as a teacher. (她接受了一个教师的职位。)
- **pos**itive /ˈpɑzətɪv/ = pos (放置) + itive (形容词后缀) → 确定的 → 积极的/正面的：He has a positive attitude towards life. (他对生活有积极的态度。)
- post**pon**e /poʊstˈpoʊn/ = post (后) + pon (放) + e → 往后放 → 推迟（=delay）：The meeting was postponed to next week. (会议被推迟到下周了。)
- com**pos**e /kəmˈpoʊz/ = com (一起) + pos (放) + e → 放在一起 → 组成/作曲：She composes music in her free time. (她空闲时创作音乐。)
- com**pos**ition /ˌkɑmpəˈzɪʃən/ = com (一起) + pos (放) + ition (名词后缀) → 组合 → 作文/作品：The student wrote an excellent composition. (那个学生写了一篇优秀的作文。)
- ex**pos**e /ɪkˈspoʊz/ = ex (出) + pos (放) + e → 放出来 → 暴露（=uncover）/揭露（=reveal）：Don't expose your skin to the sun too long. (不要让皮肤暴露在阳光下太久。)
- ex**pos**ure /ɪkˈspoʊʒər/ = ex (出) + pos (放) + ure (名词后缀) → 暴露/曝光：Long exposure to loud noise can damage hearing. (长时间暴露在噪音中会损害听力。)
- op**pos**e /əˈpoʊz/ = op (对着) + pos (放) + e → 对着放 → 反对：Most people oppose the new policy. (大多数人反对新政策。)
- op**pos**ite /ˈɑpəzɪt/ = op (对着) + pos (放) + ite → 相对放的 → 相反的：The bank is on the opposite side of the street. (银行在街对面。)
- pro**pos**e /prəˈpoʊz/ = pro (前) + pos (放) + e → 放到前面 → 提议（=suggest）/求婚：He proposed a plan to reduce costs. (他提出了一个降低成本的计划。)
- pro**pos**al /prəˈpoʊzəl/ = pro (前) + pos (放) + al (名词后缀) → 提议/提案（=suggestion）：The proposal was accepted by the committee. (该提案被委员会接受了。)
- pur**pos**e /ˈpərpəs/ = pur (前) + pos (放) + e → 放在前面的 → 目的：What is the purpose of this meeting? (这次会议的目的是什么？)
- de**pos**it /dɪˈpɑzət/ = de (下) + pos (放) + it → 放下 → 存放（=put down）/押金（=security money）：You need to pay a deposit to rent the apartment. (你需要付押金来租公寓。)
- dis**pos**e /dɪˈspoʊz/ = dis (分开) + pos (放) + e → 分开放置 → 处理/处置（=get rid of）：Please dispose of the waste properly. (请妥善处理垃圾。)
- **pos**e /poʊz/ = pos (放) + e → 摆放姿势 → 姿势/提出：The model posed for the camera. (模特对着相机摆姿势。)
- sup**pos**e /səˈpoʊz/ = sup (下) + pos (放) + e → 放下想法 → 假设（=guess）/认为：I suppose you are right. (我想你是对的。)


★**form=shape 形状**: 

- re**form** /rɪˈfɔrm/ = re (再) + form (形状) → 重新塑形 → 改革：The government plans to reform the education system. (政府计划改革教育体系。)
- trans**form** /ˈtrænsfɔrm/ = trans (跨越) + form (形状) → 变形 → 转变/改造：Technology has transformed our lives. (科技改变了我们的生活。)
- uni**form** /ˈjunəˌfɔrm/ = uni (一) + form (形状) → 统一的形状 → 制服/一致的：Students must wear a school uniform. (学生必须穿校服。)
- in**form** /ˌɪnˈfɔrm/ = in (入) + form (形状) → 使成形 → 通知（=message）：Please inform me of any changes. (如有变动请通知我。)
- in**form**ation /ˌɪnˌfɔrˈmeɪʃən/ = in (入) + form (形状) + ation (名词后缀) → 信息：You can find more information online. (你可以在网上找到更多信息。)
- con**form** /kənˈfɔrm/ = con (一起) + form (形状) → 同一个形状 → 遵守/符合：All products must conform to safety standards. (所有产品必须符合安全标准。)
- per**form** /pərˈfɔrm/ = per (彻底) + form (形状) → 彻底成形 → 表演/执行：The band will perform live tonight. (乐队今晚将进行现场演出。)
- per**form**ance /pərˈfɔrməns/ = per (彻底) + form (形状) + ance (名词后缀) → 表演/表现/性能：The car has excellent performance. (这辆车性能优异。)
- **form**er /ˈfɔrmər/ = form (形状) + er (比较) → 先成形 → 前者的/前任的：She is a former champion. (她是一位前冠军。)
- **form**al /ˈfɔrməl/ = form (形状) + al (形容词后缀) → 有一定形状的 → 正式的：Please wear formal attire to the dinner. (请穿正装参加晚宴。)
- in**form**al /ˌɪnˈfɔrməl/ = in (不) + form (形状) + al (形容词后缀) → 非正式的：We had an informal chat after work. (我们下班后进行了非正式的聊天。)
- plat**form** /ˈplætˌfɔrm/ = plat (平的) + form (形状) → 平的地方 → 平台/月台：The train departs from platform 3. (火车从3号站台出发。)
- **form**ula /ˈfɔrmjələ/ = form (形状) + ula (小) → 小形式 → 公式/配方：The baby drinks a special milk formula. (这个宝宝喝一种特殊的配方奶粉。)
- **form**at /ˈfɔrˌmæt/ = form (形状) + at → 形式 → 格式（=layout）：Please submit your essay in PDF format. (请以PDF格式提交你的论文。)
- **form**ation /fɔrˈmeɪʃən/ = form (形状) + ation (名词后缀) → 形成/编队：The rock formation is millions of years old. (这个岩石形成已有数百万年了。)


★**lect/leg/lig=choose/gather 选择/收集**: 

- col**lect** /kəˈlɛkt/ = col (一起) + lect (收集) → 收集：Please collect all the papers from the desk. (请把桌子上的所有文件收集起来。)
- col**lect**ion /kəˈlɛkʃən/ = col (一起) + lect (收集) + ion (名词后缀) → 收集/收藏品：She has an impressive collection of vintage stamps. (她收藏了大量珍贵的复古邮票。)
- col**lect**ive /kəˈlɛktɪv/ = col (一起) + lect (收集) + ive (形容词后缀) → 集体的/共同的（=shared）：We made a collective decision to move forward. (我们做出了集体决定来推进。)
- e**lect** /ɪˈlɛkt/ = e (出) + lect (选择) → 选举/推选：The citizens will elect a new mayor next month. (市民们将于下月选举新市长。)
- e**lect**ion /ɪˈlɛkʃən/ = e (出) + lect (选择) + ion (名词后缀) → 选举：The election results will be announced at midnight. (选举结果将于午夜公布。)
- se**lect** /səˈlɛkt/ = se (分开) + lect (选择) → 选择/挑选：You can select any seat you like in the theater. (你可以在剧院里选择任何你喜欢的座位。)
- se**lect**ion /səˈlɛkʃən/ = se (分开) + lect (选择) + ion (名词后缀) → 选择/精选：The restaurant offers a wide selection of desserts. (这家餐厅提供种类繁多的甜点选择。)
- intel**lect** /ˈɪnəˌlɛkt/ = intel (在……之间) + lect (选择/辨别) → 智力/才智：He is a man of remarkable intellect and deep insight. (他是一个智力非凡、洞察力深刻的人。)
- intel**lect**ual /ˌɪnəˈlɛkʧuəl/ = intel (在……之间) + lect (选择) + ual (形容词后缀) → 智力的/知识的：She enjoys intellectual conversations about philosophy. (她喜欢关于哲学的智力对话。)
- neg**lect** /nɪˈglɛkt/ = neg (不) + lect (选择/收集) → 忽视（=ignore）/疏忽（=ignore）：Don't neglect your health while pursuing your career. (追求事业时不要忽视你的健康。)
- recol**lect** /ˌrɛkəˈlɛkt/ = re (再次) + col (一起) + lect (收集) → 回忆/记起：I can't recollect where I left my car keys. (我想不起来把车钥匙放哪儿了。)
- e**leg**ant /ˈɛləgənt/ = e (出) + leg (选择) + ant (形容词后缀) → 优雅的/精致的：She wore an elegant dress to the ceremony. (她穿了一件优雅的连衣裙参加典礼。)
- e**lig**ible /ˈɛlɪʤəbəl/ = e (出) + lig (选择) + ible (可……的) → 合格的/有资格的：Only permanent residents are eligible to vote. (只有永久居民才有资格投票。)
- de**leg**ate /ˈdɛləˌgeɪt/ = de (离开) + leg (选择) + ate (动词/名词后缀) → 委派/代表：The manager delegated the task to his assistant. (经理把任务委派给了助手。)
- **leg**end /ˈlɛʤənd/ = leg (阅读/收集) + end (名词后缀) → 传奇/传说：The story of King Arthur is a famous legend. (亚瑟王的故事是一个著名的传奇。)


★**scrib/script=write 写**: 

- de**scrib**e /dɪˈskraɪb/ = de (向下/完全) + scrib (写) → 描述/形容：Can you describe the suspect to the police officer? (你能向警察描述一下嫌疑犯的样子吗？)
- de**script**ion /dɪˈskrɪpʃən/ = de (向下) + script (写) + ion (名词后缀) → 描述/说明：The job description includes a detailed list of responsibilities. (职位描述包含了一份详细的职责清单。)
- pre**script**ion /prəˈskrɪpʃən/ = pre (之前) + script (写) + ion (名词后缀) → 处方/药方：The doctor wrote a prescription for antibiotics. (医生开了一张抗生素处方。)
- manu**script** /ˈmænjəˌskrɪpt/ = manu (手) + script (写) → 手稿/原稿：The ancient manuscript was discovered in a hidden cave. (这份古代手稿是在一个隐秘的洞穴里发现的。)
- sub**scrib**e /səbˈskraɪb/ = sub (在……之下) + scrib (写) → 订阅/签署：I subscribe to several online news platforms. (我订阅了几个在线新闻平台。)
- in**scrib**e /ˌɪnˈskraɪb/ = in (在……上) + scrib (写) → 题写/刻写：The artist inscribed his signature on the sculpture. (艺术家在雕塑上题写了签名。)
- **script** /skrɪpt/ = script (写) → 剧本/手迹：The actor memorized the entire script in one week. (那位演员仅用一周就背下了整个剧本。)


★**graph/gram=write/draw 写/画**: 

- photo**graph** /ˈfoʊtəˌgræf/ = photo (光) + graph (写/画) → 用光画 → 照片：This photograph was taken at sunrise on the mountain peak. (这张照片是在山顶日出时拍的。)
- photo**graph**y /fəˈtɑgrəfi/ = photo (光) + graph (写/画) + y (名词后缀) → 摄影：He developed a passion for wildlife photography during his travels. (他在旅行中培养了对野生动物摄影的热情。)
- auto**graph** /ˈɔtəˌgræf/ = auto (自己) + graph (写) → 亲笔签名：Fans waited in line for the singer's autograph. (粉丝们排队等候歌手的亲笔签名。)
- tele**gram** /ˈtɛləˌgræm/ = tele (远) + gram (写) → 从远方写来的 → 电报：They sent a telegram to inform the family of the good news. (他们发了一封电报通知家人好消息。)
- **gram**mar /ˈgræmər/ = gram (写/字母) + mar (名词后缀) → 语法/文法：Good grammar is essential for clear communication. (良好的语法对于清晰沟通至关重要。)
- dia**gram** /ˈdaɪəˌgræm/ = dia (穿过) + gram (写/画) → 图表/示意图：The teacher drew a diagram to explain the water cycle. (老师画了一个图表来解释水循环。)
- para**graph** /ˈpɛrəˌgræf/ = para (旁边) + graph (写) → 段落：Each paragraph should focus on one main idea. (每个段落应该聚焦于一个主要观点。)
- bio**graph**y /baɪˈɑgrəfi/ = bio (生命) + graph (写) + y (名词后缀) → 传记（=life story）：She is reading an inspiring biography of Marie Curie. (她正在读一本鼓舞人心的居里夫人传记。)
- pro**gram** /ˈproʊˌgræm/ = pro (之前/向前) + gram (写) → 节目/程序：This software program is designed to be user-friendly. (这个软件程序设计得非常友好。)
- **graph**ic /ˈgræfɪk/ = graph (写/画) + ic (形容词后缀) → 图表的/生动的：The report includes several graphic illustrations. (报告包含了几幅图表插图。)


**plic/ply=fold 折叠/重叠**: 

- ap**ply** /əˈplaɪ/ = ap (向) + ply (折叠) → 折叠过去 → 申请/应用：You should apply for the scholarship before the deadline. (你应该在截止日期前申请奖学金。)
- ap**plic**ation /ˌæpləˈkeɪʃən/ = ap (向) + plic (折叠) + ation (名词后缀) → 申请/应用：The application of AI has transformed many industries. (人工智能的应用改变了许多行业。)
- ap**plic**ant /ˈæplɪkənt/ = ap (向) + plic (折叠) + ant (人) → 申请人：Each applicant must submit a resume and cover letter. (每位申请人都必须提交简历和求职信。)
- im**ply** /ˌɪmˈplaɪ/ = im (在内) + ply (折叠) → 折在里面 → 暗示/意指：His tone seemed to imply that he was unsatisfied. (他的语气似乎在暗示他不太满意。)
- re**ply** /rɪˈplaɪ/ = re (回) + ply (折叠) → 折回去 → 回复/回答：I sent her a message but she hasn't replied yet. (我给她发了消息，但她还没回复。)
- sup**ply** /səˈplaɪ/ = sup (从下面) + ply (折叠/填充) → 供应/提供：The company supplies office equipment to schools. (这家公司向学校供应办公设备。)
- com**plic**ate /ˈkɑmpləˌkeɪt/ = com (一起) + plic (折叠) + ate (动词后缀) → 折叠到一起 → 使复杂化（=make complex）：Too many details will only complicate the issue. (太多细节只会使问题复杂化。)
- com**plic**ated /ˈkɑmpləˌkeɪtəd/ = com (一起) + plic (折叠) + ated (形容词后缀) → 复杂的：The instructions are too complicated for beginners. (这些说明对初学者来说太复杂了。)
- ex**plic**it /ɪkˈsplɪsət/ = ex (向外) + plic (折叠) + it → 展开的 → 明确的/清楚的（=clear）：She gave explicit instructions on how to complete the task. (她对如何完成任务给出了明确的指示。)
- im**plic**it /ˌɪmˈplɪsət/ = im (在内) + plic (折叠) + it → 折在里面的 → 隐含的：There was an implicit agreement between the two parties. (双方之间有一个隐性的协议。)
- multi**ply** /ˈməltəˌplaɪ/ = multi (多) + ply (折叠) → 多次折叠 → 乘/繁殖：Rabbits can multiply at an astonishing rate. (兔子可以以惊人的速度繁殖。)
- **plur**al /ˈplʊrəl/ = plur (更多) + al (形容词后缀) → 复数/复数的："Children" is the irregular plural form of "child". ("Children"是"child"的不规则复数形式。)


**ploy/ploit=fold 折叠/用**: 

- em**ploy** /ɪmˈplɔɪ/ = em (入内) + ploy (折叠/卷入) → 雇佣/使用：The company plans to employ over 200 new workers this year. (公司计划今年雇佣200多名新员工。)
- em**ploy**ment /ɪmˈplɔɪmənt/ = em (入内) + ploy (折叠) + ment (名词后缀) → 就业/雇佣：The government is implementing policies to increase employment. (政府正在实施政策来提高就业。)
- em**ploy**er /ɪmˈplɔɪər/ = em (入内) + ploy (折叠) + er (人) → 雇主/老板：A responsible employer values the well-being of employees. (有责任心的雇主重视员工的福祉。)
- em**ploy**ee /ɪmˈplɔɪi/ = em (入内) + ploy (折叠) + ee (被……的人) → 雇员/员工：Every full-time employee is entitled to paid annual leave. (每位全职雇员都有权享受带薪年假。)
- unem**ploy**ment /ˌənɪmˈplɔɪmənt/ = un (不) + em (入内) + ploy (折叠) + ment (名词后缀) → 失业：Unemployment rates rose sharply during the economic crisis. (经济危机期间失业率急剧上升。)


**tang/tact/tag=touch 触摸**: 

- con**tact** /ˈkɑnˌtækt/ = con (一起/与) + tact (触摸) → 接触/联系：Please feel free to contact me if you have any questions. (如有任何问题，请随时与我联系。)
- in**tact** /ˌɪnˈtækt/ = in (不) + tact (触摸) → 未被触碰的 → 完整无损的（=unbroken）：The ancient temple remained intact after the earthquake. (古庙在地震后依然完好无损。)
- **tact**ic /ˈtæktɪk/ = tact (触摸/安排) + ic (……的艺术) → 战术/策略（=plan）：The coach developed a brilliant new tactic for the match. (教练为比赛制定了一个出色的新战术。)
- **tag** /tæg/ = tag (接触/标记) → 标签/标牌：Please attach a price tag to each item. (请给每件商品贴上价格标签。)


**pict=paint 画**: 

- **pict**ure /ˈpɪkʧər/ = pict (画) + ure (名词后缀) → 图画/照片：She drew a beautiful picture of the sunset over the ocean. (她画了一幅美丽的海上日落图画。)
- **pict**orial /pɪkˈtɔriəl/ = pict (画) + orial (形容词后缀) → 图画的/图片的：The book contains rich pictorial descriptions of ancient Rome. (这本书包含了描绘古罗马的丰富图画。)
- de**pict** /dɪˈpɪkt/ = de (完全) + pict (描绘) → 描绘/刻画（=show in picture）：The mural vividly depicts scenes from local history. (壁画生动地描绘了当地历史的场景。)
- **pict**uresque /ˈpɪkʧərəsk/ = pict (画) + uresque (……风格的) → 风景如画的（=scenic）：We spent the weekend in a picturesque little village. (我们在一个风景如画的小村庄度过了周末。)

#### 口与言语


★**dict=say/speak 说**: 

- **dict**ionary /ˈdɪkʃəˌnɛri/ = dict (说) + ion (名词后缀) + ary (名词后缀，表集合) → 字典/词典：I looked up the unfamiliar word in the dictionary. (我在词典里查了这个生词。)
- pre**dict** /prɪˈdɪkt/ = pre (前/预先) + dict (说) → 预测/预言（=tell beforehand）：The economist predicts that inflation will drop next quarter. (这位经济学家预测下季度通胀将下降。)
- **dict**ate /ˈdɪkˌteɪt/ = dict (说) + ate (动词后缀) → 口述/命令/支配（=say aloud）：The CEO dictated a memo to her assistant. (首席执行官向助理口述了一份备忘录。)
- **dict**ation /dɪkˈteɪʃən/ = dict (说) + ation (名词后缀) → 听写/口述：The students had a French dictation this morning. (学生们今早进行了法语听写。)
- contra**dict** /ˌkɑntrəˈdɪkt/ = contra (反对/相反) + dict (说) → 反驳/与……矛盾（=disagree with）：His later statement contradicts what he said earlier. (他后来的声明与他之前说的相矛盾。)
- ver**dict** /ˈvərdɪkt/ = ver (真实) + dict (说) → 裁决/判断/定论（=judgment）：The jury returned a verdict of guilty after deliberation. (陪审团经过评议后做出了有罪裁决。)
- in**dic**ate /ˈɪndəˌkeɪt/ = in (向内/朝向) + dic (说) + ate (动词后缀) → 表明/指示/暗示（=point to）：The survey results indicate strong public support for the policy. (调查结果表明公众对该政策有强烈支持。)
- de**dic**ate /ˈdɛdəˌkeɪt/ = de (向下/离开) + dic (说) + ate (动词后缀) → 奉献/致力于（=devote）：She dedicated her entire career to medical research. (她把整个职业生涯奉献给了医学研究。)


★**log/loqu=speak 说**: 

- dia**log**ue /ˈdaɪəˌlɔg/ = dia (穿过/之间) + logue (说) → 对话/对白：The two leaders engaged in a constructive dialogue on trade issues. (两位领导人就贸易问题进行了建设性对话。)
- apo**log**y /əˈpɑləˌʤi/ = apo (离开/脱离) + log (说) + y (名词后缀) → 道歉/歉意：He wrote a heartfelt apology for his rude behavior. (他为自己粗鲁的行为写了一封诚挚的道歉信。)
- apo**log**ize /əˈpɑləˌʤaɪz/ = apo (离开/脱离) + log (说) + ize (动词后缀) → 道歉/认错：I sincerely apologize for the misunderstanding. (我为这次误会真诚道歉。)
- **log**ic /ˈlɑʤɪk/ = log (说/推理) + ic (名词/形容词后缀) → 逻辑/推理/道理：There is a serious flaw in your logic. (你的逻辑中有严重漏洞。)
- **log**ical /ˈlɑʤɪkəl/ = log (说/推理) + ical (形容词后缀) → 逻辑的/合乎情理的：It is the most logical explanation for the phenomenon. (这是对该现象最合乎情理的解释。)
- mono**log**ue /ˈmɑnəˌlɔg/ = mono (单一/独自) + logue (说) → 独白/独角戏（=solo speech）：The actor's opening monologue captivated the audience. (那位演员的开场独白迷住了观众。)
- cata**log** /ˈkætəlɔg/ = cata (向下/完全) + log (说/列举) → 目录/编目：You can browse our entire product catalog online. (你可以在线浏览我们的全部产品目录。)


★**claim/clam=shout/cry out 呼喊**: 

- ex**claim** /ɪkˈskleɪm/ = ex (出/向外) + claim (呼喊) → 惊呼/大声说出（=shout out）："How wonderful!" she exclaimed when she saw the gift. ("太棒了！"她看到礼物时惊呼道。)
- pro**claim** /proʊˈkleɪm/ = pro (向前/公开) + claim (呼喊) → 宣布/宣告/声明（=announce publicly）：The president proclaimed a national day of mourning. (总统宣布了全国哀悼日。)
- ac**claim** /əˈkleɪm/ = ac (向) + claim (呼喊) → 称赞/欢呼/喝彩（=praise）：The novel was internationally acclaimed for its originality. (这部小说因其独创性而享誉国际。)
- **claim** /kleɪm/ = claim (呼喊/声称) → 声称/要求/索赔（=say）：He claims to have solved the puzzle in under a minute. (他声称不到一分钟就解开了那道谜题。)
- re**claim** /riˈkleɪm/ = re (回/重新) + claim (呼喊/要求) → 回收（=use again）/开垦/重新获得（=get back）：The company hopes to reclaim its position as market leader. (该公司希望重新夺回市场领导地位。)
- dis**claim** /dɪˈskleɪm/ = dis (否定/相反) + claim (声称/要求) → 否认/放弃权利（=deny）：The author disclaimed any intention to offend readers. (作者否认有任何冒犯读者的意图。)


★**voc/vok=call 叫/喊**: 

- **voic**e /vɔɪs/ = voic (呼唤/声音) + e → 声音/嗓音/发言权：She lost her voice after cheering at the concert. (她在音乐会上欢呼后嗓子哑了。)
- **voc**al /ˈvoʊkəl/ = voc (呼唤/声音) + al (形容词后缀) → 声音的（=sound-related）/直言不讳的：He has been a vocal critic of government corruption. (他一直是政府腐败问题的直言批评者。)
- ad**voc**ate /ˈædvəˌkeɪt/ = ad (朝向) + voc (呼唤) + ate (动词/名词后缀) → 提倡/拥护/倡导者（=support）：The organization advocates for animal rights worldwide. (该组织在全球倡导动物权益。)
- e**vok**e /ɪˈvoʊk/ = e (出/向外) + vok (呼唤) + e → 唤起/引起/使人想起（=bring to mind）：The old photograph evoked memories of her childhood. (那张旧照片勾起了她的童年回忆。)
- pro**vok**e /prəˈvoʊk/ = pro (向前/向外) + vok (呼唤) + e → 激怒/激起/引发（=stir up）：His sarcastic tone provoked an angry response from the crowd. (他讽刺的语气激起了人群的愤怒回应。)
- **voc**abulary /voʊˈkæbjəˌlɛri/ = voc (呼唤/声音) + abul (连接成分) + ary (名词后缀) → 词汇/词汇量：Reading widely is the best way to build your vocabulary. (广泛阅读是扩充词汇量的最佳方法。)
- **voc**ation /voʊˈkeɪʃən/ = voc (呼唤) + ation (名词后缀) → 职业/使命感（=calling）：She found her true vocation in nursing and never looked back. (她在护理中找到了自己真正的使命。)
- **voc**ational /voʊˈkeɪʃənəl/ = voc (呼唤) + ation (名词后缀) + al (形容词后缀) → 职业的/行业的（=job-related）：The school offers a range of vocational courses. (该校提供一系列职业课程。)


★**nounce/nunci=announce 宣布**: 

- an**nounce** /əˈnaʊns/ = an (向) + nounce (宣布/报告) → 宣布/公布/通告（=make known）：The company will announce its quarterly earnings next Monday. (公司将于下周一公布季度财报。)
- de**nounce** /dɪˈnaʊns/ = de (向下/反对) + nounce (宣布/报告) → 谴责/指责/告发（=condemn）：The UN denounced the invasion as a violation of international law. (联合国谴责此次入侵是对国际法的违反。)
- pro**nounce** /prəˈnaʊns/ = pro (向前) + nounce (宣布/报告) → 发音/宣布/断言（=say）：How do you pronounce this word correctly? (这个词怎么正确发音？)
- pro**nunci**ation /prəˌnənsiˈeɪʃən/ = pro (向前) + nunci (宣布/报告) + ation (名词后缀) → 发音/读法（=way of saying）：His English pronunciation has improved dramatically. (他的英语发音有了显著进步。)
- pro**nounce**d /prəˈnaʊnst/ = pro (向前) + nounce (宣布/报告) + ed (形容词后缀) → 明显的（=clear）/显著的（=noticeable）：There is a pronounced gap between rich and poor in the city. (这座城市里贫富差距十分明显。)
- re**nounce** /rɪˈnaʊns/ = re (回/背离) + nounce (宣布/报告) → 放弃/宣布放弃/断绝关系（=give up）：He renounced his inheritance and chose to make his own fortune. (他放弃了遗产继承，选择自己去创造财富。)


**fab/fam=speak 说**: 

- **fab**le /ˈfeɪbəl/ = fab (说/故事) + le (名词后缀) → 寓言/传说：The fable of the tortoise and the hare teaches the value of perseverance. (龟兔赛跑的寓言教会人们坚持不懈的价值。)
- **fab**ulous /ˈfæbjələs/ = fab (说/故事) + ulous (形容词后缀) → 极好的/惊人的（=amazing）：We spent a fabulous week exploring the islands of Greece. (我们在希腊群岛度过了美妙的一周。)
- **fam**ous /ˈfeɪməs/ = fam (说/名声) + ous (形容词后缀) → 著名的/出名的：The city is famous for its ancient temples and vibrant nightlife. (这座城市以其古老的寺庙和充满活力的夜生活而闻名。)
- **fam**e /feɪm/ = fam (说/名声) + e → 名声/声誉（=reputation）/名望（=reputation）：She rose to fame after starring in a blockbuster film. (她因主演了一部大片而成名。)
- in**fam**ous /ˈɪnfəməs/ = in (不/否定) + fam (说/名声) + ous (形容词后缀) → 臭名昭著的（=known for bad）/声名狼藉的（=notorious）：The prison was infamous for its harsh conditions. (那所监狱因恶劣的条件而臭名昭著。)
- de**fam**e /dɪˈfeɪm/ = de (向下/否定) + fam (说/名声) + e → 诽谤/中伤/诋毁（=attack reputation）：The politician sued the newspaper for attempting to defame him. (那位政治家起诉了那家报纸试图诽谤他的人格。)


**ora=speak/pray 说/祈祷**: 

- **ora**l /ˈɔrəl/ = ora (说) + al (形容词后缀) → 口头的/口腔的（=spoken）：We will have an oral presentation instead of a written exam. (我们将进行一次口头展示，而不是笔试。)

- **ador**e /əˈdɔr/ = ad (朝向) + or (说/祈祷) + e → 崇拜/爱慕/极喜欢（=love deeply）：I absolutely adore walking through the park on a crisp autumn morning. (我极喜欢在清爽的秋日早晨穿过公园散步。)



**plor=cry/wail 哭/喊**: 

- ex**plor**e /ɪkˈsplɔr/ = ex (出/向外) + plore (呼喊/哭泣) → 探索/探险/探究（=search）：We spent the afternoon exploring the narrow streets of the old town. (我们花了一个下午探索老城区的狭窄街道。)
- ex**plor**ation /ˌɛksplərˈeɪʃən/ = ex (出/向外) + plor (呼喊/哭泣) + ation (名词后缀) → 探索/勘探/研究（=search）：Space exploration has led to countless technological innovations. (太空探索带来了无数科技创新。)
- ex**plor**er /ɪkˈsplɔrər/ = ex (出/向外) + plor (呼喊/哭泣) + er (名词后缀，表行为者) → 探险家/探索者（=searcher）：Zheng He was one of the greatest explorers of the Ming Dynasty. (郑和是明代最伟大的探险家之一。)


#### 移动与趋向


★**ced/ceed/cess=go 走**: 

- pro**ceed** /pərˈsid/ = pro (向前) + ceed (走) → 进行/继续：We should proceed with the plan as scheduled. (我们应该按计划继续推进。)
- suc**ceed** /səkˈsid/ = suc (在下) + ceed (走) → 成功/继承：Hard work and persistence will help you succeed. (努力和坚持会帮助你成功。)
- suc**cess** /səkˈsɛs/ = suc (在下) + cess (走) → 成功/成就：His success came from years of dedicated effort. (他的成功来自多年的专注努力。)
- pro**cess** /ˈprɔˌsɛs/ = pro (向前) + cess (走) → 过程/处理：Learning a new language is a gradual process. (学习一门新语言是一个渐进的过程。)
- ac**cess** /ˈækˌsɛs/ = ac (向) + cess (走) → 进入/通道/访问（=entry）：Students have free access to the online library. (学生可以免费访问在线图书馆。)
- ex**cess** /ˈɛkˌsɛs/ = ex (超出) + cess (走) → 过度/过量（=too much）：Excess of anything can be harmful to health. (任何事物过度都对健康有害。)
- pre**ced**e /prɪˈsid/ = pre (在前) + cede (走) → 先于/在……之前（=come before）：The introduction precedes the main content of the book. (引言在书的正文之前。)
- re**ced**e /rɪˈsid/ = re (向后) + cede (走) → 后退/减退（=go back）：The flood waters began to recede after days of rain. (洪水在几天雨后开始退去。)
- con**ced**e /kənˈsid/ = con (共同) + cede (走) → 让步/承认（=admit）：He finally had to concede defeat in the debate. (他最终不得不在辩论中承认失败。)
- pro**ced**ure /prəˈsiʤər/ = pro (向前) + ced (走) + ure (名词后缀) → 程序/步骤（=steps）：Please follow the standard safety procedure. (请按照标准安全程序操作。)


★**mot/mob=move 移动**: 

- **mot**ion /ˈmoʊʃən/ = mot (移动) + ion (名词后缀) → 运动：The car was in constant motion on the highway. (汽车在高速公路上不停地运动。)
- pro**mot**e /prəˈmoʊt/ = pro (向前) + mot (移动) + e → 向前推动 → 促进（=boost）：The company launched a campaign to promote its new product. (公司发起了一场活动来推广新产品。)
- pro**mot**ion /pərˈmoʊʃən/ = pro (向前) + mot (移动) + ion (名词后缀) → 晋升/推广（=advancement）：She received a promotion after years of hard work. (经过多年努力，她获得了晋升。)
- **mob**ile /ˈmoʊbəl/ = mob (移动) + ile (形容词后缀) → 移动的（=moving）：Mobile phones have changed the way we communicate. (手机改变了我们的沟通方式。)
- auto**mob**ile /ˌɔtəmoʊˈbil/ = auto (自己) + mob (移动) + ile → 自己移动的 → 汽车：The automobile industry is shifting toward electric vehicles. (汽车工业正在向电动汽车转型。)
- **mot**ive /ˈmoʊtɪv/ = mot (移动) + ive (名词后缀) → 驱动力 → 动机（=reason）：The police are still trying to determine the motive for the crime. (警方仍在试图确定犯罪动机。)
- **mot**ivate /ˈmoʊtəˌveɪt/ = mot (移动) + ivate (动词后缀) → 使行动 → 激励（=encourage）：A good teacher knows how to motivate students to learn. (好老师知道如何激励学生学习。)
- e**mot**ion /ˈiˌmoʊʃən/ = e (向外) + mot (移动) + ion (名词后缀) → 向外表现出来 → 情感（=feeling）：He struggled to control his emotions during the speech. (他在演讲中努力控制自己的情感。)
- **mot**or /ˈmoʊtər/ = mot (移动) + or (名词后缀，物) → 让东西动起来的装置 → 马达（=engine）：The motor stopped working due to overheating. (马达因过热停止工作了。)
- **mov**ement /ˈmuvmənt/ = move (移动) + ment (名词后缀) → 运动/活动：The civil rights movement changed the course of history. (民权运动改变了历史的进程。)


★**ven/vent=come 来**: 

- **vent**ure /ˈvɛnʧər/ = vent (来) + ure (名词后缀) → 来到未知领域 → 冒险（=risky trip）：They decided to venture into the jungle alone. (他们决定独自冒险进入丛林。)
- in**vent** /ˌɪnˈvɛnt/ = in (进入) + vent (来) → 来到脑子里 → 发明（=create）：Thomas Edison helped invent the electric light bulb. (托马斯·爱迪生帮助发明了电灯泡。)
- in**vent**ion /ˌɪnˈvɛnʃən/ = in (进入) + vent (来) + ion (名词后缀) → 发明（=create）：The smartphone is one of the most important inventions of our time. (智能手机是我们这个时代最重要的发明之一。)
- in**vent**or /ˌɪnˈvɛntər/ = in (进入) + vent (来) + or (人) → 发明（=create）家：The inventor spent years perfecting his design. (这位发明家花了多年时间完善他的设计。)
- e**vent** /ɪˈvɛnt/ = e (出) + vent (来) → 出现的事情 → 事件（=happening）：The concert was the biggest event of the summer. (这场音乐会是夏季最大的活动。)
- e**vent**ually /ɪˈvɛnʧəwəli/ = e (出) + vent (来) + ual (形容词后缀) + ly (副词后缀) → 最终到来的 → 最终：After many delays, the project was eventually completed. (经过多次延误，项目最终完成了。)
- pre**vent** /prɪˈvɛnt/ = pre (前) + vent (来) → 提前来到阻止 → 防止（=stop）：Eating a balanced diet can help prevent many diseases. (均衡饮食有助于预防多种疾病。)
- pre**vent**ion /priˈvɛnʃən/ = pre (前) + vent (来) + ion (名词后缀) → 预防：Prevention is always better than cure. (预防总比治疗好。)
- ad**vent**ure /ədˈvɛnʧər/ = ad (向) + vent (来) + ure (名词后缀) → 向未知走来 → 冒险（=risky trip）：The children set out on an exciting adventure in the woods. (孩子们在树林里开始了一场激动人心的冒险。)
- a**ven**ue /ˈævəˌnu/ = a (向) + ven (来) + ue → 来的路 → 大道（=wide street）：The restaurant is located on a beautiful tree-lined avenue. (餐厅位于一条美丽的林荫大道上。)
- con**vent**ion /kənˈvɛnʃən/ = con (一起) + vent (来) + ion (名词后缀) → 大家来到一起 → 大会（=conference）/惯例（=custom）：By convention, the bride wears white at the wedding. (按照惯例，新娘在婚礼上穿白色礼服。)
- con**vent**ional /kənˈvɛnʃənəl/ = con (一起) + vent (来) + ion + al (形容词后缀) → 传统的（=usual）：She prefers conventional teaching methods to modern ones. (她偏爱传统教学方法而非现代方法。)
- re**ven**ue /ˈrɛvəˌnu/ = re (回) + ven (来) + ue → 回来的钱 → 收入（=earnings）：The company's annual revenue exceeded one billion dollars. (公司的年收入超过了十亿美元。)
- sou**ven**ir /ˌsuvəˈnɪr/ = sou (下) + ven (来) + ir → 从下面带来的 → 纪念品（=keepsake）：He bought a small souvenir from the gift shop. (他从礼品店买了一个小纪念品。)


★**grad/gress=step/walk 步/走**: 

- **grad**e /greɪd/ = grad (步) + e → 一步一步 → 年级/等级：She got the highest grade in the math exam. (她在数学考试中得了最高分。)
- **grad**ual /ˈgræʤuəl/ = grad (步) + ual (形容词后缀) → 一步一步的 → 逐渐的（=step by step）：There has been a gradual improvement in his health. (他的健康状况逐渐改善。)
- **grad**ually /ˈgræʤuəli/ = grad (步) + ual + ly (副词后缀) → 逐渐地（=step by step）：The noise gradually faded away as the plane took off. (随着飞机起飞，噪音逐渐消失。)
- **grad**uate /ˈgræʤəˌweɪt/ = grad (步) + uate (动词后缀) → 走完学业 → 毕业：She will graduate from university with honors this June. (她将于今年六月以优异成绩从大学毕业。)
- **grad**uation /ˌgræʤəˈweɪʃən/ = grad (步) + uation (名词后缀) → 毕业：His parents attended his graduation ceremony proudly. (他的父母骄傲地参加了他的毕业典礼。)
- pro**gress** /ˈprɑˌgrɛs/ = pro (向前) + gress (走) → 向前走 → 进步：The students are making good progress in their studies. (学生们在学习上取得了良好的进步。)
- pro**gress**ive /prəˈgrɛsɪv/ = pro (向前) + gress (走) + ive (形容词后缀) → 进步的/发展的：The company has a progressive policy on employee benefits. (该公司在员工福利方面有进步的政策。)
- ag**gress**ive /əˈgrɛsɪv/ = ag (向) + gress (走) + ive (形容词后缀) → 向前冲的 → 侵略的/好斗的（=hostile）：His aggressive driving style makes passengers nervous. (他激进的驾驶风格让乘客紧张。)
- con**gress** /ˈkɑŋgrəs/ = con (一起) + gress (走) → 走到一起 → 国会（=national meeting）：The new law was passed by Congress yesterday. (新法律昨天在国会通过了。)
- de**grad**e /dɪˈgreɪd/ = de (向下) + grad (步) + e → 向下走 → 降级/退化（=break down）：Plastic takes hundreds of years to degrade in the environment. (塑料需要数百年才能在环境中降解。)
- up**grad**e /ˈəpˈgreɪd/ = up (向上) + grad (步) + e → 向上走 → 升级（=improve）：I need to upgrade my computer to run the latest software. (我需要升级电脑来运行最新软件。)


★**cur/curs=run 跑**（→ rid/corridor 为意大利语音变形式）: 

- oc**cur** /əˈkər/ = oc (向) + cur (跑) → 跑出来 → 发生：Earthquakes occur frequently in this region. (这个地区地震频繁发生。)
- oc**cur**rence /əˈkərəns/ = oc (向) + cur (跑) + r + ence (名词后缀) → 发生/事件：Theft is a rare occurrence in this neighborhood. (盗窃在这个社区很少发生。)
- **cur**rent /ˈkɑrənt/ = curr (跑) + ent (形容词后缀) → 正在跑的 → 当前的（=present）/水流（=flow）：The current situation requires immediate attention. (当前的情况需要立即关注。)
- **cur**rency /ˈkərənsi/ = curr (跑/流通) + ency (名词后缀) → 流通的东西 → 货币/流通（=money）：The euro is the official currency of many European countries. (欧元是许多欧洲国家的官方货币。)
- **cur**riculum /kərˈɪkjələm/ = curr (跑) + iculum (名词后缀) → 跑步的轨道 → 课程（=study plan）：The school updated its curriculum to include more technology courses. (学校更新了课程，增加了更多技术课程。)
- **curs**or /ˈkərsər/ = curs (跑) + or (名词后缀，物) → 在屏幕上跑的东西 → 光标：Move the cursor to the beginning of the line. (将光标移到行首。)
- ex**curs**ion /ɪkˈskərʒən/ = ex (向外) + curs (跑) + ion (名词后缀) → 跑出去 → 远足（=short trip）：The school organized an excursion to the science museum. (学校组织了一次去科学博物馆的远足。)
- **cours**e /kɔrs/ = cours (跑) + e → 跑的路 → 课程（=study plan）/路线：The ship changed its course to avoid the storm. (船只改变了航线以避开风暴。)
- **corridor** /ˈkɔrɪdər/ = cor (一起) + rid (跑) + or (名词后缀)（rid ← cur 音变） → 一起跑的地方 → 走廊：The students walked quietly down the school corridor. (学生们安静地走过学校走廊。)


**it=go 走**: 

- ex**it** /ˈɛksət/ = ex (向外) + it (走) → 走出去 → 出口：Please use the emergency exit in case of fire. (发生火灾时请使用紧急出口。)
- in**it**ial /ˌɪˈnɪʃəl/ = in (进入) + it (走) + ial (形容词后缀) → 走进去的 → 最初的（=first）/首字母（=first letter）：The initial stage of the project is the most critical. (项目的最初阶段是最关键的。)
- in**it**ially /ˌɪˈnɪʃəli/ = in (进入) + it (走) + ial + ly (副词后缀) → 最初：Initially, I found the job difficult but I soon got used to it. (起初，我觉得这份工作很难，但很快就适应了。)
- in**it**iate /ˌɪˈnɪʃiˌeɪt/ = in (进入) + it (走) + iate (动词后缀) → 走进去 → 开始/发起（=start）：The government plans to initiate a nationwide vaccination program. (政府计划发起一个全国疫苗接种计划。)
- in**it**iative /ˌɪˈnɪʃətɪv/ = in (进入) + it (走) + iative (名词后缀) → 主动走进去 → 主动性（=drive）：She showed great initiative by solving the problem on her own. (她表现出了极大的主动性，自己解决了问题。)
- circu**it** /ˈsərkət/ = circ (环) + u + it (走) → 绕圈走 → 巡回（=loop）/电路（=electrical loop）：The electric circuit was broken, causing a power outage. (电路断了，导致停电。)
- trans**it** /ˈtrænzɪt/ = trans (穿过) + it (走) → 穿过走 → 运输/通行（=transport）：The package is in transit and should arrive tomorrow. (包裹正在运输中，应该明天到达。)
- trans**it**ion /trænˈzɪʃən/ = trans (穿过) + it (走) + ion (名词后缀) → 穿过走过去 → 过渡（=change）：The country is in a period of economic transition. (这个国家正处于经济转型期。)



**migr=move 迁移**: 

- **migr**ate /ˈmaɪˌgreɪt/ = migr (迁移) + ate (动词后缀) → 迁徙：Many birds migrate south before winter arrives. (许多鸟类在冬天到来前向南迁徙。)
- **migr**ation /maɪˈgreɪʃən/ = migr (迁移) + ation (名词后缀) → 迁徙：The annual migration of wildebeest attracts many tourists. (每年角马的迁徙吸引了大量游客。)
- im**migr**ant /ˈɪməgrənt/ = im (进入) + migr (迁移) + ant (人) → 移入的人 → 移民：My grandparents were immigrants who came to this country in the 1950s. (我的祖父母是1950年代来到这个国家的移民。)
- im**migr**ate /ˈɪməˌgreɪt/ = im (进入) + migr (迁移) + ate (动词后缀) → 移入：His family decided to immigrate to Canada for better opportunities. (他的家庭决定为了更好的机会移民到加拿大。)
- im**migr**ation /ˌɪməˈgreɪʃən/ = im (进入) + migr (迁移) + ation (名词后缀) → 移入/移民：Immigration policies have become stricter in recent years. (近年来移民政策变得更加严格了。)
- e**migr**ate /ˈɛməˌgreɪt/ = e (向外) + migr (迁移) + ate (动词后缀) → 移出 → 移居国外（=move abroad）：Many young people chose to emigrate in search of work. (许多年轻人选择移居国外寻找工作。)
- e**migr**ant /ˈɛməgrənt/ = e (向外) + migr (迁移) + ant (人) → 移出的人 → 移民：The ship carried hundreds of emigrants to a new land. (那艘船载着数百名移民前往新大陆。)
- **migr**ant /ˈmaɪgrənt/ = migr (迁移) + ant (人/形容词) → 迁徙者/流动工人（=moving worker）：Migrant workers often face difficult living conditions. (流动工人经常面临艰苦的生活条件。)


**scend/scens=climb 爬**: 

- a**scend** /əˈsɛnd/ = a (向) + scend (爬) → 向上爬 → 上升/登高（=go up）：The hikers began to ascend the mountain at dawn. (徒步者们在黎明时分开始登山。)
- de**scent** /dɪˈsɛnt/ = de (向下) + scent (爬) → 向下爬 → 下降（=go down）/血统（=ancestry）：The plane began its descent toward the airport. (飞机开始向机场下降。)
- de**scend**ant /dɪˈsɛndənt/ = de (向下) + scend (爬) + ant (人) → 向下传下来的人 → 后代（=offspring）：She claims to be a descendant of a famous poet. (她声称是一位著名诗人的后代。)
- de**scend** /dɪˈsɛnd/ = de (向下) + scend (爬) → 向下爬 → 下降：The elevator began to descend slowly to the ground floor. (电梯开始缓慢下降到一楼。)



**ori=rise/begin 升起/开始**: 

- **ori**gin /ˈɔrəʤən/ = ori (升起/开始) + gin (产生) → 起源的地方 → 起源/出身：Scientists are still studying the origin of the universe. (科学家们仍在研究宇宙的起源。)
- **ori**ginal /ərˈɪʤənəl/ = ori (升起) + gin + al (形容词后缀) → 原始的（=ancient）（=first）/独创的（=creative）：This is not a copy; it's the original painting. (这不是复制品，是原画。)
- **ori**ginality /ərˌɪʤəˈnælɪti/ = ori (升起) + gin + al + ity (名词后缀) → 独创性（=creativity）：The judges praised the originality of her design. (评委们称赞了她设计的独创性。)
- **ori**ginate /ərˈɪʤəˌneɪt/ = ori (升起/开始) + gin + ate (动词后缀) → 起源：The custom of giving red envelopes originates from ancient China. (发红包的习俗起源于古代中国。)
- **ori**ent /ˈɔriˌɛnt/ = ori (升起) + ent → 太阳升起的地方 → 东方（=east）/定向（=find direction）：The first few days are designed to orient new employees to the company. (最初几天旨在帮助新员工熟悉公司。)
- **ori**entation /ˌɔriɛnˈteɪʃən/ = ori (升起) + ent + ation (名词后缀) → 定位/方向/迎新：New students are required to attend the orientation program. (新生需要参加迎新活动。)
- dis**ori**ent /dɪˈsɔriˌɛnt/ = dis (否定/丧失) + ori (升起/方向) + ent → 使迷失方向（=confuse）：The fog disoriented the hikers on the trail. (大雾使徒步旅行者在路上迷失了方向。)


**pass=pass through 通过**: 

- **pass** /pæs/ = pass (通过) → 通过/经过：Please show your ID to pass through the security gate. (请出示身份证通过安检门。)
- **pass**age /ˈpæsɪʤ/ = pass (通过) + age (名词后缀) → 通过的通道 → 通道（=pathway）/段落（=section of text）：There is a secret passage behind the bookshelf. (书架后面有一条秘密通道。)
- **pass**enger /ˈpæsənʤər/ = pass (通过) + enger (人) → 通过的人 → 乘客：Each passenger is allowed one piece of carry-on luggage. (每位乘客允许携带一件随身行李。)
- **pass**port /ˈpæˌspɔrt/ = pass (通过) + port (港口) → 通过港口的凭证 → 护照：You need a valid passport to travel abroad. (出国旅行需要有效的护照。)
- **pas**t /pæst/ = pas(s) (通过) + t → 已经过去的 → 过去的：Don't dwell on the past; focus on the future instead. (不要沉湎于过去，而要着眼于未来。)
- com**pass** /ˈkəmpəs/ = com (一起) + pass (通过/步) → 一起走 → 指南针（=direction finder）/范围（=scope）：A compass needle always points to the magnetic north. (指南针的指针总是指向磁北。)
- sur**pass** /sərˈpæs/ = sur (超越) + pass (通过) → 超越过去 → 超越（=go past）：Her performance surpassed everyone's expectations. (她的表现超越了所有人的期望。)


#### 搬运携带与给予


★**fer=carry/bring 携带**: 

- trans**fer** /ˈtrænsfər/ = trans (跨越) + fer (携带) → 转移（=move）：Please transfer the money to my account. (请把钱转到我的账户。)
- re**fer** /rɪˈfər/ = re (回) + fer (携带) → 提及/参考（=look at）：You can refer to the manual for instructions. (你可以参考手册获取说明。)
- re**fer**ence /ˈrɛfərəns/ = re (回) + fer (携带) + ence (名词后缀) → 参考：Please provide a reference for your claim. (请为你的说法提供参考。)
- dif**fer** /ˈdɪfər/ = dif (分开) + fer (携带) → 不同/相异：Opinions differ on this issue. (在这个问题上意见不同。)
- dif**fer**ence /ˈdɪfərəns/ = dif (分开) + fer (携带) + ence (名词后缀) → 差异：There is a big difference between the two. (两者之间有巨大差异。)
- dif**fer**ent /ˈdɪfərənt/ = dif (分开) + fer (携带) + ent (形容词后缀) → 不同的：They have different opinions. (他们有不同的意见。)
- of**fer** /ˈɔfər/ = of (向) + fer (携带) → 提供：He offered me a cup of tea. (他给我提供了一杯茶。)
- con**fer**ence /ˈkɑnfərəns/ = con (一起) + fer (携带) + ence (名词后缀) → 会议：The conference will be held next week. (会议将于下周举行。)
- pre**fer** /prɪˈfər/ = pre (前) + fer (携带) → 偏爱（=like more）：I prefer tea to coffee. (比起咖啡我更喜欢茶。)
- pre**fer**ence /ˈprɛfərəns/ = pre (前) + fer (携带) + ence (名词后缀) → 偏好（=liking）：She has a preference for classical music. (她偏爱古典音乐。)
- suf**fer** /ˈsəfər/ = suf (在下) + fer (携带) → 遭受（=go through）：He suffered a lot during the war. (他在战争中遭受了很多苦难。)
- in**fer** /ˌɪnˈfər/ = in (入) + fer (携带) → 推断（=figure out）：What can we infer from the data? (我们能从数据中推断出什么？)
- **fer**tile /ˈfərtəl/ = fer (携带/产出) + ile (能…的) → 肥沃的（=rich in nutrients）：The soil here is very fertile. (这里的土壤非常肥沃。)
- **fer**tilizer /ˈfərtəˌlaɪzər/ = fer (携带/产出) + il(e) + iz(e) (动词后缀) + er (物) → 肥料：Farmers use fertilizer to help crops grow. (农民使用肥料帮助庄稼生长。)


★**port=carry 搬运**: 

- trans**port** /ˈtrænspɔrt/ = trans (跨越) + port (搬运) → 运输：The goods are transported by truck. (货物由卡车运输。)
- im**port** /ˌɪmˈpɔrt/ = im (进入) + port (搬运) → 进口：The country imports oil from abroad. (该国从国外进口石油。)
- ex**port** /ˈɛkspɔrt/ = ex (出) + port (搬运) → 出口：They export tea to many countries. (他们向许多国家出口茶叶。)
- **port**able /ˈpɔrtəbəl/ = port (搬运) + able (能…的) → 便携的（=easy to carry）：This laptop is light and portable. (这台笔记本电脑轻便易携。)
- sup**port** /səˈpɔrt/ = sup (从下) + port (搬运) → 支撑（=hold up）/支持（=hold up）：Thank you for your support. (谢谢你的支持。)
- re**port** /rɪˈpɔrt/ = re (回) + port (搬运) → 报告/汇报（=tell about）：She wrote a detailed report. (她写了一份详细的报告。)
- **port**er /ˈpɔrtər/ = port (搬运) + er (人) → 搬运工：The porter helped carry our luggage. (搬运工帮我们搬运行李。)
- **port**ion /ˈpɔrʃən/ = port (搬运/分配) + ion (名词后缀) → 部分（=piece）：A large portion of the budget goes to education. (预算的一大部分用于教育。)
- pro**port**ion /prəˈpɔrʃən/ = pro (向前) + port (分配) + ion (名词后缀) → 比例（=ratio）：The proportion of men to women is roughly equal. (男女比例大致相等。)


★**miss/mit=send 发送**: 

- ad**mit** /ədˈmɪt/ = ad (向) + mit (发送) → 承认（=confess）/接纳（=let in）：He admitted his mistake honestly. (他诚实地承认了错误。)
- ad**miss**ion /ədˈmɪʃən/ = ad (向) + miss (发送) + ion (名词后缀) → 承认（=confession）/入场券（=entry ticket）：Admission to the museum is free on Sundays. (博物馆周日免费入场。)
- com**mit** /kəˈmɪt/ = com (一起) + mit (发送) → 犯(罪)（=do wrong）/承诺（=pledge）：He committed a serious crime. (他犯下了严重的罪行。)
- com**mit**ment /kəˈmɪtmənt/ = com (一起) + mit (发送) + ment (名词后缀) → 承诺（=pledge）：She has a strong commitment to her work. (她对工作有很强的承诺感。)
- e**mit** /ɪˈmɪt/ = e (出) + mit (发送) → 发出/排放（=send out）：The factory emits harmful gases. (工厂排放有害气体。)
- o**miss**ion /oʊˈmɪʃən/ = o (不) + miss (发送) + ion (名词后缀) → 省略（=leave out）：The omission of his name was intentional. (他名字的省略是故意的。)
- o**mit** /oʊˈmɪt/ = o (不) + mit (发送) → 省略（=leave out）：Please don't omit any details. (请不要省略任何细节。)
- per**mit** /ˈpərˌmɪt/ = per (通过) + mit (发送) → 允许（=allow）：Smoking is not permitted here. (此处不允许吸烟。)
- per**miss**ion /pərˈmɪʃən/ = per (通过) + miss (发送) + ion (名词后缀) → 许可（=permission）：You need permission to enter. (你需要许可才能进入。)
- sub**mit** /səbˈmɪt/ = sub (在下) + mit (发送) → 提交（=hand in）：Please submit your report by Friday. (请在周五前提交报告。)
- trans**mit** /trænzˈmɪt/ = trans (跨越) + mit (发送) → 传输/传播（=send across）：The signal is transmitted via satellite. (信号通过卫星传输。)
- trans**miss**ion /trænzˈmɪʃən/ = trans (跨越) + miss (发送) + ion (名词后缀) → 传输/传播（=send across）：The transmission of data is fast. (数据传输很快。)
- pro**mise** /ˈprɑməs/ = pro (向前) + mise (发送) → 承诺（=pledge）：I promise to help you. (我承诺会帮助你。)
- pro**mis**ing /ˈprɑməsɪŋ/ = pro (向前) + mis (发送) + ing (形容词后缀) → 有前途的（=hopeful）：She is a promising young artist. (她是一位有前途的年轻艺术家。)
- **miss**ion /ˈmɪʃən/ = miss (发送) + ion (名词后缀) → 使命/任务（=task）：Their mission is to explore the planet. (他们的使命是探索这颗行星。)
- **miss**ile /ˈmɪsəl/ = miss (发送) + ile (物) → 导弹：The missile was launched successfully. (导弹成功发射了。)
- dis**miss** /dɪsˈmɪs/ = dis (离开) + miss (发送) → 解散/解雇（=fire）：The boss decided to dismiss him. (老板决定解雇他。)
- **miss** /mɪs/ = miss (错过/未击中) → 错过：I missed the bus this morning. (我今天早上错过了公交车。)
- **mess**age /ˈmɛsɪʤ/ = mess (发送) + age (名词后缀) → 信息：I left a message on your phone. (我在你手机上留了信息。)
- **mess**enger /ˈmɛsɪnʤər/ = mess (发送) + enger (人) → 信使：The messenger delivered the letter promptly. (信使及时送达了信件。)


★**tribut=give 给予**: 

- con**tribut**e /kənˈtrɪbjut/ = con (一起) + tribut (给予) + e → 贡献/捐献（=give）：Everyone should contribute to the team. (每个人都应该为团队做贡献。)
- con**tribut**ion /ˌkɑntrəˈbjuʃən/ = con (一起) + tribut (给予) + ion (名词后缀) → 贡献（=give）：His contribution to science is remarkable. (他对科学的贡献是卓越的。)
- dis**tribut**e /dɪˈstrɪbjut/ = dis (分开) + tribut (给予) + e → 分配（=set aside）/分发（=give out）：The teacher distributed the test papers. (老师分发了试卷。)
- dis**tribut**ion /ˌdɪstrəˈbjuʃən/ = dis (分开) + tribut (给予) + ion (名词后缀) → 分配（=set aside）/分布（=spread）：The distribution of wealth is unequal. (财富分配是不平等的。)
- at**tribut**e /əˈtrɪˌbjut/ = at (向) + tribut (给予) + e → 归因于（=credit）/属性（=quality）：She attributes her success to hard work. (她把成功归因于努力工作。)
- **tribut**e /ˈtrɪbjut/ = tribut (给予) + e → 贡品/颂词（=gift of praise）：The crowd paid tribute to the hero. (人群向英雄致敬。)


**lat=carry/bring 携带**: 

- re**lat**e /rɪˈleɪt/ = re (回) + lat (携带) + e → 关联（=connect）/叙述（=tell）：I can relate to her experience. (我能理解她的经历。)
- re**lat**ion /riˈleɪʃən/ = re (回) + lat (携带) + ion (名词后缀) → 关系：They have a good working relation. (他们有良好的工作关系。)
- re**lat**ive /ˈrɛlətɪv/ = re (回) + lat (携带) + ive (形容词后缀) → 相对的（=compared）/亲戚（=family member）：She invited all her relatives to the wedding. (她邀请了所有亲戚参加婚礼。)
- re**lat**ionship /riˈleɪʃənˌʃɪp/ = re (回) + lat (携带) + ion + ship (名词后缀，表状态) → 关系：They have a close relationship. (他们有亲密的关系。)
- trans**lat**e /trænzˈleɪt/ = trans (跨越) + lat (携带) + e → 翻译（=change language）：Can you translate this into English? (你能把这个翻译成英语吗？)
- trans**lat**ion /trænzˈleɪʃən/ = trans (跨越) + lat (携带) + ion (名词后缀) → 翻译（=change language）：The translation is accurate and clear. (翻译准确而清晰。)
- trans**lat**or /trænzˈleɪtər/ = trans (跨越) + lat (携带) + or (人) → 翻译（=change language）者：She works as a translator at the UN. (她在联合国做翻译。)
- corre**lat**e /ˈkɔrəˌleɪt/ = cor (一起) + re (回) + lat (携带) + e → 相关（=be connected）：Stress levels correlate with health problems. (压力水平与健康问题相关。)


**don/dot=give 给**: 

- **don**ate /ˈdoʊˌneɪt/ = don (给) + ate (动词后缀) → 捐赠（=give away）：He decided to donate blood to help others. (他决定献血帮助他人。)
- **don**ation /doʊˈneɪʃən/ = don (给) + ation (名词后缀) → 捐赠（=give away）：The charity received a large donation. (慈善机构收到了一大笔捐款。)
- **don**or /ˈdoʊnər/ = don (给) + or (人) → 捐赠（=give away）者：The donor wishes to remain anonymous. (捐赠者希望保持匿名。)
- par**don** /ˈpɑrdən/ = par (完全) + don (给) → 原谅（=forgive）：Please pardon me for interrupting. (请原谅我打断你。)
- anti**dot**e /ˈænɪˌdoʊt/ = anti (对抗) + dot (给) + e → 解药（=cure）：There is no known antidote for this poison. (这种毒药没有已知的解药。)
- **dos**e /doʊs/ = dos (给) + e → 剂量（=amount）：Take one dose of medicine every six hours. (每六小时服一剂药。)


★**duc/duct=lead 引导**:

- e**duc**ate /ˈɛʤəˌkeɪt/ = e (出) + duc (引导) + ate (动词后缀) → 引出知识 → 教育（=teach）：Parents should educate their children about safety.
- e**duc**ation /ˌɛʤəˈkeɪʃən/ = e (出) + duc (引导) + ation (名词后缀) → 教育（=teaching）：Education is the key to a successful future.
- e**duc**ator /ˈɛʤəˌkeɪtər/ = e (出) + duc (引导) + ator (人) → 教育者（=teacher）：She is a dedicated educator who inspires her students.
- in**troduc**e /ˌɪntrəˈdus/ = intro (进入) + duc (引导) + e → 引进/介绍（=present）：Let me introduce you to my friend.
- pro**duc**e /ˈproʊdus/ = pro (向前) + duc (引导) + e → 向前引 → 生产（=make）：This factory produces high-quality toys.
- pro**duc**t /ˈprɑdəkt/ = pro (向前) + duct (引导) → 产品（=goods）：The new product was a great success.
- pro**duc**tion /pərˈdəkʃən/ = pro (向前) + duct (引导) + ion (名词后缀) → 生产（=making）：The production of cars has increased this year.
- re**duc**e /rɪˈdus/ = re (回) + duc (引导) + e → 引回 → 减少（=make less）：Please reduce the amount of salt in your cooking.
- re**duc**tion /rɪˈdəkʃən/ = re (回) + duct (引导) + ion (名词后缀) → 减少（=decrease）：There has been a reduction in price.
- con**duct** /ˈkɑndəkt/ = con (一起) + duct (引导) → 引导到一起 → 指挥（=lead）/行为（=behavior）：The students must follow the school rules and conduct themselves well.
- con**duct**or /kənˈdəktər/ = con (一起) + duct (引导) + or (人) → 指挥引导的人 → 售票员/指挥（=leader）：The bus conductor collected the fares.
- **duct** /dəkt/ = duct (引导) → 管道（=tube）：The air duct needs to be cleaned regularly.

#### 一般动作


★**act/ag=do/drive 做/驱动**: 

- **act**ion /ˈækʃən/ = act (做) + ion (名词后缀) → 行动：We need to take immediate action. (我们需要立即采取行动。)
- **act**ive /ˈæktɪv/ = act (做) + ive (形容词后缀) → 积极的/活跃的（=busy）：She stays active by jogging every day. (她每天慢跑保持活跃。)
- **ag**ent /ˈeɪʤənt/ = ag (做) + ent (人) → 代理人/经纪人（=representative）：The agent negotiated the deal on his behalf. (代理人代表他谈判了这笔交易。)
- re**act** /riækt/ = re (回) + act (做/行动) → 反应（=respond）：How did he react to the news? (他对这个消息反应如何？)
- **ag**enda /əˈʤɛndə/ = ag (做) + enda (名词后缀，表待做) → 议程（=plan）：The first item on the agenda is the budget. (议程的第一项是预算。)
- **ag**ency /ˈeɪʤənsi/ = ag (做) + ency (名词后缀) → 机构/代理处（=organization）：She works for a travel agency. (她在一家旅行社工作。)
- ex**act** /ɪgˈzækt/ = ex (出) + act (做/驱动) → 精确的（=exact）/强求（=demand）：Give me the exact time please. (请告诉我确切的时间。)
- inter**act** /ˌɪnərˈækt/ = inter (之间) + act (做/行动) → 互动（=interact）：Children learn to interact with others. (孩子们学习与他人互动。)


★**fact/fect/fic=make/do 做**: 

- **fact**ory /ˈfæktəri/ = fact (做) + ory (场所) → 工厂：The factory produces thousands of cars each year. (这家工厂每年生产数千辆汽车。)
- **fact**or /ˈfæktər/ = fact (做) + or (物) → 因素：Weather is an important factor in farming. (天气是农业的重要因素。)
- af**fect** /əˈfɛkt/ = af (向) + fect (做) → 影响（=effect）：The weather can affect your mood. (天气会影响你的心情。)
- af**fect**ion /əˈfɛkʃən/ = af (向) + fect (做) + ion (名词后缀) → 感情/喜爱（=love）：She has deep affection for her family. (她对家人有深厚的感情。)
- ef**fect** /ˈifɛkt/ = ef (出) + fect (做) → 效果/影响（=result）：The medicine had an immediate effect. (药效立竿见影。)
- ef**fect**ive /ˈifɛktɪv/ = ef (出) + fect (做) + ive (形容词后缀) → 有效的（=working）：This is an effective way to learn. (这是有效的学习方法。)
- in**fect** /ˌɪnˈfɛkt/ = in (入) + fect (做) → 感染（=spread disease）：The wound became infected. (伤口感染了。)
- per**fect** /ˈpərˌfɪkt/ = per (彻底) + fect (做) → 完美的（=flawless）：Practice makes perfect. (熟能生巧。)
- ef**fic**ient /ɪˈfɪʃənt/ = ef (出) + fic (做) + ient (形容词后缀) → 高效的（=productive）：This machine is very efficient. (这台机器非常高效。)
- ef**fic**iency /ɪˈfɪʃənsi/ = ef (出) + fic (做) + iency (名词后缀) → 效率（=productivity）：We need to improve work efficiency. (我们需要提高工作效率。)
- bene**fic**ial /ˌbɛnəˈfɪʃəl/ = bene (好) + fic (做) + ial (形容词后缀) → 有益的（=helpful）：Exercise is beneficial to health. (锻炼对健康有益。)
- bene**fit** /ˈbɛnəfɪt/ = bene (好) + fit (做) → 利益/好处（=good）：The new policy will benefit everyone. (新政策将使所有人受益。)
- de**fect** /ˈdifɛkt/ = de (否定) + fect (做) → 缺陷/缺点（=flaw）：The product was recalled due to a defect. (产品因缺陷被召回。)
- de**fic**ient /dɪˈfɪʃənt/ = de (否定) + fic (做) + ient (形容词后缀) → 不足的（=lacking）：His diet is deficient in vitamins. (他的饮食缺乏维生素。)
- **fic**tion /ˈfɪkʃən/ = fict (做/编造) + ion (名词后缀) → 小说（=made-up story）：She enjoys reading science fiction. (她喜欢读科幻小说。)
- pro**fic**ient /prɑˈfɪʃənt/ = pro (向前) + fic (做) + ient (形容词后缀) → 熟练的（=skilled）：He is proficient in three languages. (他精通三种语言。)
- suf**fic**ient /səˈfɪʃənt/ = suf (在下) + fic (做) + ient (形容词后缀) → 足够的（=enough）：One hour is sufficient for the task. (一小时足够完成这个任务。)
- sacri**fic**e /ˈsækrəˌfaɪs/ = sacri (神圣) + fice (做) → 牺牲（=give up）：She sacrificed her career for her family. (她为家庭牺牲了事业。)
- of**fic**ial /əˈfɪʃəl/ = of (向) + fic (做) + ial (形容词后缀) → 官方的（=formal）：The official announcement will be made tomorrow. (官方公告将于明天发布。)
- arti**fic**ial /ˌɑrtəˈfɪʃəl/ = art (艺术/技巧) + i + fic (做) + ial (形容词后缀) → 人工的（=man-made）：These are artificial flowers. (这些是人造花。)


★**struct=build 建造**: 

- con**struct** /ˈkɑnstrəkt/ = con (一起) + struct (建造) → 建造/构造（=build）：They plan to construct a new bridge. (他们计划建造一座新桥。)
- con**struct**ion /kənˈstrəkʃən/ = con (一起) + struct (建造) + ion (名词后缀) → 建造/建筑物（=building）：The construction of the building took two years. (这栋建筑的建造用了两年。)
- **struct**ure /ˈstrəkʧər/ = struct (建造) + ure (名词后缀) → 结构（=framework）：The structure of the essay is clear. (这篇文章的结构很清晰。)
- de**struct**ion /dɪˈstrəkʃən/ = de (否定/相反) + struct (建造) + ion (名词后缀) → 破坏（=tear down）：The earthquake caused widespread destruction. (地震造成了广泛破坏。)
- in**struct**ion /ˌɪnˈstrəkʃən/ = in (入) + struct (建造) + ion (名词后缀) → 指示/教导（=teach）：Read the instructions carefully before use. (使用前请仔细阅读说明。)
- in**struct** /ˌɪnˈstrəkt/ = in (入) + struct (建造) → 教导/指示（=teach）：The coach instructed the players on the new strategy. (教练指导球员新战术。)
- in**struct**or /ˌɪnˈstrəktər/ = in (入) + struct (建造) + or (人) → 指导者/教练（=teacher）：The swimming instructor is very patient. (游泳教练非常有耐心。)
- in**stru**ment /ˈɪnstrəmənt/ = in (入) + stru (建造) + ment (名词后缀) → 工具/乐器（=tool）：She plays several musical instruments. (她会演奏几种乐器。)
- ob**struct** /əbˈstrəkt/ = ob (对着/阻碍) + struct (建造) → 阻碍（=block）：Don't obstruct the entrance please. (请不要挡住入口。)
- infra**struct**ure /ˌɪnfrəˈstrəkʧər/ = infra (在下) + struct (建造) + ure (名词后缀) → 基础设施（=basic facilities）：The government invests heavily in infrastructure. (政府在基础设施上大量投资。)


★**ject=throw 投掷**: 

- pro**ject** /ˈprɑʤɛkt/ = pro (向前) + ject (投掷) → 投射/项目（=undertaking）：The team is working on a new project. (团队正在做一个新项目。)
- re**ject** /ˈriʤɛkt/ = re (回) + ject (投掷) → 拒绝（=saying no）：The committee rejected his proposal. (委员会拒绝了他的提议。)
- in**ject** /ˌɪnˈʤɛkt/ = in (进入) + ject (投掷) → 注射/注入（=put in）：The doctor injected the vaccine into his arm. (医生将疫苗注射到他手臂中。)
- e**ject** /ɪˈʤɛkt/ = e (出) + ject (投掷) → 弹出/驱逐（=throw out）：Press the button to eject the CD. (按按钮弹出CD。)
- sub**ject** /ˈsəbʤɪkt/ = sub (在下) + ject (投掷) → 主题/隶属（=topic）：The subject of the lecture is climate change. (讲座的主题是气候变化。)
- ob**ject** /ˈɑbʤɛkt/ = ob (对着) + ject (投掷) → 物体（=thing）/反对（=disagree）：I object to this decision. (我反对这个决定。)
- ob**ject**ive /əˈbʤɛktɪv/ = ob (对着) + ject (投掷) + ive (形容词后缀) → 客观的（=factual）/目标（=goal）：We need to set clear objectives. (我们需要设定明确的目标。)
- ad**ject**ive /ˈæʤɪktɪv/ = ad (向) + ject (投掷) + ive (形容词后缀) → 形容词："Beautiful" is an adjective. ("Beautiful"是形容词。)


★**vert/vers=turn 转**: 

- con**vert** /ˈkɑnvərt/ = con (一起/完全) + vert (转) → 转换（=change）：They converted the old factory into an art gallery. (他们把旧工厂改造成了美术馆。)
- re**vers**e /rɪˈvərs/ = re (回) + vers (转) + e → 反转/颠倒（=flip）：Please reverse the car into the parking space. (请把车倒进停车位。)
- ad**vert**ise /ˈædvərˌtaɪz/ = ad (向) + vert (转) + ise (动词后缀) → 做广告（=promote）：They advertise their products on TV. (他们在电视上做产品广告。)
- di**vers**e /dɪˈvərs/ = di (分开) + vers (转) + e → 多样的（=varied）：The city has a diverse population. (这座城市有多元化的人口。)
- di**vers**ity /dɪˈvərsɪti/ = di (分开) + vers (转) + ity (名词后缀) → 多样性（=variety）：We value cultural diversity. (我们重视文化多样性。)
- **vers**ion /ˈvərʒən/ = vers (转) + ion (名词后缀) → 版本（=variant）：This is the latest version of the software. (这是软件的最新版本。)
- uni**vers**ity /ˌjunəˈvərsəti/ = uni (一) + vers (转) + ity (名词后缀) → 大学：She studies at a famous university. (她在一所著名大学学习。)
- uni**vers**al /ˌjunəˈvərsəl/ = uni (一) + vers (转) + al (形容词后缀) → 普遍的（=widespread）：Music is a universal language. (音乐是普遍的语言。)
- con**vers**ation /ˌkɑnvərˈseɪʃən/ = con (一起) + vers (转) + ation (名词后缀) → 对话/交谈（=talk）：We had a pleasant conversation over dinner. (我们在晚餐时进行了愉快的交谈。)
- **vert**ical /ˈvərtɪkəl/ = vert (转) + ical (形容词后缀) → 垂直的（=upright）：The cliff is almost vertical. (这个悬崖几乎是垂直的。)
- anni**vers**ary /ˌænəˈvərsəri/ = anni (年) + vers (转) + ary (名词后缀) → 周年纪念日（=yearly reminder）：They celebrated their 10th wedding anniversary. (他们庆祝了结婚十周年纪念日。)
- contro**vers**y /ˈkɑntrəˌvərsi/ = contro (反对) + vers (转) + y (名词后缀) → 争议（=disagreement）：The new law caused a lot of controversy. (新法律引起了很多争议。)


★**pel/puls=drive/push 推**: 

- com**pel** /kəmˈpɛl/ = com (一起/加强) + pel (推) → 迫使/强迫（=force）：The law compels drivers to wear seat belts. (法律强制司机系安全带。)
- re**pel** /rɪˈpɛl/ = re (回) + pel (推) → 击退/排斥（=push away）：This spray repels mosquitoes effectively. (这种喷雾有效驱蚊。)
- ex**pel** /ɪkˈspɛl/ = ex (出) + pel (推) → 开除/驱逐（=kick out）：He was expelled from school for bad behavior. (他因不良行为被学校开除。)
- im**puls**e /ˌɪmˈpəls/ = im (向内) + puls (推) + e → 冲动（=sudden urge）：He bought the car on impulse. (他一时冲动买了那辆车。)
- com**puls**ory /kəmˈpəlsəri/ = com (一起/加强) + puls (推) + ory (形容词后缀) → 强制性的（=required）：Education is compulsory for all children. (所有儿童都必须接受义务教育。)
- **puls**e /pəls/ = puls (推/跳动) + e → 脉搏（=heartbeat）：The doctor checked her pulse. (医生检查了她的脉搏。)
- dis**pel** /dɪˈspɛl/ = dis (分开) + pel (推) → 驱散/消除（=remove）：The news dispelled all our doubts. (这条消息消除了我们所有的疑虑。)


**pend/pens=hang/weigh 悬挂/称量**: 

- de**pend** /dɪˈpɛnd/ = de (下) + pend (悬挂) → 依赖（=rely on）：Children depend on their parents for food and shelter. (孩子们依赖父母提供食物和住所。)
- de**pend**ent /dɪˈpɛndənt/ = de (下) + pend (悬挂) + ent (形容词后缀) → 依赖（=rely on）的：He is financially dependent on his parents. (他在经济上依赖父母。)
- inde**pend**ent /ˌɪndɪˈpɛndənt/ = in (不) + de (下) + pend (悬挂) + ent (形容词后缀) → 独立的（=free）：She is an independent woman with her own career. (她是一位有自己事业的独立女性。)
- inde**pend**ence /ˌɪndɪˈpɛndəns/ = in (不) + de (下) + pend (悬挂) + ence (名词后缀) → 独立（=freedom）：The country gained independence in 1960. (这个国家在1960年获得独立。)
- sus**pend** /səˈspɛnd/ = sus (在下) + pend (悬挂) → 悬挂（=hang）/暂停（=pause）：The bridge is suspended by steel cables. (这座桥由钢缆悬吊着。)
- sus**pens**e /səˈspɛns/ = sus (在下) + pens (悬挂) + e → 悬念/紧张（=uncertainty）：The movie kept us in suspense until the end. (这部电影让我们一直紧张到结尾。)
- ex**pens**ive /ɪkˈspɛnsɪv/ = ex (出) + pens (称量/花费) + ive (形容词后缀) → 昂贵的（=costly）：That watch is too expensive for me. (那块手表对我来说太贵了。)
- ex**pens**e /ɪkˈspɛns/ = ex (出) + pens (称量) + e → 花费/开销（=cost）：Traveling is a major expense for the company. (差旅是公司的主要开销。)
- **pens**ion /ˈpɛnʃən/ = pens (称量/支付) + ion (名词后缀) → 养老金（=retirement pay）：He receives a monthly pension from the government. (他每月从政府领取养老金。)
- ap**pend**ix /əˈpɛndɪks/ = ap (向) + pend (悬挂) + ix → 附录（=extra part）：The data is listed in the appendix at the end. (数据列在末尾的附录中。)
- com**pens**ate /ˈkɑmpənˌseɪt/ = com (一起) + pens (称量) + ate (动词后缀) → 补偿（=pay back）：The company compensated workers for overtime. (公司为加班工人提供补偿。)
- com**pens**ation /ˌkɑmpənˈseɪʃən/ = com (一起) + pens (称量) + ation (名词后缀) → 补偿（=pay back）：He received compensation for his injury. (他因受伤获得了赔偿。)
- **pend**ing /ˈpɛndɪŋ/ = pend (悬挂) + ing (形容词后缀) → 待定的/悬而未决的（=undecided）：The case is still pending in court. (这个案子仍在法院审理中。)
- **pend**ulum /ˈpɛnʤələm/ = pend (悬挂) + ulum (名词后缀) → 钟摆（=swinging weight）：The pendulum swings back and forth. (钟摆来回摆动。)


**sum/sumpt=take 拿/取**: 

- con**sum**e /kənˈsum/ = con (一起/完全) + sum (拿/取) + e → 消费/消耗（=use）：The fire consumed the entire building. (大火吞噬了整栋建筑。)
- con**sum**er /kənˈsumər/ = con (一起/完全) + sum (拿/取) + er (人) → 消费者（=user）：Consumers have the right to refund. (消费者有权退款。)
- con**sumpt**ion /kənˈsəmʃən/ = con (一起/完全) + sumpt (拿/取) + ion (名词后缀) → 消费/消耗（=use）：Fuel consumption increases at high speed. (高速行驶时油耗增加。)
- as**sum**e /əˈsum/ = as (向) + sum (拿/取) + e → 假设（=guess）/承担（=take on）：We cannot assume he is guilty. (我们不能假设他有罪。)
- as**sumpt**ion /əˈsəmpʃən/ = as (向) + sumpt (拿/取) + ion (名词后缀) → 假设（=guess）：That's a dangerous assumption. (那是一个危险的假设。)
- re**sum**e /ˈrɛzəˌmeɪ/ = re (再) + sum (拿) + e → 重新开始（=restart）/简历（=CV）：The meeting will resume after lunch. (会议将在午餐后继续。)
- pre**sum**e /prɪˈzum/ = pre (提前) + sum (拿/取) + e → 假定/推测（=guess）：I presume you've already met her. (我猜想你已经见过她了。)
- **sum** /səm/ = sum (总计) → 总计/和：The sum of two plus three is five. (二加三的和是五。)
- **sum**mary /ˈsəməri/ = sum (总) + mary (名词后缀) → 摘要/总结（=short form）：Please write a brief summary of the article. (请写一篇文章的简短摘要。)
- **sum**marize /ˈsəmərˌaɪz/ = sum (总) + marize (动词后缀) → 总结/概括（=shorten）：Can you summarize the main points? (你能概括一下要点吗？)
- **sum**mit /ˈsəmɪt/ = summ (最高/总) + it (名词后缀) → 顶峰/峰会（=top）：The leaders attended the global summit. (领导人出席了全球峰会。)


**fus=pour 倾/倒**: 

- re**fus**e /ˈrɛfˌjuz/ = re (回) + fus (倒) + e → 拒绝（=saying no）：She refused his invitation politely. (她礼貌地拒绝了他的邀请。)
- re**fus**al /rɪfˈjuzəl/ = re (回) + fus (倒) + al (名词后缀) → 拒绝（=saying no）：His refusal to help surprised everyone. (他的拒绝帮助令所有人惊讶。)
- con**fus**e /kənfˈjuz/ = con (一起) + fus (倒) + e → 使困惑/混淆（=mix up）：Don't confuse me with too many details. (不要用太多细节把我搞糊涂。)
- con**fus**ion /kənfˈjuʒən/ = con (一起) + fus (倒) + ion (名词后缀) → 困惑/混乱（=disorder）：There was confusion after the announcement. (公告后出现了混乱。)
- dif**fus**e /dɪfˈjuz/ = dif (分开) + fus (倒) + e → 扩散/散播（=spread）：The aroma of coffee diffused through the room. (咖啡的香气在房间里弥漫开来。)
- in**fus**e /ˌɪnfˈjuz/ = in (入) + fus (倒) + e → 注入/灌输（=fill with）：The teacher infused enthusiasm into her students. (老师向学生灌输了热情。)
- **fus**e /fjuz/ = fus (倒/融) + e → 保险丝（=safety wire）/融合（=joining）：The fuse blew out during the storm. (暴风雨中保险丝烧断了。)
- **fus**ion /fˈjuʒən/ = fus (倒/融) + ion (名词后缀) → 融合（=joining）：Jazz fusion combines different musical styles. (融合爵士结合了不同的音乐风格。)


**clud/claus=shut 关闭**: 

- in**clud**e /ˌɪnˈklud/ = in (入) + clud (关闭) + e → 包括/包含：The price includes tax and service charge. (价格包含税费和服务费。)
- in**clus**ive /ˌɪnˈklusɪv/ = in (入) + clus (关闭) + ive (形容词后缀) → 包括的：The price is inclusive of all meals. (价格已包含所有餐食。)
- ex**clud**e /ɪkˈsklud/ = ex (出) + clud (关闭) + e → 排除/排斥（=keep out）：Children are excluded from this event. (儿童被排除在此活动之外。)
- ex**clus**ive /ɪkˈsklusɪv/ = ex (出) + clus (关闭) + ive (形容词后缀) → 排外的/专属的（=only）：This is an exclusive interview with the star. (这是对这位明星的独家专访。)
- con**clud**e /kənˈklud/ = con (一起) + clud (关闭) + e → 总结/结束（=finish）：Let me conclude my speech with a quote. (让我用一句名言结束我的演讲。)
- con**clus**ion /kənˈkluʒən/ = con (一起) + clus (关闭) + ion (名词后缀) → 结论（=final thought）：We came to the same conclusion. (我们得出了相同的结论。)
- **clos**e /kloʊz/ = clos (关闭) + e → 关闭/结束：Please close the door behind you. (请随手关门。)
- **disclos**e /dɪˈskloʊz/ = dis (否定/相反) + clos (关闭) + e → 揭露/透露（=reveal）：He refused to disclose his source. (他拒绝透露消息来源。)
- en**clos**ure /ɪnˈkloʊʒər/ = en (使) + clos (关闭) + ure (名词后缀) → 围场/附件（=enclosed area）：The animals are kept in a large enclosure. (动物被关在一个大围场里。)


**volv/volut=roll/turn 卷/转**: 

- in**volv**e /ˌɪnˈvɑlv/ = in (入) + volv (卷) + e → 涉及/卷入（=include）：Don't involve me in your argument. (别把我卷入你们的争论中。)
- in**volv**ement /ˌɪnˈvɑlvmənt/ = in (入) + volv (卷) + e + ment (名词后缀) → 参与/卷入（=taking part）：His involvement in the project is crucial. (他对项目的参与至关重要。)
- e**volv**e /ɪˈvɑlv/ = e (出) + volv (卷/转) + e → 进化/演变（=development）：Species evolve over millions of years. (物种经过数百万年进化。)
- e**volut**ion /ˌɛvəˈluʃən/ = e (出) + volut (卷/转) + ion (名词后缀) → 进化/演变（=development）：Darwin's theory of evolution changed science. (达尔文的进化论改变了科学。)
- re**volut**ion /ˌrɛvəˈluʃən/ = re (回/反复) + volut (转) + ion (名词后缀) → 革命（=big change）/旋转（=spin）：The Industrial Revolution transformed society. (工业革命改变了社会。)
- re**volv**e /riˈvɑlv/ = re (回/反复) + volv (转) + e → 旋转（=spinning）/围绕（=circle）：The Earth revolves around the Sun. (地球围绕太阳旋转。)
- **volu**me /ˈvɑljum/ = vol (卷) + ume (名词后缀) → 卷（=book part）/音量（=loudness）/体积（=size）：Please turn down the volume of the TV. (请把电视音量调低。)
- re**volt** /rɪˈvoʊlt/ = re (回/反对) + volt (转) → 反叛/反抗（=rise up）：The citizens revolted against the dictator. (市民反抗独裁者。)


**cumb/cub=lie down 躺**: 

- in**cub**ate /ˈɪnkjəˌbeɪt/ = in (入) + cub (躺) + ate (动词后缀) → 孵化/培育（=hatch）：The eggs need to incubate for three weeks. (这些蛋需要孵化三周。)
- in**cumb**ent /ˌɪnˈkəmbənt/ = in (在…上) + cumb (躺) + ent (形容词后缀) → 现任的/在职的（=current）：The incumbent president won the election. (现任总统赢得了选举。)
- suc**cumb** /səˈkəm/ = suc (在下) + cumb (躺) → 屈服/死于（=give in）：He finally succumbed to the illness. (他最终死于疾病。)



**pract=do 做**: 

- **pract**ice /ˈpræktɪs/ = pract (做) + ice (名词后缀) → 实践/练习：Practice makes perfect. (熟能生巧。)
- **pract**ical /ˈpræktɪkəl/ = pract (做) + ical (形容词后缀) → 实践的/实用的（=useful）：We need a practical solution to this problem. (我们需要一个解决这个问题的实际方案。)
- **pract**ically /ˈpræktɪkəli/ = pract (做) + ical + ly (副词后缀) → 几乎/实际地（=almost）：It's practically impossible to finish today. (今天完成几乎不可能。)



**oper=work 工作**: 

- **oper**ate /ˈɔpərˌeɪt/ = oper (工作) + ate (动词后缀) → 操作（=running）/手术（=medical procedure）：Can you show me how to operate this machine? (你能教我如何操作这台机器吗？)
- **oper**ation /ˌɑpərˈeɪʃən/ = oper (工作) + ation (名词后缀) → 操作（=running）/手术（=medical procedure）：The operation was successful. (手术很成功。)
- **oper**ator /ˈɑpərˌeɪtər/ = oper (工作) + ator (人) → 操作员/接线员：Press zero to speak to an operator. (按零联系接线员。)
- **oper**a /ˈɑprə/ = oper (工作/作品) + a → 歌剧：They went to the opera last night. (他们昨晚去看了歌剧。)
- co**oper**ate /kˈwɑpərˌeɪt/ = co (共同) + oper (工作) + ate (动词后缀) → 合作（=working together）：The two companies decided to cooperate. (两家公司决定合作。)
- co**oper**ation /kˌwɔpərˈeɪʃən/ = co (共同) + oper (工作) + ation (名词后缀) → 合作（=working together）：International cooperation is needed to solve this problem. (解决这个问题需要国际合作。)
- co**oper**ative /koʊˈɑpərˌeɪtɪv/ = co (共同) + oper (工作) + ative (形容词后缀) → 合作（=working together）的：The children were very cooperative during the trip. (孩子们在旅途中非常配合。)


**orn=decorate 装饰**: 

- **orn**ament /ˈɔrnəmənt/ = orn (装饰) + ament (名词后缀) → 装饰/装饰品（=decoration）：She hung colorful ornaments on the Christmas tree. (她在圣诞树上挂上了五彩缤纷的装饰品。)
- **orn**amental /ˌɔrnəˈmɛntəl/ = orn (装饰) + ament + al (形容词后缀) → 装饰性的（=decorative）：The garden has ornamental plants along the path. (花园沿路种了观赏植物。)



**fend/fens=strike 打击**: 

- de**fend** /dɪˈfɛnd/ = de (离开/避开) + fend (打击) → 防御/辩护（=protection）：The soldiers defended the city bravely. (士兵们勇敢地保卫了城市。)
- de**fens**e /dɪˈfɛns/ = de (离开/避开) + fens (打击) + e → 防御/辩护（=protection）：The lawyer presented a strong defense. (律师提出了强有力的辩护。)
- de**fend**ant /dɪˈfɛndənt/ = de (离开/避开) + fend (打击) + ant (人) → 被告（=accused person）：The defendant pleaded not guilty. (被告辩称无罪。)
- of**fend** /əˈfɛnd/ = of (对着) + fend (打击) → 冒犯/得罪（=upset）：I hope I didn't offend you with my words. (希望我的话没有冒犯到你。)
- of**fens**e /əˈfɛns/ = of (对着) + fens (打击) + e → 冒犯（=insult）/进攻（=attack）：His remark was a serious offense. (他的言论是严重的冒犯。)
- of**fens**ive /əˈfɛnsɪv/ = of (对着) + fens (打击) + ive (形容词后缀) → 冒犯的（=insulting）/进攻的（=attacking）：That joke was offensive to many people. (那个笑话冒犯了很多人。)
- **fenc**e /fɛns/ = fenc (打击/防御) + e → 篱笆/击剑：They built a fence around the garden. (他们在花园周围建了篱笆。)


**junct=join 连接**: 

- **junct**ion /ˈʤəŋkʃən/ = junct (连接) + ion (名词后缀) → 连接/枢纽/交叉口（=joining point）：Turn left at the next junction. (在下一个路口左转。)
- con**junct**ion /kənˈʤəŋkʃən/ = con (一起) + junct (连接) + ion (名词后缀) → 连词/结合（=connecting word）：The word "and" is a conjunction. ("and"这个词是连词。)



**lav/lut=wash 洗**: 

- **lav**atory /ˈlævəˌtɔri/ = lav (洗) + atory (场所) → 洗手间：Excuse me, where is the lavatory? (请问洗手间在哪里？)
- **laund**ry /ˈlɔndri/ = laund (洗) + ry (场所) → 洗衣房/待洗衣物：I need to do the laundry today. (我今天需要洗衣服。)
- di**lut**e /dɪˈlut/ = di (分开) + lut (洗) + e → 稀释/冲淡（=water down）：Dilute the juice with water before drinking. (喝之前用水稀释果汁。)
- pol**lut**e /pəˈlut/ = pol (完全) + lut (洗/弄脏) + e → 污染（=dirtiness）：Cars pollute the air in big cities. (汽车污染大城市的空气。)
- pol**lut**ion /pəˈluʃən/ = pol (完全) + lut (洗/弄脏) + ion (名词后缀) → 污染（=dirtiness）：Air pollution is a serious problem. (空气污染是严重的问题。)
- pol**lut**ant /pəˈlutənt/ = pol (完全) + lut (洗/弄脏) + ant (物) → 污染（=dirtiness）物：Factories release pollutants into the river. (工厂向河流中排放污染物。)


**par=bring forth 生产**: 

- **par**ent /ˈpɛrənt/ = par (生产) + ent (人) → 父母/家长：My parents always support my decisions. (我的父母总是支持我的决定。)
- ap**par**ent /əˈpɛrənt/ = ap (向) + par (显现) + ent (形容词后缀) → 明显的（=clear）/表面上的（=seeming）：It soon became apparent that he was lying. (很快就明显看出他在撒谎。)
- ap**par**ently /əˈpɛrəntli/ = ap (向) + par (显现) + ent + ly (副词后缀) → 显然/表面上（=seemingly）：Apparently, she didn't receive the message. (显然，她没有收到信息。)
- trans**par**ent /trænˈspɛrənt/ = trans (穿过) + par (显现) + ent (形容词后缀) → 透明的（=see-through）：Glass is transparent. (玻璃是透明的。)
- trans**par**ency /trænˈspɛrənsi/ = trans (穿过) + par (显现) + ency (名词后缀) → 透明/透明度（=clarity）：The government promised greater transparency. (政府承诺更大的透明度。)

**flect/flex=bend 弯曲**:

- re**flect** /rɪˈflɛkt/ = re (回) + flect (弯曲) → 反射（=mirror）/反映/思考：The mirror reflects the light.
- re**flect**ion /rɪˈflɛkʃən/ = re (回) + flect (弯曲) + ion (名词后缀) → 反射/映像/思考（=mirror image）：I saw my reflection in the water.
- **flex**ible /ˈflɛksəbəl/ = flex (弯曲) + ible (可……的) → 灵活的/易弯曲的（=bendable）：Rubber is a flexible material.
- **flex**ibility /ˌflɛksəˈbɪləti/ = flex (弯曲) + ibility (名词后缀) → 灵活性（=adaptability）：Yoga improves your flexibility.
- de**flect** /dɪˈflɛkt/ = de (离开) + flect (弯曲) → 使偏斜/转移（=turn away）：The shield deflected the arrow.
- in**flect**ion /ˌɪnˈflɛkʃən/ = in (入) + flect (弯曲) + ion (名词后缀) → 弯曲/音调变化：Her voice had a rising inflection at the end.

#### 状态变化


★**rupt=break 破/断裂**: 

- dis**rupt** /dɪsˈrəpt/ = dis (分开) + rupt (破) → 扰乱（=break up）：The loud noise disrupted the meeting. (巨大的噪音扰乱了会议。)
- e**rupt** /ˈirəpt/ = e (出) + rupt (破) → 爆发（=burst out）：The volcano erupted after centuries of silence. (火山在沉寂数个世纪后爆发了。)
- inter**rupt** /ˌɪntərˈəpt/ = inter (之间) + rupt (破) → 打断（=cut in）：Please don't interrupt me while I'm speaking. (我说话时请不要打断我。)
- bank**rupt** /ˈbæŋkrəpt/ = bank (银行) + rupt (破) → 破产的（=money-broken）：The company went bankrupt due to poor management. (那家公司因管理不善而破产了。)
- ab**rupt** /əˈbrəpt/ = ab (离开) + rupt (破) → 突然的（=sudden）：The meeting came to an abrupt end. (会议突然结束了。)
- cor**rupt**ion /kərˈəpʃən/ = cor (一起) + rupt (破) + ion (名词后缀) → 腐败（=dishonesty）：The government promised to fight corruption. (政府承诺打击腐败。)
- cor**rupt** /kərəpt/ = cor (一起) + rupt (破) → 腐败（=dishonesty）的：He was accused of accepting corrupt payments. (他被指控收受腐败款项。)

**frag/fract=break 破/碎**:

- **frag**ile /ˈfræʤəl/ = frag (破/碎) + ile (容易……的) → 易碎的（=easily broken）：Please handle the glass carefully; it's very fragile.
- **frag**ment /ˈfrægmənt/ = frag (破/碎) + ment (名词后缀) → 碎片/片段（=piece）：The mirror fell and broke into fragments.
- **fract**ure /ˈfrækʧər/ = fract (破) + ure (名词后缀) → 骨折/断裂（=break）：He suffered a leg fracture in the accident.
- **fract**ion /ˈfrækʃən/ = fract (破) + ion (名词后缀) → 分数/小部分（=part）：Only a small fraction of the population lives there.
- **fract**ion**al** /ˈfrækʃənəl/ = fract (破) + ion + al (形容词后缀) → 极小的/分数的（=tiny）：There was a fractional difference between the two measurements.
- **fring**e /frɪnʤ/ = fring (破/边) + e → 边缘/刘海（=edge）：The village lies on the fringe of the city.


★**flu=flow 流**: 

- **flu**ent /fluənt/ = flu (流) + ent (形容词后缀) → 流利的：She speaks fluent French after living in Paris for five years. (她在巴黎住了五年后说法语很流利。)
- **flu**ency /ˈfluənsi/ = flu (流) + ency (名词后缀) → 流利：He achieved fluency in Japanese within two years. (他在两年内达到了日语流利的程度。)
- in**flu**ence /ˈɪnfluəns/ = in (入) + flu (流) + ence (名词后缀) → 影响（=effect）：Her parents had a great influence on her career choice. (她的父母对她的职业选择有很大影响。)
- in**flu**ential /ˌɪnfluˈɛnʃəl/ = in (入) + flu (流) + ent + ial (形容词后缀) → 有影响力的（=powerful）：He is one of the most influential scientists of our time. (他是我们这个时代最有影响力的科学家之一。)
- **flu**id /fluɪd/ = flu (流) + id (形容词后缀) → 流体（=liquid）/流畅的（=smooth）：The dancer's movements were fluid and graceful. (舞者的动作流畅而优美。)
- **flu**ctuate /ˈfləkʧəˌweɪt/ = flu (流) + ctuate (动词后缀) → 波动（=go up and down）：Stock prices fluctuate daily based on market conditions. (股票价格根据市场状况每日波动。)
- af**flu**ent /ˈæfluənt/ = af (向) + flu (流) + ent (形容词后缀) → 富裕的（=wealthy）：He grew up in an affluent neighborhood. (他在一个富裕的社区长大。)
- **flu**sh /fləʃ/ = flu (流) + sh → 冲洗（=wash out）：Please flush the toilet after use. (使用后请冲洗马桶。)
- **flu**x /fləks/ = flu (流) + x → 流量/不断变化（=change）：The project is in a state of flux right now. (这个项目目前处于不断变化的状态。)


★**solv/solu/solut=loosen 放松/解决**: 

- **solv**e /sɑlv/ = solv (解开) + e → 解决（=figure out）：We need to solve this problem as soon as possible. (我们需要尽快解决这个问题。)
- **solu**tion /səˈluʃən/ = solu (解开) + tion (名词后缀) → 溶液（=liquid mix）/解决方案（=answer）：The scientists are working on a solution to the energy crisis. (科学家们正在研究能源危机的解决方案。)
- re**solv**e /riˈzɑlv/ = re (再) + solv (解开) + e → 解决（=figure out）/决心：She resolved to study harder for the final exam. (她下定决心为期终考试更加努力学习。)
- re**solu**tion /ˌrɛzəˈluʃən/ = re (再) + solu (解开) + tion (名词后缀) → 决心（=determination）/决议（=formal decision）：The UN passed a resolution calling for peace. (联合国通过了一项呼吁和平的决议。)
- dis**solv**e /dɪˈzɑlv/ = dis (分开) + solv (解开) + e → 溶解（=melt）/解散（=break up）：Sugar dissolves quickly in hot water. (糖在热水中溶解得很快。)
- ab**solu**te /ˈæbsəˌlut/ = ab (离开) + solu (解开) + te → 绝对的（=total）：You have my absolute trust and support. (你有我绝对的信任和支持。)
- ab**solu**tely /ˌæbsəˈlutli/ = ab (离开) + solu (解开) + te + ly (副词后缀) → 绝对地（=totally）：I absolutely agree with your opinion. (我绝对同意你的意见。)
- **solu**ble /ˈsɑljəbəl/ = solu (解开) + ble (可……的) → 可溶的（=can dissolve）：This vitamin is water-soluble. (这种维生素是水溶性的。)


★**val/vail=be worth 有价值**: 

- **val**ue /ˈvælju/ = val (价值) + ue → 价值：The value of education cannot be overstated. (教育的价值怎么强调都不为过。)
- **val**uable /ˈvæljəbəl/ = val (价值) + uable (可……的) → 有价值的：She gave me some valuable advice on my career. (她给了我一些关于职业的宝贵建议。)
- e**val**uate /ɪˈvæljuˌeɪt/ = e (出) + val (价值) + uate (动词后缀) → 评估（=judge）：The teacher will evaluate students based on their performance. (老师将根据表现评估学生。)
- **val**id /ˈvælɪd/ = val (价值/力量) + id (形容词后缀) → 有效的（=working）：Your passport must be valid for at least six months. (你的护照必须至少有六个月的有效期。)
- in**val**id /ˌɪnˈvæləd/ = in (不) + val (价值) + id (形容词后缀) → 无效的（=not working）：The ticket is invalid because it has expired. (这张票因过期而无效。)
- equi**val**ent /ɪkˈwɪvələnt/ = equi (相等) + val (价值) + ent (形容词后缀) → 等价的（=same as）：One mile is equivalent to about 1.6 kilometers. (一英里大约相当于1.6公里。)
- a**vail**able /əˈveɪləbəl/ = a (向) + vail (有价值) + able (可……的) → 可用的（=ready to use）：Is this seat available or is it taken? (这个座位空着还是有人坐？)
- a**vail**ability /əˌveɪləˈbɪlɪti/ = a (向) + vail (有价值) + ability (名词后缀) → 可用性（=readiness）：The availability of clean water is a global concern. (清洁水的可用性是一个全球关注的问题。)
- pre**vail** /prɪˈveɪl/ = pre (前) + vail (有价值/力量) → 盛行（=win out）：Justice will prevail in the end. (正义终将获胜。)
- pre**val**ent /ˈprɛvələnt/ = pre (前) + val (有价值/力量) + ent (形容词后缀) → 普遍的（=widespread）：Smartphones are prevalent in modern society. (智能手机在现代社会中很普遍。)


★**fin=end/limit 结束/界限**: 

- **fin**ish /ˈfɪnɪʃ/ = fin (结束) + ish (动词后缀) → 完成（=finishing）：I need to finish this report before the deadline. (我需要在截止日期前完成这份报告。)
- **fin**al /ˈfaɪnəl/ = fin (结束) + al (形容词后缀) → 最终的：This is your final chance to change your mind. (这是你改变主意的最后机会。)
- **fin**ally /ˈfaɪnəli/ = fin (结束) + al + ly (副词后缀) → 最终：After hours of waiting, the bus finally arrived. (等待数小时后，公交车终于到了。)
- de**fin**e /dɪˈfaɪn/ = de (完全) + fin (界限) + e → 定义（=explanation）：Can you define the word "freedom" in your own words? (你能用自己的话来定义"自由"这个词吗？)
- de**fin**ition /ˌdɛfəˈnɪʃən/ = de (完全) + fin (界限) + ition (名词后缀) → 定义（=explanation）：The dictionary gives a clear definition of each word. (字典给出了每个词的清晰定义。)
- de**fin**ite /ˈdɛfənət/ = de (完全) + fin (界限) + ite (形容词后缀) → 明确的（=clear）：We need a definite answer by tomorrow. (我们需要在明天之前得到明确答复。)
- de**fin**itely /ˈdɛfənətli/ = de (完全) + fin (界限) + ite + ly (副词后缀) → 明确地（=clearly）：I will definitely attend your wedding. (我一定会参加你的婚礼。)
- in**fin**ite /ˈɪnfənət/ = in (不) + fin (界限) + ite (形容词后缀) → 无限的（=endless）：The universe seems to be infinite in size. (宇宙在大小上似乎是无限的。)
- in**fin**ity /ˌɪnˈfɪnɪti/ = in (不) + fin (界限) + ity (名词后缀) → 无限（=endlessness）：The concept of infinity is hard to grasp. (无限的概念很难理解。)
- **fin**ance /ˈfaɪˌnæns/ = fin (结束/结算) + ance (名词后缀) → 金融（=money matters）：He works in the finance department of a large company. (他在一家大公司的财务部门工作。)
- **fin**ancial /ˌfaɪˈnænʃəl/ = fin (结束/结算) + ancial (形容词后缀) → 金融（=money matters）的：The company is facing serious financial difficulties. (公司正面临严重的财务困难。)
- con**fin**e /kənˈfaɪn/ = con (一起) + fin (界限) + e → 限制（=limit）：Please confine your remarks to the topic at hand. (请将你的发言限制在当前话题范围内。)
- re**fin**e /rɪˈfaɪn/ = re (再) + fin (界限) + e → 精炼（=purify）：Oil must be refined before it can be used as fuel. (石油必须经过精炼才能用作燃料。)
- **fin**ite /ˈfaɪˌnaɪt/ = fin (界限) + ite (形容词后缀) → 有限的（=limited）：The Earth's natural resources are finite. (地球的自然资源是有限的。)


★**string/strict=draw tight 拉紧**: 

- **strict** /strɪkt/ = strict (拉紧) → 严格的（=tight）：The school has strict rules about uniforms. (学校对着装有严格的规定。)
- re**strict** /riˈstrɪkt/ = re (回) + strict (拉紧) → 限制（=limit）：The new law restricts the sale of alcohol to minors. (新法律限制向未成年人出售酒类。)
- re**strict**ion /riˈstrɪkʃən/ = re (回) + strict (拉紧) + ion (名词后缀) → 限制（=limit）：There are no restrictions on the number of entries. (参赛数量没有限制。)
- di**strict** /ˈdɪstrɪkt/ = di (分开) + strict (拉紧/划分) → 区域（=area）：She lives in the business district of the city. (她住在城市的商业区。)
- con**strain** /kənˈstreɪn/ = con (一起) + strain (拉紧) → 约束（=hold back）：Budget constraints forced us to cancel the project. (预算约束迫使我们取消了项目。)
- **string** /strɪŋ/ = string (拉紧的线) → 细绳（=thin rope）：She tied the package with a piece of string. (她用一根细绳捆扎了包裹。)
- **straight** /streɪt/ = straight (拉直的) → 直的：Draw a straight line from point A to point B. (从A点到B点画一条直线。)
- **straight**en /ˈstreɪtən/ = straight (直的) + en (动词后缀) → 弄直：Can you help me straighten this bent wire? (你能帮我把这根弯的铁丝弄直吗？)
- **strain** /streɪn/ = strain (拉紧) → 拉紧/压力（=stress）：Working long hours puts a strain on your health. (长时间工作会给健康带来压力。)
- re**strain** /riˈstreɪn/ = re (回) + strain (拉紧) → 克制（=holding back）：I had to restrain myself from laughing out loud. (我不得不克制自己不笑出声来。)
- re**straint** /rɪˈstreɪnt/ = re (回) + straint (拉紧) → 克制（=holding back）：She showed remarkable restraint in the argument. (她在争论中表现出了非凡的克制。)


★**cern/cert/cret=separate 区分**: 

- con**cern** /kənˈsərn/ = con (一起) + cern (区分/筛选) → 关心/涉及（=worry about）：Environmental protection concerns all of us. (环境保护关系到我们所有人。)
- con**cern**ing /kənˈsərnɪŋ/ = con (一起) + cern (区分) + ing → 关于（=about）：I received a letter concerning the job application. (我收到了一封关于求职申请的信。)
- **cert**ain /ˈsərtən/ = cert (区分/确定) + ain (形容词后缀) → 确定的（=sure）：I am certain that he will arrive on time. (我确定他会准时到达。)
- **cert**ainly /ˈsərtənli/ = cert (区分/确定) + ain + ly (副词后缀) → 当然（=of course）：Can you help me? Certainly! (你能帮我吗？当然！)
- **cert**ainty /ˈsərtənti/ = cert (区分/确定) + ainty (名词后缀) → 确定（=sureness）：We can say with certainty that the project will succeed. (我们可以确定地说这个项目会成功。)
- **cert**ificate /sərˈtɪfɪkət/ = cert (区分/确定) + ific (做) + ate (名词后缀) → 证书（=proof paper）：She received a certificate for completing the training. (她获得了完成培训的证书。)
- **cert**ify /ˈsərtəˌfaɪ/ = cert (区分/确定) + ify (动词后缀) → 证明（=confirm）：The document needs to be certified by a notary. (这份文件需要公证人证明。)
- as**cert**ain /ˌæsərˈteɪn/ = as (向) + cert (区分/确定) + ain → 查明（=find out）：The police are trying to ascertain the cause of the fire. (警方正在努力查明火灾原因。)
- dis**cern** /dɪˈsərn/ = dis (分开) + cern (区分) → 辨别（=tell apart）：It's difficult to discern the truth from the rumors. (很难从谣言中辨别真相。)
- dis**creet** /dɪˈskrit/ = dis (分开) + creet (区分) → 谨慎的（=careful）：She was very discreet about her personal life. (她对个人生活非常谨慎。)
- se**cret** /ˈsikrɪt/ = se (分开) + cret (区分) → 秘密（=hidden thing）：Can you keep a secret? (你能保守秘密吗？)
- se**cret**ary /ˈsɛkrəˌtɛri/ = se (分开) + cret (区分) + ary (人) → 秘书（=assistant）：The secretary arranged the meeting for the boss. (秘书为老板安排了会议。)


**surg/surrect=rise 升**: 

- **surg**e /sərʤ/ = surg (升) + e → 汹涌（=rush）：There was a surge of excitement in the crowd. (人群中涌起一阵兴奋。)
- **surg**eon /ˈsərʤɪn/ = surg (手) + eon (人) → 外科医生（=operation doctor）：The surgeon performed a complex heart operation. (外科医生进行了一台复杂的心脏手术。)
- **surg**ery /ˈsərʤəri/ = surg (手) + ery (名词后缀) → 外科手术（=operation）：He is recovering well after the surgery. (手术后他恢复得很好。)
- in**surg**ent /ˌɪnˈsərʤənt/ = in (入) + surg (升) + ent (形容词后缀) → 起义的（=rebellious）：The insurgent forces took control of the region. (起义军控制了该地区。)
- re**surrect** /ˌrɛzərˈɛkt/ = re (再) + surrect (升起) → 复活（=bring back）：The artist's old songs were resurrected by a new generation. (这位艺术家的老歌被新一代人重新发掘。)
- **sourc**e /sɔrs/ = sourc (升起/涌出) + e → 来源（=origin）：We need to find the source of the problem. (我们需要找到问题的来源。)
- re**sourc**e /ˈrisɔrs/ = re (再) + source (来源) → 资源（=supply）：Water is a precious natural resource. (水是宝贵的自然资源。)


**merg/mers=dip/sink 沉/浸**: 

- **merg**e /mərʤ/ = merg (沉/浸) + e → 合并/融合（=join）：The two companies decided to merge next year. (两家公司决定明年合并。)
- e**merg**e /ˈimərʤ/ = e (出) + merg (沉) + e → 浮现（=come out）：New evidence emerged during the investigation. (调查过程中浮现出新证据。)
- e**merg**ence /ˈimərʤəns/ = e (出) + merg (沉) + ence (名词后缀) → 浮现（=come out）：The emergence of social media changed communication. (社交媒体的出现改变了交流方式。)
- e**merg**ency /ˈimərʤənsi/ = e (出) + merg (沉) + ency (名词后缀) → 紧急情况（=emergency）：Call 911 only in case of an emergency. (仅在紧急情况下拨打911。)
- im**mers**e /ˌɪˈmərs/ = im (入) + mers (沉) + e → 沉浸/浸没（=deeply involve）：She immersed herself in the novel for hours. (她沉浸在那本小说中好几个小时。)
- sub**merg**e /səbˈmərʤ/ = sub (下) + merg (沉) + e → 淹没（=flood）：The village was submerged by the flood. (村庄被洪水淹没了。)


**plen/plete=fill 满**: 

- **plen**ty /ˈplɛnti/ = plen (满) + ty (名词后缀) → 丰富（=plenty）：There's plenty of food for everyone at the party. (派对上有足够的食物给大家。)
- **plen**tiful /ˈplɛnɪfəl/ = plen (满) + ti + ful (形容词后缀) → 丰富的（=plentiful）：Fresh fruit is plentiful in the summer months. (夏季新鲜水果很丰富。)
- com**plete** /kəmˈplit/ = com (一起) + plete (满) → 完成/完整的（=finish）：Please complete the form and return it to us. (请填写表格并交还给我们。)
- com**plet**ion /kəmˈpliʃən/ = com (一起) + plet (满) + ion (名词后缀) → 完成（=finishing）：The project is nearing completion. (项目接近完成。)
- com**plete**ly /kəmˈplitli/ = com (一起) + plete (满) + ly (副词后缀) → 完全地（=totally）：I completely forgot about the meeting. (我完全忘记了会议。)
- com**ple**ment /ˈkɑmpləmənt/ = com (一起) + ple (满) + ment (名词后缀) → 补充/补足（=add to）：The wine is a perfect complement to the meal. (这款酒是这顿饭的完美搭配。)
- **imple**ment /ˈɪmpləmənt/ = im (入) + ple (满) + ment → 实施（=carry out）/工具（=tool）：The company plans to implement new safety measures. (公司计划实施新的安全措施。)
- sup**ple**ment /ˌsəpləˈmɛnt/ = sup (下/补充) + ple (满) + ment (名词后缀) → 补充/增刊（=add-on）：She takes vitamin supplements every morning. (她每天早上服用维生素补充剂。)
- de**plete** /dɪˈplit/ = de (否定/去除) + plete (满) → 耗尽（=use up）：Overfishing has depleted the ocean's resources. (过度捕捞已经耗尽了海洋资源。)


**prob/prov=test/prove 测试/证明**: 

- **prov**e /pruv/ = prov (证明) + e → 证明（=confirm）：The evidence proved his innocence beyond doubt. (证据毫无疑问地证明了他的清白。)
- **proof** /pruf/ = proof (证明) → 证据（=proof）：Do you have any proof of what you're saying? (你有你说的话的证据吗？)
- ap**prov**e /əˈpruv/ = ap (向) + prov (证明) + e → 批准/赞同（=say yes）：The committee approved the budget for next year. (委员会批准了明年的预算。)
- ap**prov**al /əˈpruvəl/ = ap (向) + prov (证明) + al (名词后缀) → 批准（=okay）：The plan needs the manager's approval before we proceed. (计划需要经理批准才能继续。)
- disap**prov**e /ˌdɪsəˈpruv/ = dis (不) + ap (向) + prov (证明) + e → 不赞成（=disagreement）：Her parents disapprove of her decision to drop out. (她的父母不赞成她辍学的决定。)
- disap**prov**al /dɪsəˈpruvəl/ = dis (不) + ap (向) + prov (证明) + al (名词后缀) → 不赞成（=disagreement）：He shook his head in disapproval. (他摇头表示不赞成。)
- im**prov**e /ˌɪmˈpruv/ = im (入/加强) + prov (证明/好) + e → 改善/提高（=make better）：Reading can help improve your vocabulary. (阅读有助于提高词汇量。)

#### 位置与姿势


★**sed/sid/sess=sit 坐**: 

- as**sess** /əˈsɛs/ = as (向) + sess (坐) → 评估（=judge）/评定：The teacher will assess each student's progress at the end of the term. (老师将在学期末评估每个学生的进步。)
- as**sess**ment /əˈsɛsmənt/ = as (向) + sess (坐) + ment (名词后缀) → 评估（=judge）：The company conducted an environmental assessment. (公司进行了一次环境评估。)
