- pos**sess**ion /pəˈzɛʃən/ = pos (放置) + sess (坐) + ion (名词后缀) → 拥有/财产（=ownership）：The ring is her most treasured possession. (那枚戒指是她最珍视的财产。)
- ob**sess** /əbˈsɛs/ = ob (对着) + sess (坐) → 使着迷/困扰（=haunt）：He is obsessed with video games. (他对电子游戏着迷了。)
- ob**sess**ion /əbˈsɛʃən/ = ob (对着) + sess (坐) + ion (名词后缀) → 着迷（=fixation）：Her obsession with cleanliness drives her family crazy. (她对清洁的痴迷让家人抓狂。)
- pre**sid**e /prɪˈzaɪd/ = pre (前) + sid (坐) + e → 主持（=lead）：The mayor will preside over the opening ceremony. (市长将主持开幕式。)
- pre**sid**ent /ˈprɛzɪdənt/ = pre (前) + sid (坐) + ent (人) → 总统/主席（=leader）：The president gave a speech to the nation. (总统向全国发表了演讲。)
- re**sid**e /rɪˈzaɪd/ = re (回) + sid (坐) + e → 居住（=live）：He resides in a small town near the mountains. (他居住在山边的一个小镇上。)
- re**sid**ence /ˈrɛzɪdəns/ = re (回) + sid (坐) + ence (名词后缀) → 居住（=live）/住所：The ambassador's official residence is located downtown. (大使的官邸位于市中心。)
- re**sid**ent /ˈrɛzɪdənt/ = re (回) + sid (坐) + ent (人) → 居民/住院医生（=dweller）：All residents of the building were evacuated safely. (楼内所有居民都安全撤离了。)
- sub**sid**y /ˈsəbsɪdi/ = sub (下) + sid (坐) + y (名词后缀) → 补贴/补助金（=financial aid）：The government provides subsidies to farmers. (政府向农民提供补贴。)
- con**sid**er /kənˈsɪdər/ = con (一起) + sid (坐) + er → 考虑（=think about）：Please consider my suggestion before making a decision. (做决定前请考虑我的建议。)
- con**sid**eration /kənˌsɪdərˈeɪʃən/ = con (一起) + sid (坐) + er + ation (名词后缀) → 考虑（=think about）/体谅：Thank you for your consideration and kindness. (感谢你的体谅和善意。)
- con**sid**erable /kənˈsɪdərəbəl/ = con (一起) + sid (坐) + er + able (形容词后缀) → 相当大的（=big）：The project required a considerable amount of time and effort. (这个项目需要相当多的时间和精力。)
- con**sid**erate /kənˈsɪdərət/ = con (一起) + sid (坐) + er + ate (形容词后缀) → 体贴的（=thoughtful）：She is always considerate of others' feelings. (她总是体贴他人的感受。)
- **sess**ion /ˈsɛʃən/ = sess (坐) + ion (名词后缀) → 会议/学期（=meeting）：The summer session starts in July. (暑期学期从七月开始。)


**st/still/stit=stand 站立**: 

- **st**able /ˈsteɪbəl/ = st (站立) + able (可……的) → 稳定的（=steady）/马厩（=horse house）：The economy is now relatively stable. (经济现在相对稳定。)
- **st**ability /stəˈbɪlɪti/ = st (站立) + ability (名词后缀) → 稳定性（=steadiness）：Political stability is essential for economic growth. (政治稳定对经济增长至关重要。)
- e**st**ablish /ɪˈstæblɪʃ/ = e (出) + st (站立) + abl (能) + ish (动词后缀) → 建立/设立（=set up）：They plan to establish a new branch office in Tokyo. (他们计划在东京设立新的分公司。)
- e**st**ablishment /ɪˈstæblɪʃmənt/ = e (出) + st (站立) + abl + ish + ment (名词后缀) → 建立/机构（=organization）：The hotel is a well-known establishment in the city. (这家酒店是城里知名的机构。)
- **st**age /steɪʤ/ = st (站立) + age (名词后缀) → 舞台/阶段（=phase）：The project is still in its early stages. (项目仍处于早期阶段。)
- **st**agnant /ˈstægnənt/ = stagn (站立/不动) + ant (形容词后缀) → 停滞的（=not moving）：The stagnant water attracted mosquitoes. (停滞的水引来了蚊子。)
- **st**ationary /ˈsteɪʃəˌnɛri/ = station (站立) + ary (形容词后缀) → 固定的/静止的（=still）：The car remained stationary at the red light. (汽车在红灯处保持静止。)
- **st**ationery /ˈsteɪʃəˌnɛri/ = station (站立) + ery (名词后缀，物品) → 文具（=writing supplies）：She bought some stationery for the new school year. (她为新学年买了一些文具。)
- con**stit**ute /ˈkɑnstəˌtut/ = con (一起) + stit (站立) + ute → 构成/建立/任命（=make up）：Twelve members constitute the committee. (十二名成员构成了这个委员会。)
- con**stit**ution /ˌkɑnstəˈtuʃən/ = con (一起) + stit (站立) + ution (名词后缀) → 宪法/构成/体质（=basic law）：The constitution guarantees freedom of speech. (宪法保障言论自由。)
- in**stit**ute /ˈɪnstɪˌtut/ = in (入) + stit (站立) + ute → 学院/机构（=school）：She works at a research institute. (她在一家研究所工作。)
- in**stit**ution /ˌɪnstɪˈtuʃən/ = in (入) + stit (站立) + ution (名词后缀) → 机构/制度（=organization）：Marriage is a sacred institution in many cultures. (婚姻在许多文化中是神圣的制度。)
- sub**stit**ute /ˈsəbstəˌtut/ = sub (下) + stit (站立) + ute → 替代品/代替（=replace）：You can substitute honey for sugar in this recipe. (在这个食谱中你可以用蜂蜜代替糖。)
- de**stit**ute /ˈdɛstəˌtut/ = de (离开) + stit (站立) + ute → 贫困的（=poor）：The charity provides food for destitute families. (慈善机构为贫困家庭提供食物。)
- con**st**ant /ˈkɑnstənt/ = con (一起) + st (站立) + ant (形容词后缀) → 不变的/经常的/常数（=unchanging）：He is in constant pain from his back injury. (他因背部受伤而持续疼痛。)
- con**st**antly /ˈkɑnstəntli/ = con (一起) + st (站立) + ant + ly (副词后缀) → 不断地（=always）：She is constantly checking her phone for messages. (她不断地查看手机消息。)
- di**st**ance /ˈdɪstəns/ = di (分开) + st (站立) + ance (名词后缀) → 距离（=space between）：The distance between the two cities is about 300 kilometers. (两个城市之间的距离大约是300公里。)
- di**st**ant /ˈdɪstənt/ = di (分开) + st (站立) + ant (形容词后缀) → 遥远的（=far）：We could hear the distant sound of thunder. (我们能听到遥远的雷声。)
- in**st**ant /ˈɪnstənt/ = in (不) + st (站立) + ant → 瞬间/立即的（=right away）：The response to our advertisement was instant. (对我们广告的反应是立即的。)
- in**st**antly /ˈɪnstəntli/ = in (不) + st (站立) + ant + ly (副词后缀) → 立即（=instantly）：She recognized him instantly despite the years. (尽管多年未见，她立刻就认出了他。)
- circum**st**ance /ˈsərkəmˌstæns/ = circum (环绕) + st (站立) + ance (名词后缀) → 环境/情况（=situation）：Under no circumstances should you open that door. (在任何情况下你都不应该打开那扇门。)
- sub**st**ance /ˈsəbstəns/ = sub (下) + st (站立) + ance (名词后缀) → 物质/实质（=material）：Water is a substance essential to all life. (水是对所有生命都至关重要的物质。)
- sub**st**antial /səbˈstænʃəl/ = sub (下) + st (站立) + ant + ial (形容词后缀) → 大量的/实质的/坚固的（=significant）：She made a substantial contribution to the project. (她对项目做出了实质性的贡献。)


**tain/ten/tent=hold 保持**: 

- con**tain** /kənˈteɪn/ = con (一起) + tain (保持) → 包含：This box contains old photographs from my childhood. (这个盒子装着我童年的旧照片。)
- con**tain**er /kənˈteɪnər/ = con (一起) + tain (保持) + er (物) → 容器（=holder）：Please put the leftovers in a sealed container. (请把剩菜放进密封容器里。)
- ob**tain** /əbˈteɪn/ = ob (靠近) + tain (保持) → 获得（=get）：You need a license to obtain this medication. (你需要处方才能获得这种药物。)
- re**tain** /rɪˈteɪn/ = re (回) + tain (保持) → 保留（=keep）：The company wants to retain its best employees. (公司想要留住最优秀的员工。)
- main**tain** /meɪnˈteɪn/ = main (手) + tain (保持) → 维持（=keep up）：It is important to maintain a healthy lifestyle. (保持健康的生活方式很重要。)
- main**ten**ance /ˈmeɪntənəns/ = main (手) + ten (保持) + ance (名词后缀) → 维护（=upkeep）：Regular maintenance keeps the machine running smoothly. (定期维护使机器平稳运行。)
- sus**tain** /səˈsteɪn/ = sus (在下) + tain (保持) → 支撑（=hold up）：The bridge cannot sustain the weight of heavy trucks. (这座桥无法承受重型卡车的重量。)
- sus**tain**able /səˈsteɪnəbəl/ = sus (在下) + tain (保持) + able (可……的) → 可持续的（=lasting）：We should use sustainable energy sources. (我们应该使用可持续能源。)
- enter**tain** /ˌɛnərˈteɪn/ = enter (之间) + tain (保持) → 娱乐（=amusement）：The magician entertained the children with tricks. (魔术师用魔术逗乐了孩子们。)
- enter**tain**ment /ˌɛnərˈteɪnmənt/ = enter (之间) + tain (保持) + ment (名词后缀) → 娱乐（=amusement）：Watching movies is a popular form of entertainment. (看电影是一种流行的娱乐形式。)
- de**tain** /dɪˈteɪn/ = de (向下) + tain (保持) → 拘留（=hold）：The police may detain suspects for up to 24 hours. (警方最多可以拘留嫌疑人24小时。)
- con**tin**ent /ˈkɑntənənt/ = con (一起) + tin (保持) + ent (名词后缀) → 大陆（=large land）：Africa is the second largest continent. (非洲是第二大大陆。)
- **ten**ant /ˈtɛnənt/ = ten (保持/持有) + ant (人) → 房客（=renter）：The tenant pays rent on the first of each month. (房客每月一号付房租。)
- **ten**nis /ˈtɛnɪs/ = ten (握/持) + nis → 网球（手掌击球）：He plays tennis every weekend with his friends. (他每周末和朋友打网球。)


**tend/tent/tens=stretch 伸展**: 

- ex**tend** /ɪkˈstɛnd/ = ex (出) + tend (伸展) → 扩展（=addition）：We plan to extend our business to overseas markets. (我们计划将业务扩展到海外市场。)
- ex**tens**ion /ɪkˈstɛnʃən/ = ex (出) + tens (伸展) + ion (名词后缀) → 扩展（=addition）：They built an extension to the house. (他们给房子建了扩建部分。)
- ex**tens**ive /ɪkˈstɛnsɪv/ = ex (出) + tens (伸展) + ive (形容词后缀) → 广泛的（=wide）：She has extensive knowledge of art history. (她有广泛的艺术史知识。)
- in**tend** /ˌɪnˈtɛnd/ = in (入) + tend (伸展) → 打算（=plan）：I intend to study abroad next year. (我打算明年出国留学。)
- in**tent**ion /ˌɪnˈtɛnʧən/ = in (入) + tent (伸展) + ion (名词后缀) → 意图（=plan）：His intention was not to hurt your feelings. (他的意图不是要伤害你的感受。)
- in**tent**ional /ˌɪnˈtɛnʃənəl/ = in (入) + tent (伸展) + ion + al (形容词后缀) → 故意的（=on purpose）：Was the mistake intentional or accidental? (这个错误是故意的还是偶然的？)
- in**tent**ionally /ˌɪnˈtɛnʃənəli/ = in (入) + tent (伸展) + ion + al + ly (副词后缀) → 故意地（=on purpose）：He intentionally ignored her calls. (他故意忽略了她的来电。)
- pre**tend** /priˈtɛnd/ = pre (前) + tend (伸展) → 假装（=fake）：Children love to pretend they are superheroes. (孩子们喜欢假装自己是超级英雄。)
- at**tend** /əˈtɛnd/ = at (向) + tend (伸展) → 参加（=go to）：Hundreds of guests attended the wedding ceremony. (数百位宾客参加了婚礼。)
- at**tend**ance /əˈtɛndəns/ = at (向) + tend (伸展) + ance (名词后缀) → 出席（=being there）：Attendance at the meeting is mandatory. (参加会议是强制性的。)
- **tens**ion /ˈtɛnʃən/ = tens (伸展/拉紧) + ion (名词后缀) → 紧张（=stress）：There was a lot of tension in the room before the exam. (考试前房间里充满了紧张气氛。)
- **tens**e /tɛns/ = tens (伸展/拉紧) + e → 紧张（=stress）的/时态：She felt tense before the interview. (面试前她感到紧张。)
- in**tens**e /ˌɪnˈtɛns/ = in (入) + tens (伸展/拉紧) + e → 强烈的（=strong）：The intense heat made it hard to work outside. (酷热使人难以在户外工作。)
- in**tens**ity /ˌɪnˈtɛnsɪti/ = in (入) + tens (伸展) + ity (名词后缀) → 强度/强烈（=strength）：The storm increased in intensity throughout the night. (暴风雨的强度整夜都在增加。)
- in**tens**ive /ˌɪnˈtɛnsɪv/ = in (入) + tens (伸展) + ive (形容词后缀) → 加强的/集中的/密集的（=focused）：She is taking an intensive English course this summer. (她今年夏天在上一门英语强化课程。)
- **tend**ency /ˈtɛndənsi/ = tend (伸展/倾向) + ency (名词后缀) → 趋势（=trend）：There is a growing tendency to shop online. (网上购物的趋势越来越明显。)


**hibit=hold 持有**: 

- ex**hibit** /ɪgˈzɪbɪt/ = ex (出) + hibit (持有) → 展览/展示（=display）：The museum will exhibit ancient artifacts from Egypt. (博物馆将展出古埃及文物。)
- ex**hibit**ion /ˌɛksəˈbɪʃən/ = ex (出) + hibit (持有) + ion (名词后缀) → 展览（=display）：We visited an art exhibition at the gallery. (我们去画廊参观了一场艺术展览。)
- in**hibit** /ˌɪnˈhɪbət/ = in (入) + hibit (持有) → 抑制（=holding back）：Fear of failure can inhibit creativity. (对失败的恐惧会抑制创造力。)
- in**hibit**ion /ˌɪnəˈbɪʃən/ = in (入) + hibit (持有) + ion (名词后缀) → 抑制（=holding back）：Alcohol can reduce a person's inhibitions. (酒精可以降低一个人的抑制力。)
- pro**hibit** /proʊˈhɪbət/ = pro (前) + hibit (持有) → 禁止（=ban）：Smoking is prohibited in all public buildings. (所有公共建筑内禁止吸烟。)
- pro**hibit**ion /ˌproʊəˈbɪʃən/ = pro (前) + hibit (持有) + ion (名词后缀) → 禁令（=ban）：There is a prohibition on parking in this area. (此区域禁止停车。)

### 感官与思维词根

> 表示视觉、听觉、思考、情感等认知活动。

#### 感官


★**vis/vid=see 看**: 

- **vis**ible /ˈvɪzəbəl/ = vis (看) + ible (可…的) → 可见的（=can be seen）：The stars are clearly visible tonight. (今晚星星清晰可见。)
- **vis**ion /ˈvɪʒən/ = vis (看) + ion (名词后缀) → 视力/视野/愿景（=sight）：She has a clear vision for the company's future. (她对公司的未来有清晰的愿景。)
- **vis**ual /ˈvɪʒəwəl/ = vis (看) + ual (形容词后缀) → 视觉的（=sight-related）：Visual aids can help students understand better. (视觉辅助可以帮助学生更好地理解。)
- **vis**it /ˈvɪzɪt/ = vis (看) + it (去) → 参观/访问（=go to see）：I plan to visit my grandparents this weekend. (我计划这个周末去看望祖父母。)
- **vis**itor /ˈvɪzɪtər/ = vis (看) + it (去) + or (人) → 参观者/访客（=guest）：The museum receives thousands of visitors every day. (博物馆每天接待成千上万的参观者。)
- **vid**eo /ˈvɪdioʊ/ = vid (看) + eo → 视频：She uploaded a video of her trip to social media. (她把旅行视频上传到了社交媒体。)
- e**vid**ence /ˈɛvədəns/ = e (出) + vid (看) + ence (名词后缀) → 证据（=proof）：The police found no evidence of a crime. (警方没有发现犯罪证据。)
- e**vid**ent /ˈɛvədənt/ = e (出) + vid (看) + ent (形容词后缀) → 明显的（=clear）：It became evident that he was lying. (很明显他在撒谎。)
- ob**vi**ous /ˈɑbviəs/ = ob (对面) + vi (看) + ous (形容词后缀) → 明显的（=clear）/显然的：The answer is obvious to everyone. (答案对每个人来说都很明显。)
- ob**vi**ously /ˈɑbviəsli/ = ob (对面) + vi (看) + ous (形容词后缀) + ly (副词后缀) → 明显地（=clearly）：Obviously, she didn't mean to hurt you. (显然，她不是故意要伤害你。)
- ad**vis**e /ədˈvaɪz/ = ad (向) + vis (看) + e → 建议（动词）：I advise you to see a doctor immediately. (我建议你立即去看医生。)
- **ad**vice /ədˈvaɪs/ = ad (向) + vice → 建议（名词）：My father gave me some good advice about life. (父亲给了我一些关于人生的好建议。)
- re**vis**e /rɪˈvaɪz/ = re (再) + vis (看) + e → 修订/复习（=review）：You should revise your essay before submitting it. (提交之前你应该修改你的论文。)
- super**vis**e /ˈsupərˌvaɪz/ = super (上面) + vis (看) + e → 监督/管理（=oversee）：A teacher must supervise the students during the exam. (考试期间老师必须监督学生。)
- super**vis**or /ˈsupərˌvaɪzər/ = super (上面) + vis (看) + or (人) → 主管/监督人（=overseer）：My supervisor approved my vacation request. (我的主管批准了我的休假申请。)
- tele**vis**ion /ˈtɛləˌvɪʒən/ = tele (远) + vis (看) + ion (名词后缀) → 电视（=TV）：Children spend too much time watching television. (孩子们花太多时间看电视。)
- pro**vid**e /prəˈvaɪd/ = pro (前) + vid (看) + e → 提供（提前看到）：The hotel provides free breakfast for all guests. (酒店为所有客人提供免费早餐。)
- pro**vis**ion /prəˈvɪʒən/ = pro (前) + vis (看) + ion (名词后缀) → 供应（=supply）/条款（=rule）：The contract includes a provision for early termination. (合同包含提前终止的条款。)
- **vis**ualize /ˈvɪʒwəˌlaɪz/ = vis (看) + ual + ize (动词后缀) → 想象/使可视化（=picture in mind）：Try to visualize yourself achieving your goal. (试着想象自己实现目标的场景。)


★**spec/spect=look 看**: 

- re**spect** /rɪˈspɛkt/ = re (回) + spect (看) → 回头看 → 尊重（=value）：You should respect other people's opinions. (你应该尊重他人的意见。)
- re**spect**ive /rɪˈspɛktɪv/ = re (回) + spect (看) + ive (形容词后缀) → 各自的（=own）：They went back to their respective homes. (他们回到了各自的家。)
- ex**pect** /ɪkˈspɛkt/ = ex (出) + spect (看) → 向外看 → 期望/预期（=look forward to）：I didn't expect to see you here. (我没想到会在这里见到你。)
- ex**pect**ation /ˌɛkspɛkˈteɪʃən/ = ex (出) + spect (看) + ation (名词后缀) → 期望（=hope）：The results exceeded everyone's expectations. (结果超出了所有人的预期。)
- in**spect** /ˌɪnˈspɛkt/ = in (里) + spect (看) → 往里看 → 检查（=examination）：The mechanic will inspect the car thoroughly. (机械师将彻底检查这辆汽车。)
- in**spect**ion /ˌɪnˈspɛkʃən/ = in (里) + spect (看) + ion (名词后缀) → 检查（=examination）：The building passed the safety inspection. (这栋楼通过了安全检查。)
- su**spect** /ˈsəˌspɛkt/ = su(s) (下) + spect (看) → 怀疑（=doubt）：I suspect he hasn't told us the truth. (我怀疑他没有告诉我们真相。)
- su**spic**ion /səˈspɪʃən/ = su(s) (下) + spic (看) + ion (名词后缀) → 怀疑（=doubt）/嫌疑：Her behavior aroused the police's suspicion. (她的行为引起了警方的怀疑。)
- pro**spect** /ˈprɑspɛkt/ = pro (前) + spect (看) → 前景/展望（=future）：The company has a bright prospect for growth. (公司有光明的发展前景。)
- a**spect** /ˈæˌspɛkt/ = a (向) + spect (看) → 方面/层面（=side）：We need to consider every aspect of the problem. (我们需要考虑问题的每个方面。)
- **spect**ator /ˈspɛkteɪtər/ = spect (看) + ator (人) → 观众（=watcher）：Thousands of spectators watched the football match. (成千上万的观众观看了足球比赛。)
- **spect**acle /ˈspɛktəkəl/ = spect (看) + acle (名词后缀) → 景象/奇观（=sight）：The fireworks created a magnificent spectacle. (烟花创造了壮丽的奇观。)
- per**spect**ive /pərˈspɛktɪv/ = per (穿透) + spect (看) + ive (名词后缀) → 视角/观点（=viewpoint）：From a historical perspective, this event is significant. (从历史的角度看，这个事件很重要。)
- retro**spect** /ˈrɛtrəˌspɛkt/ = retro (向后) + spect (看) → 回顾（=look back）：In retrospect, I should have made a different choice. (回顾过去，我应该做出不同的选择。)
- **spec**ial /ˈspɛʃəl/ = spec (看) + ial (形容词后缀) → 特别的/特殊的（=unusual）：Today is a very special day for our family. (今天对我们家来说是一个非常特别的日子。)
- **spec**ific /spɪˈsɪfɪk/ = spec (看) + ific (形容词后缀) → 具体的/特定的（=exact）：Can you give me a specific example? (你能给我一个具体的例子吗？)
- **spec**ies /ˈspiʃiz/ = spec (看) + ies → 物种/种类（=kind）：Many animal species are in danger of extinction. (许多动物物种面临灭绝的危险。)
- **spec**imen /ˈspɛsəmən/ = spec (看) + imen (名词后缀) → 标本/样本（=sample）：The scientist collected plant specimens in the forest. (科学家在森林里采集了植物标本。)
- **spect**rum /ˈspɛktrəm/ = spect (看) + rum (名词后缀) → 光谱/范围（=range）：The survey covers a wide spectrum of opinions. (这项调查涵盖了广泛的意见。)
- **spec**ulate /ˈspɛkjəˌleɪt/ = spec (看) + ulate (动词后缀) → 推测/猜测（=guess）：People are speculating about the cause of the accident. (人们在猜测事故的原因。)
- e**spec**ially /əˈspɛʃəli/ = e (出) + spec (看) + ial + ly (副词后缀) → 尤其/特别（=most of all）：I love all fruits, especially strawberries. (我喜欢所有水果，尤其是草莓。)


★**aud=hear 听**: 

- **aud**io /ˈɑdiˌoʊ/ = aud (听) + io → 音频/声音的（=sound）：The audio quality of this recording is excellent. (这段录音的音频质量很好。)
- **aud**ience /ˈɔdiəns/ = aud (听) + ience (名词后缀) → 听众/观众（=listeners）：The audience applauded enthusiastically after the speech. (演讲结束后，观众热烈鼓掌。)
- **aud**itorium /ˌɔdəˈtɔriəm/ = aud (听) + it + orium (场所) → 礼堂/观众席（=hall）：The concert will be held in the school auditorium. (音乐会将在学校礼堂举行。)
- **aud**ible /ˈɑdəbəl/ = aud (听) + ible (可…的) → 听得见的（=can be heard）：Her voice was barely audible in the noisy room. (她的声音在嘈杂的房间里几乎听不见。)
- in**aud**ible /ˌɪˈnɔdəbəl/ = in (不) + aud (听) + ible (可…的) → 听不见的（=cannot be heard）：The whisper was inaudible from the back row. (从后排听不到耳语声。)
- **aud**ition /ɑˈdɪʃən/ = aud (听) + ition (名词后缀) → 试镜/试听（=tryout）：She went to an audition for the lead role. (她去参加了主角的试镜。)
- **aud**itor /ˈɔdɪtər/ = aud (听) + itor (人) → 审计员（听账的人）（=financial checker）：The auditor reviewed the company's financial records. (审计员审查了公司的财务记录。)
- **aud**itory /ˈɔdɪˌtɔri/ = aud (听) + itory (形容词后缀) → 听觉的（=hearing-related）：Loud music can cause auditory damage over time. (长时间听大声的音乐可能会损害听觉。)


★**ped=foot 脚**: 

- **ped**estrian /pəˈdɛstriən/ = ped (脚) + estrian (…的人) → 行人/步行的（=walker）：The pedestrian crossed the street at the crosswalk. (行人在人行横道过马路。)
- **ped**al /ˈpɛdəl/ = ped (脚) + al (名词后缀) → 踏板（=foot lever）：She pushed the pedal to accelerate the car. (她踩下踏板加速汽车。)
- centi**ped**e /ˈsɛntɪˌpid/ = centi (百) + ped (脚) + e → 蜈蚣（=hundred-leg bug）：A centipede has many legs and moves very fast. (蜈蚣有很多条腿，移动很快。)
- ex**ped**ition /ˌɛkspəˈdɪʃən/ = ex (出) + ped (脚) + ition (名词后缀) → 远征/探险（=long trip）：The expedition reached the summit after ten days. (探险队在十天后到达了山顶。)
- im**ped**e /ˌɪmˈpid/ = im (在…里) + ped (脚) + e → 阻碍（=block）：Heavy rain impeded the progress of the construction. (大雨阻碍了施工进度。)

#### 认知与思考


★**sci=know 知道**: 

- **sci**ence /saɪəns/ = sci (知道) + ence (名词后缀) → 科学/知识体系（=knowledge system）：Science has greatly improved our quality of life. (科学极大地改善了我们的生活质量。)
- **sci**entist /ˈsaɪəntɪst/ = sci (知道) + entist (…家) → 科学家（=science person）：Marie Curie was a brilliant scientist. (居里夫人是一位杰出的科学家。)
- **sci**entific /ˌsaɪənˈtɪfɪk/ = sci (知道) + ent (形容词后缀) + ific → 科学的（=science-based）：We need scientific evidence to support the theory. (我们需要科学证据来支持这个理论。)
- con**sci**ous /ˈkɑnʃəs/ = con (共同) + sci (知道) + ous (形容词后缀) → 有意识的/清醒的（=aware）：He remained conscious after the accident. (事故后他仍然保持清醒。)
- con**sci**ousness /ˈkɑnʃəsnəs/ = con (共同) + sci (知道) + ous + ness (名词后缀) → 意识（=awareness）：The patient slowly regained consciousness. (病人慢慢恢复了意识。)
- uncon**sci**ous /ˌənˈkɑnʃəs/ = un (不) + con (共同) + sci (知道) + ous (形容词后缀) → 无意识的/昏迷的（=not aware）：She was unconscious for several minutes after the fall. (她摔倒后昏迷了几分钟。)
- subcon**sci**ous /səbˈkɑnʃəs/ = sub (下) + con (共同) + sci (知道) + ous (形容词后缀) → 潜意识的（=below awareness）：Our subconscious mind influences many of our decisions. (我们的潜意识影响着我们的许多决定。)
- con**sci**ence /ˈkɑnʃəns/ = con (共同) + sci (知道) + ence (名词后缀) → 良心/良知（=inner voice）：His conscience wouldn't let him lie. (他的良心不允许他撒谎。)
- con**sci**entious /ˌkɑnʃiˈɛnʃəs/ = con (共同) + sci (知道) + ent + ious (形容词后缀) → 认真负责的（=careful）：She is a conscientious worker who never misses deadlines. (她是一个认真负责的工人，从不拖延。)


★**cogn=know 知道**: 

- re**cogn**ize /ˈrɛkəgˌnaɪz/ = re (再) + cogn (知道) + ize (动词后缀) → 认出/承认（=know again）：I didn't recognize you at first with your new haircut. (你换了新发型，我一开始没认出你。)
- re**cogn**ition /ˌrɛkɪgˈnɪʃən/ = re (再) + cogn (知道) + ition (名词后缀) → 识别/认可（=knowing）：Her hard work earned her recognition from the managers. (她的努力工作赢得了经理们的认可。)
- **cogn**itive /ˈkɑgnɪtɪv/ = cogn (知道) + itive (形容词后缀) → 认知的（=thinking）：Cognitive development is important during early childhood. (认知发展在幼儿期很重要。)
- **cogn**ition /kɑgˈnɪʃən/ = cogn (知道) + ition (名词后缀) → 认知（=thinking）：The study examined the effects of music on memory and cognition. (这项研究考察了音乐对记忆和认知的影响。)
- dia**gnose** /ˌdaɪəgˈnoʊs/ = dia (通过) + gnose (知道) → 诊断（=finding problem）：The doctor can diagnose the illness with a blood test. (医生可以通过血液检查诊断这种疾病。)
- dia**gnosis** /ˌdaɪəgˈnoʊsəs/ = dia (通过) + gnosis (知道) → 诊断（=finding problem）：The diagnosis confirmed that it was just a common cold. (诊断证实这只是普通感冒。)
- i**gnore** /ˌɪgˈnɔr/ = i (不) + gnore (知道) → 忽视/不理（=pay no attention）：It's rude to ignore someone who is talking to you. (忽视正在和你说话的人是不礼貌的。)
- i**gnor**ant /ˈɪgnərənt/ = i (不) + gnor (知道) + ant (形容词后缀) → 无知的（=unknowing）：He is ignorant of even the simplest facts about history. (他对历史中哪怕最简单的事实都一无所知。)
- i**gnor**ance /ˈɪgnərəns/ = i (不) + gnor (知道) + ance (名词后缀) → 无知（=lack of knowledge）：Ignorance of the law does not excuse a crime. (对法律的无知不能成为犯罪的借口。)


★**put=think 思考**: 

- com**put**e /kəmˈpjut/ = com (一起) + put (思考/计算) + e → 计算（=calculate）：The software can compute complex mathematical formulas instantly. (该软件可以瞬间计算出复杂的数学公式。)
- com**put**er /kəmˈpjutər/ = com (一起) + put (思考/计算) + er (物) → 计算（=calculate）机：Most people today use a computer for work or study. (如今大多数人都用计算机工作或学习。)
- dis**put**e /dɪˈspjut/ = dis (分开) + put (思考) + e → 争论/纠纷（=argument）：The two countries are trying to settle their border dispute. (两国正在努力解决边境争端。)
- re**put**e /riˈpjut/ = re (再) + put (思考) + e → 名声/名望（=reputation）：The restaurant has good repute in the local community. (这家餐厅在当地社区享有良好声誉。)
- re**put**ation /ˌrɛpjəˈteɪʃən/ = re (再) + put (思考) + ation (名词后缀) → 名声/声誉（=reputation）：A good reputation is built over many years. (好名声是多年积累起来的。)
- re**put**able /ˈrɛpjətəbəl/ = re (再) + put (思考) + able (可…的) → 有声望的/有信誉的（=trusted）：Make sure you buy from a reputable dealer. (确保你从信誉良好的经销商处购买。)
- in**put** /ˈɪnˌpʊt/ = in (入) + put (放/思考) → 输入（=put in）：Please input your password to log in. (请输入密码登录。)
- out**put** /ˈaʊtˌpʊt/ = out (出) + put (放/思考) → 输出（=put out）：The factory's output has increased by 30 percent. (工厂的产量增加了30%。)
- de**put**y /ˈdɛpjəti/ = de (向下) + put (放/指派) + y → 代理人/副手（=assistant）：The deputy manager will be in charge while the boss is away. (老板不在期间将由副经理负责。)


★**not=mark 标记**: 

- **not**e /noʊt/ = not (标记) + e → 笔记/注意（=write down）：Please take notes during the lecture. (听讲座时请记笔记。)
- **not**able /ˈnoʊtəbəl/ = not (标记) + able (可…的) → 值得注意的/显著的（=important）：The town has made notable progress in recent years. (这个小镇近年来取得了显著的进步。)
- **not**ably /ˈnoʊtəbli/ = not (标记) + ably (副词后缀) → 尤其/显著地（=especially）：Several people were injured, notably a young child. (有几个人受伤了，尤其是一个小孩子。)
- **not**ice /ˈnoʊtɪs/ = not (标记) + ice (名词后缀) → 注意/通告（=see）：Did you notice the sign on the door? (你注意到门上的标志了吗？)
- **not**iceable /ˈnoʊtəsəbəl/ = not (标记) + ice + able (可…的) → 显而易见的（=easy to see）：There was a noticeable change in her attitude. (她的态度发生了明显的变化。)
- **not**ify /ˈnoʊtəˌfaɪ/ = not (标记) + ify (使…) → 通知/告知（=tell）：The school will notify parents about the meeting. (学校将通知家长有关会议的事宜。)
- **not**ification /ˌnoʊtəfəˈkeɪʃən/ = not (标记) + ification (名词后缀) → 通知（=message）：I received a notification about the package delivery. (我收到了关于包裹配送的通知。)
- **not**ion /ˈnoʊʃən/ = not (标记) + ion (名词后缀) → 概念/想法（=idea）：She has no notion of how difficult this task is. (她不知道这个任务有多难。)
- **not**orious /noʊˈtɔriəs/ = not (标记) + orious (形容词后缀) → 臭名昭著的（=known for bad）：The criminal was notorious for his cruel acts. (这个罪犯以其残忍的行为而臭名昭著。)
- de**not**e /dɪˈnoʊt/ = de (向下) + not (标记) + e → 表示/意味着（=mean）：In mathematics, "x" often denotes an unknown value. (在数学中，"x"通常表示未知值。)
- an**not**ate /ˈænəˌteɪt/ = an (向) + not (标记) + ate (动词后缀) → 注释/给…作注解（=add notes）：Students should annotate the text while reading. (学生阅读时应该给文本作注释。)


★**ment=mind 心/智**: 

- **ment**al /ˈmɛntəl/ = ment (心智) + al (形容词后缀) → 精神的/智力的（=mind-related）：Mental health is as important as physical health. (心理健康和身体健康一样重要。)
- **ment**ally /ˈmɛnəli/ = ment (心智) + ally (副词后缀) → 精神上/智力上（=in the mind）：She is mentally strong enough to handle the pressure. (她精神上足够强大，可以应对压力。)
- **ment**ion /ˈmɛnʃən/ = ment (心智) + ion (名词后缀) → 提到/说起（=say briefly）：He didn't mention anything about the trip. (他没有提到关于旅行的事情。)
- com**ment** /ˈkɑmɛnt/ = com (加强) + ment (心智) → 评论/意见（=remark）：Do you have any comments on the proposal? (你对这个提议有什么意见吗？)
- com**ment**ary /ˈkɑmənˌtɛri/ = com (加强) + ment (心智) + ary (名词后缀) → 评论/解说（=remarks）：The football match had live commentary on the radio. (这场足球比赛在广播上有现场解说。)
- com**ment**ator /ˈkɑmənˌteɪtər/ = com (加强) + ment (心智) + ator (人) → 评论员/解说员（=remarker）：The sports commentator provided exciting coverage of the game. (体育评论员对比赛进行了精彩的解说。)
- **ment**or /ˈmɛnˌtɔr/ = ment (心智) + or (人) → 导师/指导者（=guide）：A good mentor can guide you in your career. (一个好的导师可以在你的职业生涯中指导你。)


★**rat=reckon/think 计算/思考**: 

- **rat**e /reɪt/ = rat (计算) + e → 比率/速度/评价（=level）：The unemployment rate has dropped significantly this year. (今年的失业率大幅下降。)
- **rat**io /ˈreɪʃiˌoʊ/ = rat (计算) + io (名词后缀) → 比率/比例（=comparison）：The ratio of men to women in the company is two to one. (公司男女比例是二比一。)
- **rat**ional /ˈræʃənəl/ = rat (思考/理性) + ion + al (形容词后缀) → 理性的/合理的（=logical）：We need to make a rational decision based on facts. (我们需要基于事实做出理性的决定。)
- **rat**ionality /ˌræʃəˈnælɪti/ = rat (思考/理性) + ion + ality (名词后缀) → 理性/合理性（=logic）：Rationality is essential in scientific research. (理性在科学研究中至关重要。)
- ir**rat**ional /ˌɪˈræʃənəl/ = ir (不) + rat (思考/理性) + ion + al (形容词后缀) → 不合理的/不理性的（=illogical）：His fear of flying is completely irrational. (他对飞行的恐惧完全是不理性的。)
- **rea**son /ˈrizən/ = rea (来自rat) + son (名词后缀) → 原因/理性（=cause）：The reason for the delay was bad weather. (延误的原因是不良天气。)
- **rea**son**able** /ˈrizənəbəl/ = rea (来自rat) + son + able (可…的) → 合理的（=fair）：The price is reasonable for such good quality. (对于这么好的质量来说，价格是合理的。)


**soph=wise 智慧**: 

- **soph**isticated /səˈfɪstɪˌkeɪtəd/ = soph (智慧) + ist + icated (形容词后缀) → 复杂精密的/老练的（=advanced）：The laboratory is equipped with sophisticated instruments. (实验室配备了精密的仪器。)
- **soph**omore /ˈsɑfˌmɔr/ = soph (智慧) + o + more (更多) → 大二学生（=second-year student）：When I was a sophomore, I joined the debate team. (我大二时加入了辩论队。)
- philo**soph**y /fəˈlɑsəfi/ = philo (爱) + soph (智慧) + y (名词后缀) → 哲学（爱智慧）（=love of wisdom）：Ancient Greek philosophy still influences modern thought. (古希腊哲学仍然影响着现代思想。)
- **soph**ism /sophism*/ = soph (智慧) + ism (主义) → 诡辩（=clever but false）：His argument was nothing more than clever sophism. (他的论点不过是巧妙的诡辩。)


**ideo=idea 思想**: 

- **idea** /aɪˈdiə/ = ideo (思想) → 想法/主意（=thought）：That's a great idea! (那是个好主意！)
- ide**al** /aɪˈdil/ = ideo (思想) + al (形容词后缀) → 理想的/完美的（=perfect）：This place is ideal for a family vacation. (这个地方是家庭度假的理想之选。)
- ideal**ism** /aɪˈdilɪzəm/ = ideo (思想) + al + ism (主义) → 理想主义（=belief in ideals）：His idealism inspired many young people to follow him. (他的理想主义激励了许多年轻人追随他。)
- **ideo**logy /ˌaɪdiˈɑləʤi/ = ideo (思想) + logy (学说) → 意识（=awareness）形态：Political ideologies shape the policies of governments. (政治意识形态塑造了政府的政策。)


**judg/judic=judge 判断**: 

- **judg**e /ʤəʤ/ = judg (判断) + e → 判断/法官（=decide）：Don't judge a person by their appearance. (不要以貌取人。)
- **judg**ment /ˈʤəʤmənt/ = judg (判断) + ment (名词后缀) → 判断/裁决（=decision）：The court will announce its judgment tomorrow. (法庭将于明天宣布判决。)
- **judic**ial /ʤuˈdɪʃəl/ = judic (判断/法官) + ial (形容词后缀) → 司法的/审判的（=court-related）：The judicial system must be fair and independent. (司法系统必须公正和独立。)
- pre**judic**e /ˈprɛʤədɪs/ = pre (之前) + judic (判断) + e → 偏见（=unfair judgment）：We should fight against racial prejudice in society. (我们应该打击社会中的种族偏见。)
- pre**judic**ial /ˌprɛʤəˈdɪʃəl/ = pre (之前) + judic (判断) + ial (形容词后缀) → 有偏见的/不利的（=unfair）：The article contained prejudicial statements about the defendant. (这篇文章包含对被告有偏见的陈述。)
- ad**judic**ate /əˈʤudɪˌkeɪt/ = ad (向) + judic (判断) + ate (动词后缀) → 裁决/判决（=judge）：The court will adjudicate the dispute between the two parties. (法庭将裁决双方之间的争议。)


**mon=warn/advise 警告**: 

- **mon**itor /ˈmɑnətər/ = mon (警告) + itor (人/物) → 班长/监视器/监控（=watch）：The nurse will monitor the patient's condition overnight. (护士将在夜间监控病人的状况。)
- ad**mon**ish /ædˈmɑnɪʃ/ = ad (向) + mon (警告) + ish (动词后缀) → 警告/告诫（=warn）：The teacher admonished the student for cheating on the exam. (老师因学生考试作弊而警告了他。)
- pre**mon**ition /prɛməˈnɪʃən/ = pre (之前) + mon (警告) + ition (名词后缀) → 预感/预兆（=feeling beforehand）：She had a strange premonition that something bad was going to happen. (她有一种不祥的预感。)
- **mon**ument /ˈmɑnjəmənt/ = mon (警告/提醒) + ument (名词后缀) → 纪念碑（=remembrance）：The monument was built to honor the war heroes. (这座纪念碑是为纪念战争英雄而建造的。)
- sum**mon** /ˈsəmən/ = sum (下) + mon (警告/劝告) → 召唤/召集（=call）：The manager summoned all employees to an emergency meeting. (经理召集了所有员工开紧急会议。)


**clar/clear=clear 清楚**: 

- **clear** /klɪr/ = clear (清楚) → 清楚的/明白的：The instructions are very clear and easy to follow. (指示很清楚，容易遵循。)
- **clar**ify /ˈklɛrəˌfaɪ/ = clar (清楚) + ify (使…) → 澄清/阐明（=make clear）：Could you clarify what you meant by that statement? (你能澄清一下你那句话的意思吗？)
- **clar**ification /ˌklɛrəfəˈkeɪʃən/ = clar (清楚) + ification (名词后缀) → 澄清（=making clear）：The spokesperson provided clarification on the new policy. (发言人澄清了新政策。)
- **clar**ity /ˈklɛrɪti/ = clar (清楚) + ity (名词后缀) → 清晰/明确（=clearness）：The clarity of her explanation impressed the audience. (她解释的清晰度给观众留下了深刻印象。)
- de**clar**e /dɪˈklɛr/ = de (完全) + clar (清楚) + e → 宣布/声明（=announce）：The president will declare the new law next week. (总统将在下周宣布新法律。)
- de**clar**ation /ˌdɛklərˈeɪʃən/ = de (完全) + clar (清楚) + ation (名词后缀) → 宣言/声明（=announcement）：The Declaration of Independence was signed in 1776. (独立宣言于1776年签署。)


**liter=letter 文字**: 

- **liter**ature /ˈlɪtərəʧər/ = liter (文字) + ature (名词后缀) → 文学（=written works）：English literature is my favorite subject at school. (英国文学是我在学校最喜欢的科目。)
- **liter**ary /ˈlɪtərˌɛri/ = liter (文字) + ary (形容词后缀) → 文学（=written works）的：The novel won several literary awards. (这部小说获得了多个文学奖项。)
- **liter**al /ˈlɪtərəl/ = liter (文字) + al (形容词后缀) → 字面的/逐字的（=word-for-word）：The literal meaning of the word is different from its usage. (这个词的字面意思与其用法不同。)
- **liter**ally /ˈlɪtərəli/ = liter (文字) + ally (副词后缀) → 照字面地/确实（=exactly）：The room was so small that there was literally no space to move. (房间太小了，简直没有空间移动。)
- il**liter**ate /ˌɪˈlɪtərət/ = il (不) + liter (文字) + ate (形容词后缀) → 文盲的/不识字的（=cannot read）：Millions of people in the world are still illiterate. (世界上仍有数百万人是文盲。)
- **liter**acy /ˈlɪtərəsi/ = liter (文字) + acy (名词后缀) → 读写能力（=reading ability）：Improving children's literacy is a key goal of education. (提高儿童的读写能力是教育的关键目标。)


**lingu=language/tongue 语言/舌**: 

- **langu**age /ˈlæŋgwɪʤ/ = langu (语言) + age (名词后缀) → 语言：Learning a new language broadens your horizons. (学习一门新语言可以开阔你的视野。)
- **lingu**istics /lɪŋgˈwɪstɪks/ = lingu (语言) + istics (学科) → 语言学（=study of language）：She is studying linguistics at university. (她在大学学习语言学。)
- **lingu**ist /ˈlɪŋgwɪst/ = lingu (语言) + ist (…家) → 语言学（=study of language）家：Chomsky is one of the most influential linguists of our time. (乔姆斯基是我们这个时代最有影响力的语言学家之一。)
- bi**lingu**al /baɪˈlɪŋgwəl/ = bi (二) + lingu (语言) + al (形容词后缀) → 双语的（=two-language）：Growing up bilingual is a great advantage. (在双语环境中成长是一个很大的优势。)
- mono**lingu**al /ˌmɑnəˈlɪŋgwəl/ = mono (单一) + lingu (语言) + al (形容词后缀) → 单语的（=one-language）：Many monolingual speakers wish they could speak a second language. (许多单语者希望他们会说第二门语言。)
- multi**lingu**al /ˌməltiˈlɪŋwəl/ = multi (多) + lingu (语言) + al (形容词后缀) → 多语的（=many-language）：In multilingual countries, people often speak three or four languages. (在多语国家，人们通常会说三四种语言。)


**nom/onym=name 名**: 

- **name** /neɪm/ = name (名) → 名字/名称：What is the name of the restaurant you recommended? (你推荐的那家餐厅叫什么名字？)
- **nom**inate /ˈnɑməˌneɪt/ = nomin (名) + ate (动词后缀) → 提名/推荐（=name for award）：She was nominated for the Best Actress award. (她被提名了最佳女演员奖。)
- **nom**ination /ˌnɑməˈneɪʃən/ = nomin (名) + ation (名词后缀) → 提名（=naming）：His nomination for the Nobel Prize surprised many people. (他被提名诺贝尔奖让很多人感到惊讶。)
- an**onym**ous /əˈnɑnəməs/ = an (无) + onym (名) + ous (形容词后缀) → 匿名的（=nameless）：The donation was made by an anonymous benefactor. (这笔捐赠是由一位匿名捐助者捐出的。)
- syn**onym** /ˈsɪnəˌnɪm/ = syn (同) + onym (名) → 同义词（=same meaning）："Happy" is a synonym for "glad." ("Happy"是"glad"的同义词。)
- ant**onym** /antonym*/ = ant (反) + onym (名) → 反义词（=opposite meaning）："Hot" is the antonym of "cold." ("Hot"是"cold"的反义词。)
- pseud**onym** /ˈsudəˌnɪm/ = pseudo (假) + nym (名) → 笔名/假名（=fake name）：The author wrote the novel under a pseudonym. (作者用笔名写了这本小说。)


★**sign=mark 标记**: 

- **sign** /saɪn/ = sign (标记) → 符号/标志/签字：Please sign your name at the bottom of the form. (请在表格底部签上你的名字。)
- **sign**al /ˈsɪgnəl/ = sign (标记) + al (名词后缀) → 信号/发信号（=sign）：The driver didn't see the traffic signal and ran the red light. (司机没看到交通信号，闯了红灯。)
- **sign**ature /ˈsɪgnəʧər/ = sign (标记) + ature (名词后缀) → 签名（=written name）：The contract requires the signature of both parties. (合同需要双方的签名。)
- **sign**ificant /sɪgˈnɪfɪkənt/ = sign (标记) + ificant (形容词后缀) → 有意义的/重要的（=meaningful）：There has been a significant increase in sales this year. (今年的销售额有了显著的增长。)
- **sign**ificance /sɪgˈnɪfɪkəns/ = sign (标记) + ificance (名词后缀) → 意义/重要性（=meaning）：The discovery is of great significance to science. (这一发现对科学具有重要意义。)
- **sign**ify /ˈsɪgnəˌfaɪ/ = sign (标记) + ify (使…) → 表示/意味着（=mean）：A red light signifies that you must stop. (红灯表示你必须停下来。)
- as**sign** /əˈsaɪn/ = as (向) + sign (标记) → 分配/指派（=give）：The teacher will assign homework at the end of class. (老师会在下课时布置作业。)
- as**sign**ment /əˈsaɪnmənt/ = as (向) + sign (标记) + ment (名词后缀) → 任务/分配（=task）：The assignment must be completed by Friday. (这项任务必须在周五前完成。)
- de**sign** /dɪˈzaɪn/ = de (向下) + sign (标记) → 设计/计划（=plan）：She designed a beautiful logo for the company. (她为公司设计了一个漂亮的标志。)
- de**sign**er /dɪˈzaɪnər/ = de (向下) + sign (标记) + er (人) → 设计师（=planner）：She works as a fashion designer in Paris. (她在巴黎做时装设计师。)
- de**sign**ate /ˈdɛzɪgˌneɪt/ = de (向下) + sign (标记) + ate (动词后缀) → 指定/任命（=appoint）：The team leader will designate tasks to each member. (组长将向每个成员指定任务。)
- re**sign** /rɪˈzaɪn/ = re (回) + sign (标记) → 辞职（=quit job）：He decided to resign from his position due to health reasons. (他因健康原因决定辞职。)
- re**sign**ation /ˌrɛzɪgˈneɪʃən/ = re (回) + sign (标记) + ation (名词后缀) → 辞职（=quit job）/顺从：She submitted her resignation letter last Monday. (她上周一提交了辞职信。)


★**opt=choose 选择**: 

- **opt**ion /ˈɔpʃən/ = opt (选择) + ion (名词后缀) → 选择/选项（=choice）：You have the option to pay by cash or credit card. (你可以选择用现金或信用卡支付。)
- **opt**ional /ˈɔpʃənəl/ = opt (选择) + ion + al (形容词后缀) → 可选的/非强制的（=not required）：The extra activities are optional, not required. (额外活动是可选的，不是强制的。)
- ad**opt** /əˈdɑpt/ = ad (向) + opt (选择) → 采纳/收养（=taking on）：They decided to adopt a child from the orphanage. (他们决定从孤儿院收养一个孩子。)
- ad**opt**ion /əˈdɑpʃən/ = ad (向) + opt (选择) + ion (名词后缀) → 采纳/收养（=taking on）：The adoption of new technology improved productivity. (新技术的采用提高了生产力。)
- **opt** /ɑpt/ = opt (选择) → 选择/抉择（=choose）：Many students opt for online courses these days. (如今许多学生选择在线课程。)
- **opt**imum /ˈɑptɪməm/ = opt (选择) + imum (最…) → 最优的/最佳的（=best）：The optimum temperature for the experiment is 25 degrees. (实验的最佳温度是25度。)
- **opt**imize /ˈɑptɪˌmaɪz/ = opt (选择) + im + ize (动词后缀) → 优化（=make best）：We need to optimize the process to save more time. (我们需要优化流程以节省更多时间。)
- **opt**imism /ˈɑptɪˌmɪzəm/ = opt (选择) + im + ism (名词后缀) → 乐观/乐观主义（=positive outlook）：Her optimism helped her through difficult times. (她的乐观帮助她度过了困难时期。)
- **opt**imistic /ˌɑptɪˈmɪstɪk/ = opt (选择) + im + istic (形容词后缀) → 乐观的（=positive）：He is optimistic about the outcome of the negotiations. (他对谈判结果持乐观态度。)


★**test=witness 见证/证明**: 

- **test** /tɛst/ = test (证明) → 测试/检验/试验：The students will take a math test tomorrow. (学生们明天将参加数学测试。)
- **test**ify /ˈtɛstɪˌfaɪ/ = test (证明) + ify (使…) → 作证/证明（=give evidence）：The witness agreed to testify in court. (证人同意出庭作证。)
- **test**imony /ˈtɛstɪˌmoʊni/ = test (证明) + imony (名词后缀) → 证词/证据（=evidence）：Her testimony helped the jury reach a verdict. (她的证词帮助陪审团做出了裁决。)
- pro**test** /ˈproʊˌtɛst/ = pro (前) + test (证明) → 抗议/反对（=object to）：Thousands of people gathered to protest against the new law. (成千上万的人聚集起来抗议新法律。)
- con**test** /ˈkɑntɛst/ = con (一起) + test (证明) → 比赛/竞赛（=competition）：She won first prize in the singing contest. (她在歌唱比赛中获得了一等奖。)
- con**test**ant /kənˈtɛstənt/ = con (一起) + test (证明) + ant (人) → 参赛者（=competitor）：Each contestant had two minutes to answer the questions. (每位参赛者有两分钟时间回答问题。)
- de**test** /dɪˈtɛst/ = de (向下) + test (证明) → 厌恶/憎恨（=hate）：I detest people who are rude to waiters. (我厌恶对服务员无礼的人。)
- at**test** /əˈtɛst/ = at (向) + test (证明) → 证明（=confirm）：His success attests to his hard work and dedication. (他的成功证明了他的努力和奉献。)


★**prehend/prehens=catch 抓住/理解**: 

- com**prehend** /ˌkɑmpriˈhɛnd/ = com (一起) + prehend (抓住) → 理解/领会（=understand）：It is difficult to comprehend the scale of the universe. (很难理解宇宙的规模。)
- com**prehens**ion /ˌkɑmpriˈhɛnʃən/ = com (一起) + prehens (抓住) + ion (名词后缀) → 理解/理解力（=understanding）：Reading comprehension is an important skill to develop. (阅读理解是一项需要培养的重要技能。)
- com**prehens**ive /ˌkɑmpriˈhɛnsɪv/ = com (一起) + prehens (抓住) + ive (形容词后缀) → 全面的/综合的（=all-around）：The report provides a comprehensive overview of the issue. (该报告提供了对此问题的全面概述。)
- com**pris**e /kəmˈpraɪz/ = com (一起) + prise (抓住) → 包含/构成（=include）：The committee comprises experts from various fields. (该委员会由来自各个领域的专家组成。)
- enter**pris**e /ˈɛnərˌpraɪz/ = enter (在…之间) + prise (抓住) → 企业/事业（=business）：Starting a new enterprise requires courage and capital. (创办一家新企业需要勇气和资金。)
- sur**pris**e /səˈpraɪz/ = sur (上面) + prise (抓住) → 惊讶/使惊奇（=amazement）：The birthday party was a complete surprise to her. (生日派对对她来说完全是个惊喜。)
- ap**prehend** /ˌæprɪˈhɛnd/ = ap (向) + prehend (抓住) → 理解（=understand）/逮捕（=catch）：The police managed to apprehend the suspect. (警方设法逮捕了嫌疑人。)
- ap**prehens**ion /ˌæprɪˈhɛnʃən/ = ap (向) + prehens (抓住) + ion (名词后缀) → 理解（=understanding）/忧虑（=worry）：She felt a sense of apprehension before the exam. (考试前她感到一阵忧虑。)
- ap**prent**ice /əˈprɛntɪs/ = ap (向) + prent (抓住) + ice (名词后缀) → 学徒/徒弟（=learner）：He worked as an apprentice to a master carpenter. (他在一位木匠大师手下当学徒。)
- **pris**on /ˈprɪzən/ = pris (抓住) + on (名词后缀) → 监狱（=jail）：He was sentenced to three years in prison. (他被判处三年监禁。)
- **pris**on**er** /ˈprɪzənər/ = pris (抓住) + on + er (人) → 囚犯/俘虏（=captive）：The prisoner was released after serving his sentence. (囚犯在服刑期满后获释。)

#### 情感与意志


★**sent/sens=feel 感觉**:

- **sens**e /sɛns/ = sent/sens (feel) → 感觉/感官：Common sense is not so common. (常识并不常见。)
- **sens**itive /ˈsɛnsɪtɪv/ = sens (feel) + itive (adj.) → 敏感的（=easily affected）：She is very sensitive to criticism. (她对批评非常敏感。)
- **sens**ible /ˈsɛnsəbəl/ = sens (feel) + ible (adj.) → 明智的/合理的（=reasonable）：It is sensible to save money for the future. (为未来存钱是明智的。)
- **sent**iment /ˈsɛnəmənt/ = sent (feel) + ment (n.) → 情感（=feeling）/情绪：There is strong public sentiment against the policy. (公众对该政策有强烈的反感情绪。)
- con**sens**us /kənˈsɛnsəs/ = con (together) + sens (feel) + us (n.) → 共识（=shared view）：The team reached a consensus on the plan. (团队就该计划达成了共识。)
- con**sent** /kənˈsɛnt/ = con (together) + sent (feel) → 同意（=say yes）：You need parental consent to participate. (你需要父母同意才能参加。)
- dis**sent** /dɪˈsɛnt/ = dis (apart) + sent (feel) → 异议（=disagreement）：Two judges expressed their dissent from the majority opinion. (两位法官对多数意见表示了异议。)
- re**sent** /rɪˈzɛnt/ = re (back) + sent (feel) → 怨恨（=bitterness）：He resents being treated like a child. (他讨厌被当作小孩对待。)
- re**sent**ment /rɪˈzɛntmənt/ = re (back) + sent (feel) + ment (n.) → 怨恨（=bitterness）：Years of resentment built up between them. (多年的怨恨在他们之间积累。)
- pre**sent** /ˈprɛzənt/ = pre (before) + sent (feel/be) → 礼物/呈现/现在的（=gift）：She received a wonderful present for her birthday. (她收到了一份很棒的生日礼物。)
- repre**sent** /ˌrɛprɪˈzɛnt/ = re (again) + pre (before) + sent (be) → 代表（=stand for）：The lawyer will represent the client in court. (律师将在法庭上代表客户。)
- repre**sent**ation /ˌrɛprəzɛnˈteɪʃən/ = re (again) + pre (before) + sent (be) + ation (n.) → 代表（=stand for）/表现：The painting is a representation of rural life. (这幅画是乡村生活的写照。)
- non**sens**e /ˈnɑnsɛns/ = non (not) + sens (feel/sense) + e → 胡说/废话（=foolish talk）：Don't listen to him; he is talking nonsense. (别听他的，他在胡说八道。)


★**spir=breathe 呼吸**:

- **spir**it /ˈspɪrɪt/ = spir (breathe) + it (n.) → 精神/灵魂（=inner self）：Team spirit is essential for success. (团队精神对成功至关重要。)
- **spir**itual /ˈspɪrɪˌʧuəl/ = spir (breathe) + it + ual (adj.) → 精神的/心灵的（=inner）：She finds spiritual peace in meditation. (她在冥想中找到心灵的平静。)
- in**spir**e /ˌɪnˈspaɪr/ = in (into) + spir (breathe) + e → 激励（=encourage）/吸气：His speech inspired the audience to take action. (他的演讲激励了听众采取行动。)
- in**spir**ation /ˌɪnspərˈeɪʃən/ = in (into) + spir (breathe) + ation (n.) → 灵感（=creative idea）：Nature is a great source of inspiration for artists. (大自然是艺术家的重要灵感来源。)
- **expir**e /ɪkˈspaɪr/ = ex (out) + pir (breathe) + e → 到期（=run out）/呼气（=breathe out）：My passport will expire next month. (我的护照下个月到期。)
- per**spir**e /pərˈspaɪr/ = per (through) + spir (breathe) + e → 出汗（=sweat）：He began to perspire after running for ten minutes. (跑了十分钟后他开始出汗。)
- re**spir**e /respire*/ = re (again) + spir (breathe) + e → 呼吸（=breathe）：Fish respire through their gills. (鱼通过鳃呼吸。)
- re**spir**ator /ˈrɛspərˌeɪtər/ = re (again) + spir (breathe) + ator (n.) → 口罩/呼吸器（=breathing mask）：Doctors wore respirators during the surgery. (医生在手术中佩戴了口罩。)
- con**spir**e /kənˈspaɪər/ = con (together) + spir (breathe) + e → 共谋/密谋（=plot together）：They conspired to overthrow the government. (他们密谋推翻政府。)
- con**spir**acy /kənˈspɪrəsi/ = con (together) + spir (breathe) + acy (n.) → 阴谋（=secret plan）：He was accused of being involved in a conspiracy. (他被指控参与了一场阴谋。)


★**pass/pati=suffer 感受/忍受**:

- **pass**ion /ˈpæʃən/ = pass (suffer/feel) + ion (n.) → 热情/激情（=strong feeling）：He has a passion for classical music. (他对古典音乐充满热情。)
- **pass**ionate /ˈpæʃənət/ = pass (suffer/feel) + ion + ate (adj.) → 热情的（=enthusiastic）：She is a passionate advocate for human rights. (她是一位热情的人权倡导者。)
- **pass**ive /ˈpæsɪv/ = pass (suffer) + ive (adj.) → 被动的/消极的（=not active）：He is too passive and never takes the initiative. (他太被动了，从不主动。)
- **pati**ent /ˈpeɪʃənt/ = pati (suffer) + ent (adj./n.) → 病人（=sick person）/耐心的（=tolerant）：The doctor treated the patient with great care. (医生非常细心地治疗病人。)
- **pati**ence /ˈpeɪʃəns/ = pati (suffer) + ence (n.) → 耐心（=tolerance）：Learning a new language requires patience. (学习一门新语言需要耐心。)
- im**pati**ent /ˌɪmˈpeɪʃənt/ = im (not) + pati (suffer) + ent (adj.) → 不耐烦的（=not patient）：The children grew impatient waiting for dinner. (孩子们等晚饭等得不耐烦了。)
- com**pati**ble /kəmˈpætəbəl/ = com (together) + pati (suffer/feel) + ble (adj.) → 兼容的/合得来的（=fits together）：Are these two software programs compatible? (这两个软件程序兼容吗？)
- com**pati**bility /kəmˌpætəˈbɪləˌti/ = com (together) + pati (suffer/feel) + bility (n.) → 兼容性（=fit-togetherness）：Check the compatibility before installing the software. (安装软件前先检查兼容性。)


★**grat=pleasing 愉快**:

- **grat**eful /ˈgreɪtfəl/ = grat (pleasing) + e + ful (adj.) → 感激的（=thankful）：I am deeply grateful for your help. (我深深感激你的帮助。)
- **grat**itude /ˈgrætəˌtud/ = grat (pleasing) + itude (n.) → 感激（=thankfulness）：She expressed her gratitude with a handwritten note. (她用手写的便条表达了她的感激之情。)
- con**grat**ulate /kənˈgræʧəˌleɪt/ = con (together) + grat (pleasing) + ul + ate (v.) → 祝贺（=expression of joy）：I want to congratulate you on your promotion. (我想祝贺你升职。)
- con**grat**ulation /kənˌgræʧəˈleɪʃən/ = con (together) + grat (pleasing) + ul + ation (n.) → 祝贺（=expression of joy）：Congratulations on winning the award! (恭喜你获奖！)
- **grac**e /greɪs/ = grat (pleasing) → 优雅/恩典（=elegance）：She danced with great grace and elegance. (她跳舞非常优雅端庄。)
- grac**ious** /ˈgreɪʃəs/ = grat (pleasing) + ious (adj.) → 亲切的/仁慈的（=kind）：The hostess was gracious to all her guests. (女主人对所有客人都很亲切。)
- a**gree** /əˈgri/ = a (to) + gree (pleasing) → 同意（=say yes）：I completely agree with your point of view. (我完全同意你的观点。)
- a**gree**able /əˈgriəbəl/ = a (to) + gree (pleasing) + able (adj.) → 令人愉快的（=pleasant）：He is a very agreeable person to work with. (他是一个很让人愉快的共事者。)
- a**gree**ment /əˈgrimənt/ = a (to) + gree (pleasing) + ment (n.) → 协议/一致（=deal）：Both parties signed the agreement yesterday. (双方昨天签署了协议。)


**psych=soul/mind 心灵**:

- **psych**ology /saɪˈkɑləʤi/ = psych (mind) + ology (study of) → 心理学（=study of mind）：She is studying psychology at university. (她在大学学习心理学。)
- **psych**ological /ˌsaɪkəˈlɑʤɪkəl/ = psych (mind) + ology + ical (adj.) → 心理学（=study of mind）的/心理的：The accident caused him severe psychological trauma. (事故给他造成了严重的心理创伤。)
- **psych**ologist /saɪˈkɑləʤəst/ = psych (mind) + ology + ist (person) → 心理学（=study of mind）家：The psychologist helped him overcome his anxiety. (心理学家帮助他克服了焦虑。)
- **psych**iatry /sɪˈkaɪətri/ = psych (mind) + iatry (healing) → 精神病学（=study of mental illness）：Psychiatry is the branch of medicine dealing with mental disorders. (精神病学是研究精神疾病的医学分支。)


**phil=love 爱**:

- **phil**osophy /fəˈlɑsəfi/ = phil (love) + o + soph (wisdom) + y (n.) → 哲学（=love of wisdom）：Philosophy teaches us to question our assumptions. (哲学教会我们质疑自己的假设。)
- **phil**osopher /fəˈlɑsəfər/ = phil (love) + o + soph (wisdom) + er (person) → 哲学（=love of wisdom）家：Socrates is one of the most famous philosophers. (苏格拉底是最著名的哲学家之一。)
- **phil**anthropy /fɪˈlænθrəpi/ = phil (love) + anthrop (human) + y (n.) → 慈善（爱人类）（=love of humanity）：His philanthropy has helped thousands of people. (他的慈善事业帮助了成千上万的人。)


★**cord/cor=heart 心**:

- **cord**ial /ˈkɔrʤəl/ = cord (心) + ial (形容词后缀) → 衷心的/热诚的（=friendly）：We received a cordial welcome from our host.
- **cor**age /corage*/ = cor (心) + age (名词后缀) → 勇气（=bravery）：It takes courage to speak in front of a large audience.
- **cor**ageous /corageous*/ = cor (心) + age + ous (形容词后缀) → 勇敢的（=brave）：The courageous firefighter saved the child from the burning building.
- **cor**e /kɔr/ = cor (心) + e → 核心（=center）：The core of the problem is lack of communication.
- en**cor**age /encorage*/ = en (使) + cor (心) + age → 鼓励（=give support）：Teachers should encourage students to ask questions.
- en**cor**agement /encoragement*/ = en (使) + cor (心) + age + ment (名词后缀) → 鼓励（=support）：Your encouragement means a lot to me.
- dis**cor**age /discorage*/ = dis (否定) + cor (心) + age → 使气馁（=make less confident）：Don't let failure discourage you from trying again.
- ac**cord** /əˈkɔrd/ = ac (向) + cord (心) → 一致/协议（=agreement）：The two countries signed a peace accord.
- ac**cord**ing to /əˈkɔrdɪŋ tɪ/ = ac (向) + cord (心) + ing + to → 根据（=as stated by）：According to the weather report, it will rain tomorrow.
- re**cord** /ˈrɛkərd/ = re (再) + cord (心) → 记录/录音（=write down）：The teacher recorded the students' grades.


**am=love 爱**:

- **am**ateur /ˈæməˌʧər/ = am (love) + ateur (person) → 业余爱好者（=non-professional）：He is an amateur photographer who takes beautiful pictures. (他是一位业余摄影师，拍的照片很美。)
- **am**ateurish /ˈæməˌʧərɪʃ/ = am (love) + ateur + ish (adj.) → 业余的/不熟练的（=non-professional）：His painting looked amateurish compared to the professionals. (与专业人士相比，他的画看起来有点业余。)
- **am**iable /ˈeɪmiəbəl/ = am (love) + i + able (adj.) → 和蔼可亲的（=friendly）：She is an amiable old lady who always smiles. (她是一位总是微笑的和蔼可亲的老太太。)
- **am**icable /ˈæmɪkəbəl/ = am (love) + ic + able (adj.) → 友好的（=peaceful）：The divorce was amicable and both remained friends. (离婚是友好的，两人仍然是朋友。)


**pathy=feeling 情感/疾病**:

- sym**pathy** /ˈsɪmpəθi/ = sym (together) + pathy (feeling) → 同情（=feeling with）：I have sympathy for anyone who has lost a loved one. (我对任何失去亲人的人都抱有同情。)
- sym**path**etic /ˌsɪmpəˈθɛtɪk/ = sym (together) + path (feeling) + etic (adj.) → 同情（=feeling with）的：She was very sympathetic when I told her my problem. (当我告诉她我的问题时，她非常同情。)
- em**pathy** /ˈɛmpəθi/ = em (in) + pathy (feeling) → 共情/同理心（=feeling into）：Good doctors have empathy for their patients. (好医生对病人有同理心。)
- a**pathy** /ˈæpəθi/ = a (without) + pathy (feeling) → 冷漠（=lack of feeling）：Voter apathy is a serious problem in many democracies. (选民冷漠是许多民主国家的严重问题。)
- a**path**etic /ˌæpəˈθɛtɪk/ = a (without) + path (feeling) + etic (adj.) → 冷漠（=lack of feeling）的：He seems apathetic about his own future. (他似乎对自己的未来漠不关心。)
- **path**etic /pəˈθɛtɪk/ = path (feeling/suffer) + etic (adj.) → 可怜的/悲惨的（=pitiful）：The stray dog looked pathetic in the rain. (流浪狗在雨中看起来很可怜。)
- anti**pathy** /ænˈtɪpəθi/ = anti (against) + pathy (feeling) → 反感（=dislike）：He has a strong antipathy toward dishonesty. (他对不诚实有强烈的反感。)
- **patho**logy /pəˈθɑləʤi/ = path (disease) + ology (study of) → 病理学（=study of disease）：Pathology is the study of diseases and their causes. (病理学是研究疾病及其原因的学科。)


**mir=wonder 惊奇**:

- **mir**ror /ˈmɪrər/ = mir (wonder/look) + r + or (n.) → 镜子（=looking glass）：She looked at herself in the mirror before leaving. (她离开前照了照镜子。)
- **mir**acle /ˈmɪrəkəl/ = mir (wonder) + acle (n.) → 奇迹（=wonder）：It is a miracle that he survived the accident. (他在事故中幸存是一个奇迹。)
- **mir**aculous /mərˈækjələs/ = mir (wonder) + acul + ous (adj.) → 奇迹（=wonder）般的：She made a miraculous recovery from the illness. (她从疾病中奇迹般地康复了。)
- ad**mir**e /ædˈmaɪr/ = ad (at) + mir (wonder) + e → 钦佩/欣赏（=look up to）：I admire your courage to speak the truth. (我钦佩你说出真相的勇气。)
- ad**mir**ation /ˌædmərˈeɪʃən/ = ad (at) + mir (wonder) + ation (n.) → 钦佩（=respect）：She looked at the artist with admiration. (她钦佩地看着那位艺术家。)
- ad**mir**able /ˈædmərəbəl/ = ad (at) + mir (wonder) + able (adj.) → 令人钦佩的（=respectable）：His dedication to his work is admirable. (他对工作的奉献精神令人钦佩。)
- **marv**el /ˈmɑrvəl/ = mir (wonder) → 奇迹（=wonder）/惊叹：The Great Wall is a marvel of ancient engineering. (长城是古代工程的奇迹。)
- marvel**ous** /ˈmɑrvələs/ = mir (wonder) + ous (adj.) → 奇迹（=wonder）般的/极好的：We had a marvelous time at the party. (我们在聚会上玩得非常开心。)


★**spond/spons=promise 承诺**:

- re**spond** /rɪˈspɑnd/ = re (back) + spond (promise) → 回应（=answer）：He didn't respond to my message until the next day. (他直到第二天才回复我的信息。)
- re**spons**e /rɪˈspɑns/ = re (back) + spons (promise) + e → 回应（=answer）：Her response to the question was very thoughtful. (她对问题的回答非常深思熟虑。)
- re**spons**ible /riˈspɑnsəbəl/ = re (back) + spons (promise) + ible (adj.) → 负责的/有责任的（=accountable）：Parents are responsible for their children's education. (父母对孩子的教育负有责任。)
- re**spons**ibility /riˌspɑnsəˈbɪləti/ = re (back) + spons (promise) + ibility (n.) → 责任（=duty）：Taking care of a pet is a big responsibility. (照顾宠物是一份重大的责任。)
- re**spons**ive /rɪˈspɑnsɪv/ = re (back) + spons (promise) + ive (adj.) → 响应的/敏感的（=reacting）：The company is very responsive to customer complaints. (该公司对客户投诉反应非常迅速。)
- corre**spond** /ˌkɔrəˈspɑnd/ = cor (together) + re (back) + spond (promise) → 通信/相符（=exchange letters）：The two reports correspond with each other. (这两份报告相互吻合。)
- corre**spond**ence /ˌkɔrəˈspɑndəns/ = cor (together) + re (back) + spond (promise) + ence (n.) → 通信/一致（=letter exchange）：We kept up a correspondence for many years. (我们保持了多年的通信联系。)
- corre**spond**ent /ˌkɔrəˈspɑndənt/ = cor (together) + re (back) + spond (promise) + ent (person) → 记者（=reporter）：She works as a foreign correspondent for the newspaper. (她是该报的驻外记者。)
- **spons**or /ˈspɑnsər/ = spons (promise) + or (person) → 赞助/主办/赞助人（=support）：The event was sponsored by a local company. (该活动由一家本地公司赞助。)
- **spons**orship /ˈspɑnsərˌʃɪp/ = spons (promise) + or + ship (n.) → 赞助（=support）：The sports team relies on sponsorship for funding. (这支运动队依靠赞助来获得资金。)
- **spont**aneous /spɑnˈteɪniəs/ = spon (promise) + taneous (adj.) → 自发的（=natural）：The crowd broke into spontaneous applause. (人群自发地爆发出掌声。)

#### 记忆与信念


★**memor=memory 记忆**:

- **memor**y /ˈmɛməri/ = memor (memory) + y (n.) → 记忆（=remembrance）：She has a good memory for names and faces. (她对名字和面孔有很好的记忆力。)
- **remem**ber /rɪˈmɛmbər/ = re (again) + mem (memory) + ber → 记住（=keep in mind）：Please remember to lock the door when you leave. (请记得离开时锁门。)
- **memor**ial /məˈmɔriəl/ = memor (memory) + ial (adj./n.) → 纪念碑（=remembrance）/纪念的：A memorial service was held for the victims. (为遇难者举行了追悼会。)
- **memor**ize /ˈmɛmərˌaɪz/ = memor (memory) + ize (v.) → 记住（=keep in mind）/背诵：The students had to memorize a long poem. (学生们必须背诵一首长诗。)
- **memor**andum /ˌmɛmərˈændəm/ = memor (memory) + andum (n.) → 备忘录（=note）：The manager sent a memorandum to all staff. (经理向全体员工发送了一份备忘录。)
- com**memor**ate /kəˈmɛmərˌeɪt/ = com (together) + memor (memory) + ate (v.) → 纪念（=honor memory）：A statue was built to commemorate the national hero. (建造了一座雕像来纪念这位民族英雄。)


★**cred=believe 相信**:

- **cred**it /ˈkrɛdɪt/ = cred (believe) + it (n.) → 信用/学分（=trust）：You need good credit to apply for a loan. (申请贷款需要良好的信用。)
- **cred**ible /ˈkrɛdəbəl/ = cred (believe) + ible (adj.) → 可信的（=believable）：The witness gave a credible account of the incident. (目击者对事件给出了可信的描述。)
- in**cred**ible /ˌɪnˈkrɛdəbəl/ = in (not) + cred (believe) + ible (adj.) → 难以置信的（=unbelievable）：The view from the top of the mountain was incredible. (从山顶看到的景色令人难以置信。)
- in**cred**ibly /ˌɪnˈkrɛdəbli/ = in (not) + cred (believe) + ibly (adv.) → 难以置信地（=unbelievably）：She is incredibly talented at playing the piano. (她弹钢琴的天赋令人难以置信。)
- dis**cred**it /dɪˈskrɛdət/ = dis (away) + cred (believe) + it → 怀疑（=doubt）/败坏名声：The article was an attempt to discredit the politician. (那篇文章试图败坏那位政治家的名声。)
- **cred**ential /krɪˈdɛnʃəl/ = cred (believe) + ential (n.) → 证书（=proof paper）/凭证：You must present your credentials at the door. (你必须在门口出示你的证件。)


**fid=faith/trust 信任**:

- con**fid**ent /ˈkɑnfədənt/ = con (fully) + fid (trust) + ent (adj.) → 自信的（=self-trusting）：She is confident that she will pass the exam. (她自信能通过考试。)
- con**fid**ence /ˈkɑnfədɛns/ = con (fully) + fid (trust) + ence (n.) → 自信/信心（=self-trust）：Practice will help you build confidence. (练习会帮助你建立信心。)
- con**fid**ential /ˌkɑnfəˈdɛnʃəl/ = con (fully) + fid (trust) + ential (adj.) → 机密的（=secret）：This document is confidential and must not be shared. (这份文件是机密的，不得分享。)
- con**fid**e /kənˈfaɪd/ = con (fully) + fid (trust) + e → 吐露/倾诉（=share secret）：She confided her secret to her best friend. (她向她最好的朋友吐露了秘密。)
- **fid**elity /ˌfaɪˈdɛləti/ = fid (trust) + el + ity (n.) → 忠诚/忠实（=faithfulness）：He promised fidelity to his wife on their wedding day. (他在婚礼当天向妻子承诺忠诚。)
- bona **fid**e /ˈboʊnə faɪd/ = bona (good) + fide (faith) → 真诚的/真实的（=genuine）：He is a bona fide expert in his field. (他是该领域名副其实的专家。)

### 自然与物质词根

> 与自然界、物质、科学相关的词根。

#### 生命与大地


★**bio=life 生命**:

- **bio**logy /baɪˈɑləʤi/ = bio (life) + logy (study of) → 生物学（=study of life）：Biology is the study of living organisms. (生物学是研究生物体的学科。)
- **bio**logical /ˌbaɪəˈlɑʤɪkəl/ = bio (life) + logy + ical (adj.) → 生物学（=study of life）的：The biological diversity of the rainforest is amazing. (雨林的生物多样性令人惊叹。)
- **bio**logist /baɪˈɑləʤɪst/ = bio (life) + logy + ist (person) → 生物学（=study of life）家：The biologist spent years studying marine life. (这位生物学家花了多年时间研究海洋生物。)
- **bio**graphy /baɪˈɑgrəfi/ = bio (life) + graphy (writing) → 传记（=life story）：I am reading a biography of Albert Einstein. (我在读一本阿尔伯特·爱因斯坦的传记。)
- anti**bio**tic /ˌæntibaɪˈɑtɪk/ = anti (against) + bio (life) + tic (n./adj.) → 抗生素（=germ killer）：The doctor prescribed antibiotics for the infection. (医生为感染开了抗生素。)
- sym**bio**sis /ˌsɪmbaɪˈoʊsəs/ = sym (together) + bio (life) + sis (n.) → 共生（=living together）：The clownfish and sea anemone live in symbiosis. (小丑鱼和海葵共生生活。)
- **bio**degradable /ˌbaɪoʊdəˈgreɪdəbəl/ = bio (life) + de (down) + grad (step) + able (adj.) → 可生物降解的（=nature-friendly）：Use biodegradable bags to protect the environment. (使用可生物降解的袋子来保护环境。)


★**viv/vit/vig=live/life 活**:

- **viv**id /ˈvɪvɪd/ = viv (live) + id (adj.) → 生动的（=lifelike）：She gave a vivid description of her trip to Paris. (她生动地描述了她的巴黎之旅。)
- sur**viv**e /sərˈvaɪv/ = sur (over) + viv (live) + e → 幸存（=stay alive）：Only a few people survived the plane crash. (只有少数人在空难中幸存。)
- sur**viv**al /sərˈvaɪvəl/ = sur (over) + viv (live) + al (n.) → 生存（=staying alive）：Food and water are essential for survival. (食物和水对生存至关重要。)
- sur**viv**or /sərˈvaɪvər/ = sur (over) + viv (live) + or (person) → 幸存（=stay alive）者：The survivor was rescued after three days at sea. (幸存者在海上三天后被救起。)
- re**viv**e /rɪˈvaɪv/ = re (again) + viv (live) + e → 复苏/复活（=bring back to life）：The rain helped revive the dying plants. (雨水帮助枯萎的植物复苏了。)
- **vit**al /ˈvaɪtəl/ = vit (life) + al (adj.) → 至关重要的（=life-important）：Good communication is vital to a healthy relationship. (良好的沟通对健康的关系至关重要。)
- **vit**ality /vaɪˈtæləti/ = vit (life) + al + ity (n.) → 活力（=life energy）：Regular exercise can improve your health and vitality. (定期锻炼可以改善你的健康和活力。)
- **vit**amin /ˈvaɪtəmən/ = vit (life) + amin (chemical) → 维生素：Oranges are rich in vitamin C. (橙子富含维生素C。)
- **vig**or /ˈvɪgər/ = vig (live) + or (n.) → 活力（=life energy）/精力：He approached his work with great vigor and enthusiasm. (他以极大的活力和热情投入工作。)
- **vig**orous /ˈvɪgərəs/ = vig (live) + or + ous (adj.) → 充满活力的（=energetic）：The doctor recommends vigorous exercise three times a week. (医生建议每周进行三次剧烈运动。)


★**geo=earth 大地**:

- **geo**graphy /ʤiˈɑgrəfi/ = geo (earth) + graphy (writing) → 地理学（=study of earth）：Geography helps us understand the world around us. (地理学帮助我们了解周围的世界。)
- **geo**logy /ʤiˈɑləʤi/ = geo (earth) + logy (study of) → 地质学（=study of rocks）：Geology is the study of the Earth's structure and history. (地质学是研究地球结构和历史的学科。)
- **geo**metry /ʤiˈɑmətri/ = geo (earth) + metry (measure) → 几何学（=study of shapes）：Geometry is a branch of mathematics dealing with shapes. (几何学是研究形状的数学分支。)
- **geo**metric /ˌʤiəˈmɛtrɪk/ = geo (earth) + metry + ic (adj.) → 几何的（=shape-related）：The garden was designed in geometric patterns. (花园被设计成几何图案。)
- **geo**politics /ˌʤioʊˈpɑlətɪks/ = geo (earth) + politics (政治) → 地缘政治（=land politics）：Geopolitics plays a major role in international relations. (地缘政治在国际关系中扮演重要角色。)
- **geo**thermal /ˌʤioʊˈθərməl/ = geo (earth) + therm (heat) + al (adj.) → 地热的（=earth-heated）：Iceland uses geothermal energy for heating. (冰岛使用地热能供暖。)


**anthrop=human 人**:

- **anthrop**ology /ˌænθrəˈpɑləʤi/ = anthrop (human) + ology (study of) → 人类学（=study of humans）：Anthropology is the study of human societies and cultures. (人类学是研究人类社会和文化的学科。)
- phil**anthrop**ist /fɪˈlænθrəpɪst/ = phil (love) + anthrop (human) + ist (person) → 慈善家（=humanity lover）：The philanthropist donated millions to education. (这位慈善家向教育事业捐赠了数百万。)
- phil**anthrop**y /fɪˈlænθrəpi/ = phil (love) + anthrop (human) + y (n.) → 慈善（=love of humans）：Philanthropy plays an important role in society. (慈善在社会中扮演重要角色。)


**morph=form 形状**:

- **morph**ology /mɔrˈfɑləʤi/ = morph (form) + ology (study of) → 形态学（=study of forms）：Morphology is the study of the form and structure of organisms. (形态学是研究生物体形态和结构的学科。)
- a**morph**ous /əˈmɔrfəs/ = a (without) + morph (form) + ous (adj.) → 无定形的（=shapeless）：The amorphous cloud changed shape constantly. (不定形的云朵不断改变形状。)
- meta**morph**osis /ˌmɛtəˈmɔrfəsəs/ = meta (change) + morph (form) + osis (n.) → 变形/蜕变（=shape change）：A caterpillar undergoes metamorphosis to become a butterfly. (毛毛虫经过蜕变变成蝴蝶。)


**nat=born 出生**:

- **nat**ure /ˈneɪʧər/ = nat (born) + ure (n.) → 自然/本性（=born quality）：It is in her nature to be kind to everyone. (善良待人就是她的本性。)
- **nat**ural /ˈnæʧərəl/ = nat (born) + ur + al (adj.) → 自然的（=innate）：He has a natural talent for music. (他有着天生的音乐天赋。)
- **nat**urally /ˈnæʧərəli/ = nat (born) + ur + al + ly (adv.) → 自然地（=by nature）：She speaks English so naturally that you would think it's her first language. (她英语说得如此自然，你会以为那是她的母语。)
- **nat**ion /ˈneɪʃən/ = nat (born) + ion (n.) → 国家/民族（=country）：China is a nation with a long history. (中国是一个历史悠久的国家。)
- **nat**ional /ˈnæʃənəl/ = nat (born) + ion + al (adj.) → 国家的（=country's）：The national flag represents the country. (国旗代表国家。)
- **nat**ionality /ˌnæʃəˈnælɪti/ = nat (born) + ion + al + ity (n.) → 国籍（=nationality）：What is your nationality? (你的国籍是什么？)
- **nat**ive /ˈneɪtɪv/ = nat (born) + ive (adj./n.) → 本地的/本地人（=original）：He is a native of New York. (他是纽约本地人。)
- in**nat**e /ˌɪˈneɪt/ = in (in) + nat (born) + e → 天生的/固有的（=born with）：She has an innate sense of justice. (她有一种天生的正义感。)
- **naiv**e /naɪiv/ = nat (born) + ive → 天真的（=innocent）：He was naive to trust a complete stranger. (他太天真了，居然信任一个陌生人。)


**hum=ground 土/人**:

- **hum**an /ˈjumən/ = hum (human) + an (adj./n.) → 人类的/人（=people）：To err is human; to forgive, divine. (犯错是人之常情，宽恕是神圣之举。)
- **hum**anity /juˈmænɪti/ = hum (human) + an + ity (n.) → 人类/人性（=humankind）：The disaster brought out the best of humanity. (灾难展现了人性中最美好的一面。)
- **hum**anitarian /ˌjuˌmænəˈtɛriən/ = hum (human) + an + itarian (adj./n.) → 人道主义的（=caring）：The organization provides humanitarian aid to refugees. (该组织向难民提供人道主义援助。)
- **hum**ble /ˈhəmbəl/ = hum (ground) + ble (adj.) → 谦卑的（=modest）：Despite his wealth, he remained humble and kind. (尽管富有，他仍然谦卑善良。)
- **hum**iliate /hjuˈmɪliˌeɪt/ = hum (ground) + iliate (v.) → 羞辱（=shame）：He felt humiliated when his boss criticized him in public. (当老板当众批评他时，他感到受到了羞辱。)
- **hum**iliation /hjuˌmɪliˈeɪʃən/ = hum (ground) + iliate + ion (n.) → 羞辱（=shame）：She could not bear the humiliation of being fired. (她无法忍受被解雇的羞辱。)
- **hum**ility /hjuˈmɪlɪti/ = hum (ground) + ility (n.) → 谦逊（=modesty）：Humility is a virtue admired by many cultures. (谦逊是许多文化都推崇的美德。)
- **hum**orous /ˈhjumərəs/ = hum (human/fluid) + or + ous (adj.) → 幽默的（=funny）：He told a humorous story that made everyone laugh. (他讲了一个幽默的故事，让大家都笑了。)
- **hum**or /ˈhjumər/ = hum (human/fluid) + or (n.) → 幽默（=fun）：A good sense of humor can help you through difficult times. (良好的幽默感可以帮助你度过困难时期。)
- **hum**id /ˈjumɪd/ = hum (ground) + id (adj.) → 潮湿的（=damp）：The weather is hot and humid in summer. (夏天天气又热又潮湿。)
- **hum**idity /hjuˈmɪdəti/ = hum (ground) + id + ity (n.) → 湿度（=dampness）：The humidity today is very high. (今天的湿度非常高。)


**mort=death 死**:

- **mort**al /ˈmɔrtəl/ = mort (death) + al (adj./n.) → 必死的/凡人（=will die）：All human beings are mortal. (人皆有一死。)
- **mort**ality /mɔrˈtæləti/ = mort (death) + al + ity (n.) → 死亡率（=death rate）：Infant mortality has decreased significantly in recent decades. (近几十年来婴儿死亡率已显著下降。)
- im**mort**al /ˌɪˈmɔrtəl/ = im (not) + mort (death) + al (adj.) → 不朽的（=never dying）：Legends say that the gods are immortal. (传说中众神是不朽的。)
- im**mort**ality /ˌɪmɔrˈtælɪti/ = im (not) + mort (death) + al + ity (n.) → 不朽（=never dying）：Many people dream of achieving immortality through their art. (许多人梦想通过自己的艺术获得不朽。)
- **mort**gage /ˈmɔrgɪʤ/ = mort (death) + gage (pledge) → 抵押（死亡抵押）（=loan）：They took out a mortgage to buy their first house. (他们贷款买了第一套房子。)
- post**mort**em /poʊstˈmɔrtɛm/ = post (after) + mort (death) + em → 死后的/事后分析（=after-death）：The team held a postmortem meeting after the project failed. (项目失败后，团队召开了一次事后分析会议。)

#### 水火与光


★**aqua/hydr=water 水**

- **aquarium** /əkˈwɛriəm/ = aqua (水) + -arium (场所) → 水族馆（=water zoo）：We visited the aquarium to see the sharks. (我们去水族馆看鲨鱼。)
- **aquatic** /əkˈwɑtɪk/ = aqua (水) + -tic (形容词后缀) → 水生的（=water-living）：Dolphins are aquatic mammals. (海豚是水生哺乳动物。)
- **hydrate** /ˈhaɪˌdreɪt/ = hydr (水) + -ate (动词后缀) → 补水/水合物（=add water）：You should hydrate regularly during exercise. (运动时你应该定期补水。)
- **dehydrate** /dɪˈhaɪdreɪt/ = de- (去除) + hydr (水) + -ate (动词后缀) → 脱水（=remove water）：The sun will dehydrate the fruit. (太阳会使水果脱水。)
- **hydroelectric** /ˌhaɪdroʊɪˈlɛktrɪk/ = hydro (水) + electric (电的) → 水力发电的（=water-powered）：The dam provides hydroelectric power to the region. (这座水坝为该地区提供水力发电。)
- **hydrogen** /ˈhaɪdrəʤən/ = hydro (水) + -gen (产生) → 氢：Hydrogen is the most abundant element in the universe. (氢是宇宙中最丰富的元素。)
- **hydrant** /ˈhaɪdrənt/ = hydr (水) + -ant (名词后缀) → 消防栓（=water pipe）：The firefighters connected the hose to the hydrant. (消防员把水管接到消防栓上。)
- **aqueduct** /ˈækwəˌdəkt/ = aque/aqua (水) + duct (引导) → 引水渠（=water channel）：The ancient Romans built many aqueducts. (古罗马人建造了许多引水渠。)


★**photo/luc/lumin=light 光**

- **photo**graph /ˈfoʊtəˌgræf/ = photo (光) + graph (写/画) → 照片：She took a photograph of the sunset. (她拍了一张日落的照片。)
- **photo**graphy /fəˈtɑgrəfi/ = photo (光) + graph (写/画) + -y (名词后缀) → 摄影：He studied photography in college. (他在大学学习了摄影。)
- **photo**grapher /fəˈtɑgrəfər/ = photo (光) + graph (写/画) + -er (人) → 摄影师（=photo taker）：The photographer captured the perfect moment. (摄影师捕捉到了完美的瞬间。)
- **photo**n /ˈfoʊˌtɑn/ = photo (光) + -on (粒子) → 光子（=light particle）：A photon is a particle of light. (光子是光的粒子。)
- **photo**synthesis /ˌfoʊtoʊˈsɪnθəsɪs/ = photo (光) + synthesis (合成) → 光合作用（=light-making food）：Plants use photosynthesis to make food. (植物通过光合作用制造食物。)
- **luc**id /ˈlusɪd/ = luc (光/亮) + -id (形容词后缀) → 清晰的（=clear）：He gave a lucid explanation of the theory. (他对这个理论给出了清晰的解释。)
- trans**luc**ent /trænsˈlusənt/ = trans- (穿过) + luc (光) + -ent (形容词后缀) → 半透明的（=semi-clear）：The window is made of translucent glass. (这扇窗户是用半透明玻璃做的。)
- il**lumin**ate /ˌɪˈlumɪnɪt/ = il- (在……上) + lumin (光) + -ate (动词后缀) → 照亮（=light up）：The candles illuminate the room softly. (蜡烛柔和地照亮了房间。)
- il**lumin**ation /ˌɪˌluməˈneɪʃən/ = il- (在……上) + lumin (光) + -ation (名词后缀) → 照明（=lighting）：The illumination of the stadium was impressive. (体育场的照明令人印象深刻。)
- il**lustr**ate /ˈɪləˌstreɪt/ = il- (在……上) + lustr (光) + -ate (动词后缀) → 说明（=explain）：The teacher used a diagram to illustrate the concept. (老师用图表来说明这个概念。)
- il**lustr**ation /ˌɪləˈstreɪʃən/ = il- (在……上) + lustr (光) + -ation (名词后缀) → 说明（=explain）/插图：The book has beautiful illustrations. (这本书有精美的插图。)
- **lumin**ous /ˈlumənəs/ = lumin (光) + -ous (形容词后缀) → 发光的（=glowing）：The stars were luminous in the night sky. (星星在夜空中闪闪发光。)


**ign=fire 火**

- **ign**ite /ˌɪgˈnaɪt/ = ign (火) + -ite (动词后缀) → 点燃（=set on fire）：A spark can ignite the gas. (一个火花就能点燃煤气。)
- **ign**ition /ˌɪgˈnɪʃən/ = ign (火) + -ition (名词后缀) → 点火（=starting fire）：Turn the key to start the ignition. (转动钥匙启动点火装置。)
- **ign**eous /ˈɪgniəs/ = ign (火) + -eous (形容词后缀) → 火成的（=fire-formed）：Granite is an igneous rock. (花岗岩是一种火成岩。)


**therm=heat 热**

- **therm**al /ˈθərməl/ = therm (热) + -al (形容词后缀) → 热的/热量的（=heat-related）：The thermal springs are popular with tourists. (温泉很受游客欢迎。)
- **thermo**meter /θərˈmɑmətər/ = thermo (热) + meter (测量) → 温度计（=heat measurer）：The thermometer showed 38 degrees. (温度计显示38度。)
- **thermo**s /ˈθərməs/ = therm (热) + -os (名词后缀) → 热水瓶（=heat bottle）：She poured coffee from the thermos. (她从热水瓶里倒出咖啡。)
- geo**therm**al /ˌʤioʊˈθərməl/ = geo (地) + therm (热) + -al (形容词后缀) → 地热的（=earth-heated）：Iceland uses geothermal energy for heating. (冰岛利用地热能供暖。)
- **thermo**stat /ˈθərməˌstæt/ = thermo (热) + stat (稳定/调节) → 恒温器（=heat controller）：The thermostat keeps the room at a comfortable temperature. (恒温器让房间保持舒适的温度。)

#### 天空星辰与时间


★**astr/aster=star 星星**

- **astro**naut /ˈæstrəˌnɑt/ = astro (星星) + naut (航行/船) → 宇航员（=star sailor）：The astronaut walked on the moon. (宇航员在月球上行走。)
- **astro**nomy /əˈstrɑnəmi/ = astro (星星) + -nomy (法则/学科) → 天文学（=study of stars）：Astronomy is the study of stars and planets. (天文学是研究恒星和行星的科学。)
- **astro**nomer /əˈstrɑnəmər/ = astro (星星) + nom (法则) + -er (人) → 天文学（=study of stars）家：The astronomer discovered a new planet. (天文学家发现了一颗新行星。)
- **astro**nomical /ˌæstrəˈnɑmɪkəl/ = astro (星星) + nom (法则) + -ical (形容词后缀) → 天文的（=star-related）/巨大的（=huge）：The cost of the project is astronomical. (这个项目的成本是天文数字。)
- dis**aster** /dɪˈzæstər/ = dis- (坏/不正) + aster (星星) → 灾难（星位不正）（=great trouble）：The earthquake was a terrible disaster. (那场地震是一场可怕的灾难。)
- dis**astr**ous /dɪˈzæstrəs/ = dis- (坏) + aster (星星) + -ous (形容词后缀) → 灾难性的（=devastating）：The flood had disastrous consequences. (洪水带来了灾难性的后果。)
- **aster**oid /ˈæstərˌɔɪd/ = aster (星星) + -oid (像……的) → 小行星（=small planet）：An asteroid hit the Earth millions of years ago. (一颗小行星在数百万年前撞击了地球。)
- **aster**isk /ˈæstərɪsk/ = aster (星星) + -isk (小) → 星号（=star mark）：Please mark the important items with an asterisk. (请用星号标记重要项目。)


★**chron=time 时间**

- **chron**ic /ˈkrɑnɪk/ = chron (时间) + -ic (形容词后缀) → 慢性的/长期的（=long-lasting）：He suffers from chronic back pain. (他患有慢性背痛。)
- **chron**icle /ˈkrɑnɪkəl/ = chron (时间) + -icle (名词后缀) → 编年史（=time record）：The book is a chronicle of the war years. (这本书是战争年代的编年史。)
- **chrono**logy /krəˈnɑləʤi/ = chron (时间) + -ology (学科) → 年表/年代学（=time order）：She studied the chronology of ancient Egypt. (她研究了古埃及的年表。)
- **chrono**logical /ˌkrɑnəˈlɑʤɪkəl/ = chron (时间) + -ological (形容词后缀) → 按时间顺序的（=time-ordered）：The events are listed in chronological order. (这些事件是按时间顺序排列的。)
- syn**chron**ize /ˈsɪŋkrəˌnaɪz/ = syn- (共同) + chron (时间) + -ize (动词后缀) → 同步（=same time）：You need to synchronize your phone with the computer. (你需要把手机和电脑同步。)


★**phon/son=sound 声音**

- **telephon**e /ˈtɛləˌfoʊn/ = tele- (远) + phon (声音) + -e → 电话（=far sound）：I'll give you a telephone call tonight. (我今晚给你打电话。)
- sym**phon**y /ˈsɪmfəni/ = sym- (共同) + phon (声音) + -y (名词后缀) → 交响乐（=sounds together）：The orchestra played Beethoven's symphony. (管弦乐队演奏了贝多芬的交响乐。)
- **microphon**e /ˈmaɪkrəˌfoʊn/ = micro- (微小) + phon (声音) + -e → 麦克风（=small sound）：Speak into the microphone so everyone can hear you. (对着麦克风说话，这样每个人都能听到。)
- **phonet**ics /fəˈnɛtɪks/ = phon (声音) + -etics (学科) → 语音学（=study of sounds）：She is studying phonetics at university. (她在大学学习语音学。)
- **phonet**ic /fəˈnɛtɪk/ = phon (声音) + -etic (形容词后缀) → 语音的（=sound-related）：The phonetic alphabet helps with pronunciation. (语音字母表有助于发音。)
- **headphon**e /ˈhɛdˌfoʊn/ = head (头) + phon (声音) + -e → 耳机（=head speaker）：He put on his headphones to listen to music. (他戴上耳机听音乐。)
- **son**ic /ˈsɑnɪk/ = son (声音) + -ic (形容词后缀) → 声音的（=sound-related）：The jet flies at sonic speed. (这架喷气机以音速飞行。)
- **son**ar /ˈsoʊnɑr/ = son (声音) + ar → 声纳：The submarine uses sonar to detect objects. (潜艇使用声纳探测物体。)
- re**son**ant /ˈrɛzənənt/ = re- (回) + son (声音) + -ant (形容词后缀) → 共鸣的（=echoing）：His voice is deep and resonant. (他的声音深沉而洪亮。)
- dis**son**ance /ˈdɪsənəns/ = dis- (不/坏) + son (声音) + -ance (名词后缀) → 不和谐（=clash）：There was a dissonance between his words and actions. (他的言行之间存在不和谐。)


**sol=sun 太阳**

- **sol**ar /ˈsoʊlər/ = sol (太阳) + -ar (形容词后缀) → 太阳的（=sun-related）：Solar panels convert sunlight into electricity. (太阳能电池板将阳光转化为电能。)
- **sol**ar **system** /ˈsoʊlər ˈsɪstəm/ = sol (太阳) + -ar + system (系统) → 太阳系：There are eight planets in our solar system. (我们的太阳系有八颗行星。)
- **sol**stice /ˈsɔlstɪs/ = sol (太阳) + stice (站立/停止) → 至日（=sun-stop）：The summer solstice is the longest day of the year. (夏至是一年中白天最长的一天。)
- para**sol** /parasol*/ = para- (防/旁) + sol (太阳) → 遮阳伞（=sun shield）：She carried a parasol to protect herself from the sun. (她带着遮阳伞防晒。)
- **sol**arium /solarium*/ = sol (太阳) + -arium (场所) → 日光浴室（=sun room）：The hotel has a solarium on the roof. (酒店屋顶有一个日光浴室。)


**lun=moon 月亮**

- **lun**ar /ˈlunər/ = lun (月亮) + -ar (形容词后缀) → 月球的（=moon-related）：The lunar surface is covered with craters. (月球表面布满了陨石坑。)
- **lun**ar **calendar** /ˈlunər ˈkæləndər/ = lun (月亮) + -ar + calendar (日历) → 农历：The Mid-Autumn Festival is based on the lunar calendar. (中秋节是基于农历的。)
- semi**lun**ar /semilunar*/ = semi- (半) + lun (月亮) + -ar (形容词后缀) → 半月形的（=half-moon）：The semilunar valve is part of the heart. (半月瓣是心脏的一部分。)


**aer/air=air 空气**

- **air** /ɛr/ = air (空气) → 空气：Fresh air is good for your health. (新鲜空气有益健康。)
- **air**port /ˈɛrˌpɔrt/ = air (空气/航空) + port (港口) → 机场：We arrived at the airport two hours early. (我们提前两小时到达了机场。)
- **air**line /ˈɛˌrlaɪn/ = air (空气/航空) + line (线路) → 航线/航空公司：Which airline did you fly with? (你乘坐的是哪家航空公司？)
- **air**craft /ˈɛrˌkræft/ = air (空气/航空) + craft (飞行器) → 飞机（=airplane）：The aircraft took off smoothly. (飞机平稳起飞。)
- **aer**ial /ˈɛriəl/ = aer (空气) + -ial (形容词后缀) → 空中的（=in air）：The aerial view of the city was breathtaking. (城市的空中景观令人叹为观止。)
- **aer**ospace /ˈɛroʊˌspeɪs/ = aero (空气/航空) + space (空间) → 航空航天（=air and space）：She works in the aerospace industry. (她在航空航天行业工作。)
- **aer**oplane /aeroplane*/ = aero (空气) + plane (平面/机翼) → 飞机（=airplane）：The aeroplane landed safely at the airport. (飞机安全降落在机场。)
- **aer**obic /ɛˈroʊbɪk/ = aero (空气) + -bic (生物的) → 有氧的（=with oxygen）：Running is an excellent aerobic exercise. (跑步是一项极好的有氧运动。)
- **aer**odynamics /ˌɛroʊdaɪˈnæmɪks/ = aero (空气) + dynamics (力学) → 空气动力学（=study of air movement）：The car was designed with aerodynamics in mind. (这辆车在设计时考虑了空气动力学。)


**noct/nyct=night 夜**: nocturnal 夜间活动的，nocturne 夜曲，equinox 昼夜平分点


**umbri=shadow 影**

- **umbrella** /ˈəmˌbrɛlə/ = umbr (影) + -ella (小) → 雨伞（小阴影）（=umbrella）：Take an umbrella; it might rain later. (带上雨伞，晚些时候可能会下雨。)
- **umbrage** /ˈəmbrɪʤ/ = umbr (影) + -age (名词后缀) → 阴影/不快（=offense）：He took umbrage at her remarks. (他对她的话感到不快。)

#### 形状环与海洋


★**circ/cyc=ring 环**

- **circ**le /ˈsərkəl/ = circ (环) + -le (小) → 圆/圈子：The children sat in a circle. (孩子们围坐成一圈。)
- **circ**ular /ˈsərkjələr/ = circ (环) + -ular (形容词后缀) → 圆形的/循环的：The building has a circular shape. (这座建筑是圆形的。)
- **circ**ulate /ˈsərkjəˌleɪt/ = circ (环) + -ulate (动词后缀) → 循环/流通（=move around）：Blood circulates through the body. (血液在身体中循环。)
- **circ**ulation /ˈsərkjəˌleɪʃən/ = circ (环) + -ulation (名词后缀) → 循环（=moving around）：Exercise improves blood circulation. (运动促进血液循环。)
- **circ**us /ˈsərkəs/ = circ (环) + -us (名词后缀) → 马戏团（=circus）：We took the children to the circus. (我们带孩子们去看了马戏团。)
- **circ**uit /ˈsərkət/ = circ (环) + -uit (走) → 电路/巡回（=loop）：The race car completed one circuit of the track. (赛车在赛道上跑完了一圈。)
- **cyc**le /ˈsaɪkəl/ = cyc (环/轮) + -le → 循环（=moving around）/自行车：He rides his cycle to work every day. (他每天骑自行车上班。)
- **cyc**l**ist** /ˈsaɪkəlɪst/ = cyc (轮) + -ist (人) → 骑行者（=bike rider）：The cyclist won the race. (那位骑行者赢得了比赛。)
- **recyc**le /riˈsaɪkəl/ = re- (再/重新) + cyc (环) + -le → 回收（=use again）：We should recycle plastic bottles. (我们应该回收塑料瓶。)
- **bicyc**le /ˈbaɪsɪkəl/ = bi- (两) + cyc (轮) + -le → 自行车：She learned to ride a bicycle when she was five. (她五岁时学会了骑自行车。)
- en**cyc**lopedia /ɪnˌsaɪkləˈpidiə/ = en- (在……里) + cyclo (环/全面) + pedia (教育) → 百科全书（=all-knowledge book）：I looked up the information in an encyclopedia. (我在百科全书中查了这些信息。)


**rot=wheel 轮/转**

- **rot**ate /ˈroʊˌteɪt/ = rot (轮/转) + -ate (动词后缀) → 旋转（=spinning）：The Earth rotates on its axis. (地球绕其轴旋转。)
- **rot**ation /roʊˈteɪʃən/ = rot (转) + -ation (名词后缀) → 旋转（=spinning）：The rotation of the Earth causes day and night. (地球的自转产生了昼夜。)
- **rot**ary /ˈroʊtəri/ = rot (轮) + -ary (形容词后缀) → 旋转（=spinning）的：The rotary engine was invented in the 20th century. (转子发动机发明于20世纪。)
- **rot**or /ˈroʊtər/ = rot (轮/转) + -or (名词后缀) → 转子（=spinner）：The rotor of the helicopter spins very fast. (直升机的旋翼旋转得非常快。)


**mar/mer=sea 海**

- **mar**ine /mərˈin/ = mar (海) + -ine (形容词后缀) → 海洋的（=sea-related）：Marine life is incredibly diverse. (海洋生物极为多样。)
- **mar**iner /ˈmɛrənər/ = mar (海) + -iner (人) → 水手（=sailor）：The ancient mariners navigated by the stars. (古代水手依靠星星导航。)
- **submar**ine /ˌsəbmərˈin/ = sub- (在……下) + mar (海) + -ine → 潜艇（=under-sea boat）：The submarine dived deep into the ocean. (潜艇潜入深海。)
- **mar**itime /ˈmærəˌtaɪm/ = mar (海) + -itime (形容词后缀) → 海事的（=sea-related）：Maritime trade is vital to the economy. (海上贸易对经济至关重要。)
- **mer**maid /ˈmərˌmeɪd/ = mer (海) + maid (少女) → 美人鱼（=sea maiden）：The little mermaid dreamed of life on land. (小美人鱼梦想着陆地上的生活。)
- **mar**sh /mɑrʃ/ = mar (海/水) + -sh → 沼泽（=wetland）：The marsh is home to many birds. (沼泽是许多鸟类的家园。)


**nav/naut=ship 船**

- **nav**y /ˈneɪvi/ = nav (船) + -y (名词后缀) → 海军（=sea force）：He joined the navy at the age of eighteen. (他十八岁时加入了海军。)
- **nav**al /ˈneɪvəl/ = nav (船) + -al (形容词后缀) → 海军（=sea force）的：The naval base is located on the coast. (海军基地位于海岸上。)
- **nav**igate /ˈnævəˌgeɪt/ = nav (船) + ig (驱动) + -ate (动词后缀) → 航行/导航（=find way）：Sailors navigate using maps and compasses. (水手使用地图和指南针导航。)
- **nav**igation /ˌnævəˈgeɪʃən/ = nav (船) + ig (驱动) + -ation (名词后缀) → 导航（=way-finding）：GPS has made navigation much easier. (GPS使导航变得容易多了。)
- **naut**ical /ˈnɔtəkəl/ = naut (船) + -ical (形容词后缀) → 航海的（=sailing）：The museum has a collection of nautical instruments. (博物馆收藏了一些航海仪器。)
- astro**naut** /ˈæstrəˌnɑt/ = astro (星星) + naut (船/航行) → 宇航员（=star sailor）：The astronaut floated in zero gravity. (宇航员在失重状态下漂浮。)


**dent=tooth 牙齿**

- **dent**ist /ˈdɛntɪst/ = dent (牙齿) + -ist (人) → 牙医（=tooth doctor）：I have an appointment with the dentist tomorrow. (我明天预约了牙医。)
- **dent**al /ˈdɛntəl/ = dent (牙齿) + -al (形容词后缀) → 牙齿的（=tooth-related）：Regular dental checkups are important. (定期牙科检查很重要。)
- **dent**ure /ˈdɛnʧər/ = dent (牙齿) + -ure (名词后缀) → 假牙（=false teeth）：My grandfather wears dentures. (我爷爷戴着假牙。)
- in**dent** /ˌɪnˈdɛnt/ = in- (入) + dent (牙齿/齿痕) → 缩进（=push in）：You should indent the first line of each paragraph. (你应该缩进每个段落的第一行。)


**cav=hollow 空**

- **cav**e /keɪv/ = cav (空/洞) + -e → 洞穴（=hole）：They explored a deep cave in the mountain. (他们探索了山中的一个深洞穴。)
- **cav**ity /ˈkævəti/ = cav (空/洞) + -ity (名词后缀) → 空洞/蛀牙（=hole）：The dentist filled the cavity in my tooth. (牙医补了我牙齿上的蛀洞。)
- ex**cav**ate /ˈɛkskəˌveɪt/ = ex- (出) + cav (空/洞) + -ate (动词后缀) → 挖掘（=dig out）：Archaeologists excavate ancient ruins. (考古学家挖掘古代遗址。)
- **cav**ern /ˈkævərn/ = cav (空/洞) + -ern (名词后缀) → 大洞穴（=big cave）：The cavern was filled with stalactites. (这个大洞穴里满是钟乳石。)
- **concav**e /ˈkɑnkeɪv/ = con- (共同) + cav (空/凹) + -e → 凹面的（=curved in）：The mirror has a concave surface. (这面镜子有一个凹面。)


**und=wave 波浪/流动**

- ab**und**ant /əˈbəndənt/ = ab- (从) + und (波浪/涌流) + -ant (形容词后缀) → 丰富的（=plentiful）：The region is abundant in natural resources. (该地区自然资源丰富。)
- ab**und**ance /əˈbəndəns/ = ab- (从) + und (波浪/涌流) + -ance (名词后缀) → 丰富（=plenty）：There is an abundance of fresh fruit in summer. (夏天有丰富的新鲜水果。)
- **re**d**undant** /rɪˈdəndənt/ = re(d)- (再/回) + und (波浪/涌流) + -ant (形容词后缀) → 多余的（=extra）：The report contains a lot of redundant information. (这份报告包含大量多余的信息。)
- in**und**ate /ˈɪnənˌdeɪt/ = in- (入) + und (波浪) + -ate (动词后缀) → 淹没（=flood）：The heavy rain inundated the streets. (大雨淹没了街道。)
- **und**ulate /ˈənʤəˌleɪt/ = und (波浪) + -ulate (动词后缀) → 波动（=go up and down）：The grass undulated in the wind. (草在风中起伏波动。)

### 社会与人

> 与人类社会、政治、经济、人际关系相关的词根。

#### 社会政治与法律


★**popul/publ=people 人民**: 

- **popul**ar /ˈpɑpjələr/ = popul (人民) + ar (形容词后缀，…的) → 流行的，受欢迎的：This song is very popular among teenagers. (这首歌在青少年中非常流行。)
- **popul**arity /ˌpɑpjəˈlɛrəti/ = popul (人民) + arity (名词后缀) → 流行，受欢迎：The popularity of online shopping continues to grow. (网上购物的受欢迎程度持续增长。)
- **popul**ation /ˌpɑpjəˈleɪʃən/ = popul (人民) + ation (名词后缀) → 人口：The world population has exceeded eight billion. (世界人口已超过八十亿。)
- **publ**ic /ˈpəblɪk/ = publ (人民) + ic (形容词后缀，…的) → 公众的，公共的：The park is open to the public from dawn to dusk. (公园从早到晚对公众开放。)
- **publ**ish /ˈpəblɪʃ/ = publ (人民) + ish (动词后缀，做) → 公开给人民 → 出版，发布：The author plans to publish her new novel next month. (作者计划下个月出版她的新小说。)
- **publ**ication /ˌpəblɪˈkeɪʃən/ = publ (人民) + ication (名词后缀) → 出版，出版物：The magazine ceased publication after fifty years. (这本杂志在五十年后停刊了。)
- **publ**isher /ˈpəblɪʃər/ = publ (人民) + ish (动词后缀) + er (人) → 出版商，发行人：The manuscript was rejected by several publishers. (手稿被几家出版商拒绝了。)
- re**publ**ic /riˈpəblɪk/ = re (事物) + publ (人民) + ic (名词后缀) → 共和国（=people's state）：France is a republic with a long democratic tradition. (法国是一个有着悠久民主传统的共和国。)


★**leg=law 法律**: 

- **leg**al /ˈligəl/ = leg (法律) + al (形容词后缀，…的) → 合法的，法律的：You should seek legal advice before signing the contract. (在签署合同之前你应该寻求法律建议。)
- il**leg**al /ˌɪˈligəl/ = il (不) + leg (法律) + al (形容词后缀，…的) → 非法的，违法的：Smuggling goods across the border is illegal. (偷运货物过境是非法的。)
- **leg**ality /liˈgæləti/ = leg (法律) + ality (名词后缀) → 合法性，正当性：The court questioned the legality of the search. (法庭质疑搜查的合法性。)
- **leg**islation /ˌlɛʤəsˈleɪʃən/ = leg (法律) + isl (连接成分) + ation (名词后缀) → 立法（=law-making）：The government introduced new legislation on data protection. (政府出台了关于数据保护的新立法。)
- **leg**itimate /ləˈʤɪtəmət/ = leg (法律) + itim (连接成分) + ate (形容词后缀) → 合法的，正当的：He had a legitimate reason for being absent. (他有正当理由缺席。)
- privi**leg**e /ˈprɪvɪlɪʤ/ = privi (私人的) + lege (法律) → 法律赋予个人的 → 特权（=special right）：It is a privilege to be invited to this ceremony. (受邀参加这个仪式是一种特权。)


★**jur/jus=law/right 法律/权利**: 

- **jur**y /ˈʤʊri/ = jur (法律) + y (名词后缀，表集体) → 陪审团（=decision group）：The jury found the defendant not guilty. (陪审团裁定被告无罪。)
- **jur**or /ˈʤʊrər/ = jur (法律) + or (名词后缀，人) → 陪审员（=jury member）：Each juror must listen carefully to the evidence. (每位陪审员都必须认真听取证据。)
- **jus**t /ʤɪst/ = jus (法律/正义) + t → 公正的，正义的：The judge made a just decision in the case. (法官对此案做出了公正的裁决。)
- **jus**tice /ˈʤəstɪs/ = jus (法律/正义) + tice (名词后缀) → 公正，司法：The justice system must protect the rights of all citizens. (司法体系必须保护所有公民的权利。)
- **jus**tify /ˈʤəstəˌfaɪ/ = jus (法律/正义) + tify (动词后缀，使……) → 证明（=confirm）正当，为……辩护：How can you justify spending so much money on this project? (你怎么证明在这个项目上花那么多钱是合理的？)
- in**jus**tice /ˌɪnˈʤəstɪs/ = in (不) + jus (法律/正义) + tice (名词后缀) → 不公正，非正义：He fought against social injustice his entire life. (他一生都在与社会不公作斗争。)
- ad**jus**t /əˈʤəst/ = ad (向) + jus (法律/正确) + t → 向正确方向调整 → 调整，适应：It takes time to adjust to a new environment. (适应新环境需要时间。)
- ad**jus**tment /əˈʤəstmənt/ = ad (向) + jus (法律/正确) + t + ment (名词后缀) → 调整，调节：The mechanic made a few adjustments to the engine. (机械师对发动机做了一些调整。)


★**civ=citizen 公民**:
